# Skyrim:Bodyguard (Pelagius)

## Overview

| Bodyguard | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [The Mind of a Madman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:The Mind of a Madman") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0009F85E |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 550 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Pelagius Arena Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Arena_Faction "Skyrim:Pelagius Arena Faction") | | |

Bodyguard

The **Bodyguards** are two [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [citizens](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who sit on either side of [Pelagius the Suspicious](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Suspicious "Skyrim:Pelagius the Suspicious") during the quest [The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness"), observing the arena fight between two [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They wear [Dwarven armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armor "Skyrim:Dwarven Armor") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Boots "Skyrim:Dwarven Boots"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dwarven Gauntlets") and a [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Helmet "Skyrim:Dwarven Helmet"). When you hit one of them with the [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack"), they will both turn into [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") and kill Pelagius.

## Related Quests

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

# Skyrim:Boethiah Cultist

## Overview

| Boethiah Cultist | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") | Gender | Female |
| Level | Radiant (1-25) | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0004D8D1 |
| Other Information | | | |
| Voice Type | [FemaleDarkElf](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleDarkElf "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleDarkElf") | | |
| Respawns | Yes | | |

A female Dunmer Boethiah Cultist, located at the Sacellum of Boethiah

The **Boethiah Cultists** are worshippers of the Daedric Prince [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah") and are located at the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah"). They play a part in the quest [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling"), but they can also be found as a [random encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Boethiah_Cultist_attack "Skyrim:World Interactions"), carrying *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* in their inventory and initiating the quest. They can be easily recognized by a unique sign tattooed in black on the right side of their faces.

## Related Quests

## Dialogue

- *"Though we live in shadow, we carve indelible signs of our passing into the world."*
- *"A well placed word or a well placed dagger. Both can achieve equal purposes."*

## Bugs

- The Boethiah Cultist who attacks you in a [random encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") (WEDA02Cultist) doesn't become hostile until he's been very close to you for some time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, addresses this issue. An alias property needed to be adjusted to make sure he immediately attacks on sight.
- Looting the book from the dead Boethiah Cultist may fail to close the objective to investigate the cultists once the book is read.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.
- After A Matter of Pride is finished, some Boethiah Cultists may respawn in the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") when the area resets. From there, they can follow you wherever you go, and they can appear anywhere, including inside player homes.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.629, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Daedric.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Daedric.png) | **Become [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah")'s new champion.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Book: *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* or Automatic after visiting [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah") |
| Location(s): | [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah"), [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge") |
| Reward: | [Ebony Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Mail "Skyrim:Ebony Mail") |
| ID: | DA02 |
| Required Level: | 30 |
| Suggested Level: | 18 |
| Difficulty: | Hard |

[Adelaisa Vendicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adelaisa_Vendicci "Skyrim:Adelaisa Vendicci") being sacrificed to Boethiah

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Read *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")*.
2. Travel to the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah") and speak to the [Priestess of Boethiah](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Priestess_of_Boethiah&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Priestess of Boethiah (page does not exist)").
3. Sacrifice a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") on the Altar of Sacrifice.
4. Kill all the cult members.
5. Go to [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge") and kill Boethiah's [current champion](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Champion of Boethiah").

### Starting the Quest

You can start the quest any time after reaching level 30, either by reading a copy of *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* or traveling directly to the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah") and talking to the Priestess of Boethiah or killing every one of the cultists. If you wait, you may be attacked randomly in the world by Boethiah cultists, who will have a copy of *Boethiah's Proving* on their corpse.

:   *Note:* See *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* for other locations of the book. The various copies of the book appear once you reach level 30.

### The Shrine of Boethiah

First, you will have to make your way to the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah"). Follow the road northeast from the [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") up to [Traitor's Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Traitor%27s_Post "Skyrim:Traitor's Post"). Nearby is a road that leads into the mountains, up to the Sacellum. When you arrive at the Sacellum you will find two cultists fighting in a small arena. There are some more cultists and a Priestess of Boethiah watching them. Speak to the priestess. She will tell you that you need to prove that "your tongue can wield a lie". If you kill the followers of Boethiah, the Daedric Prince will appear and give the quest instructions herself; this will only change the order in which you complete the tasks. If you approach the shrine at level 29 or below, the quest won't start, and there will be no one there.

### The Sacrifice

The priestess will tell you that you need to gain someone's trust and then sacrifice them before Boethiah. She will give you the [Blade of Sacrifice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Sacrifice "Skyrim:Blade of Sacrifice") to use for the deed. Lead any *non-[essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs")* [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") to the shrine and activate command mode (holding 'use' or via the "I need you to do something" conversation option). Highlight the pillar and you should see "Use the Pillar of Sacrifice". Tell them to do this and they will move towards it and be pulled in and stuck to it. If the follower is essential, the pillar will not be triggered.

Kill the follower using any means (despite what the Priestess says, you do not have to use the Blade of Sacrifice). Once your follower is dead, Boethiah will use the body as a conduit to tell you and all of the cultists that she has a task for whomever is left standing after a battle to the death. This results in all the cultists attacking one another (and you). Be prepared for a tough fight, as they can be formidable opponents.

Alternatively, you can leave your follower on the Pillar of Sacrifice, kill all of the cultists until one is left, lead the last cultist to the Pillar of Sacrifice, get the last cultist's health to low, then kill your follower and the last cultist simultaneously. If done correctly, your follower will survive, their services should be available once again, and Boethiah will take the form of the last cultist instead.

If you have already killed all the followers of Boethiah, she will then possess the corpse of the last follower you slew and the quest proceeds as normal. See [Notes](#Notes).

### The New Champion

The Ebony Mail

After making the sacrifice and killing all the cultists, Boethiah will again use a body as a conduit (it may not be the same one) and tell you she needs a new champion. To become the new champion you must kill the old champion and his bandits at [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge"), northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

Despite Boethiah's order to kill them stealthily, being detected does not result in quest failure or any other penalty. Nonetheless, most of the bandits inside the mine are busy with their backs to you and can be assassinated. A few are standing in pools of flammable liquid that can be ignited with fire spells. It's difficult to sneak up on Boethiah's Champion because of the direction he faces when sitting, but if you climb on top of his shack, you can drop down behind him. Once you defeat Boethiah's Champion, you must equip his [Ebony Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Mail "Skyrim:Ebony Mail"). Boethiah will then speak to you one last time, telling you that you are her new champion and giving you the Ebony Mail as your reward.

## Notes

- [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah") would have either given you a second [Daedric Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Quests "Skyrim:Daedric Quests"), or a second part to this one, in which you would have killed [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")'s Jarl [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"). The quest is (mostly, see [Bugs](#Bugs)) inaccessible in the final game, but data for it can still be found [in the game files](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Bidding "Skyrim:Boethiah's Bidding").
- One or more of the bandits in Knifepoint Ridge might start a fight with the old Champion if they get close enough to him to be hurt by the poison damage done by the Ebony Mail when they are searching for you.
- If your follower survives using the alternate method, they will revert to their original equipment, and anything you gave them may be lost. To avoid this, remove everything from their inventory except for their original weapons and armor.
- While killing your follower as a sacrifice does not result in any bounties, faction-specific reactions, such as [Rejoining the College](/wiki/Skyrim:Rejoining_the_College "Skyrim:Rejoining the College") if you kill any of the apprentice followers, may still get triggered.
- If [Champion of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Champion of Boethiah") is calmed down, unique dialogue with him will become available.

## Bugs

|  |
| --- |
| **To meet our site's higher standard of quality, this article or section may require cleanup.**  **The user who placed this here had the following concern:** overlong bugs section needs testing To leave a message about the cleanup for this article, please add it to this article's [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Boethiah%27s_Calling). |

- Clearing out Knifepoint Ridge before this quest has begun may prevent the latter from starting at all.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Should you attack [Jarl Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") under any circumstances during this quest, she will flee combat and all of the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace")'s guards will turn permanently hostile to you. This is caused by leftover code tied to removed content. (see [Notes](#Notes))
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- If you refuse the quest and kill the cultists or something happens to cause Boethiah's current body to enter combat mode (such as a dragon attack), she will be stuck in the same conversational loop repeating the line *"You've gotten my attention mortal, that is most unwise"* when approached. **?**
  - To get around this, kill all the cultists and priests.
- Completing this quest can trap you inside Knifepoint Ridge.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, addresses this issue. There were invalid conditions on the event that was supposed to reset the dungeon after leaving.
- The quest can become stuck if the player kills the Priestess before talking to Boethiah.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.
- If you sacrifice a [Companion leader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle") at the Pillar, the game may not register them as killed, breaking the radiant quests from the Companions. Though the follower dies and the quest for Boethiah proceeds as normal, the other Companion leaders don't acknowledge the death, and they still respond with "*Aren't you already running a job for (name)?*" when asked about work. **?**
- If you kill the priestess before talking to Boethiah, one or two of the current fighters may become unkillable.
  -  Open the console and for each fighter that's unkillable, click on them and then type `kill`. The quest will proceed as normal once all the fighters are dead. If that does not work, open the console and type `damageactorvalue health 500`.
- On entering Knifepoint Ridge, possibly due to having been there before beginning the quest, you may be presented with a wall of iron ore veins blocking your path to the remaining bandits and the Boethiah Cultist, making the quest impossible to complete.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - A known workaround is to look at the bottom right corner of the iron vein wall, where the option to mine a corundum vein will be presented. Mining this vein will pull you through the wall, allowing you to continue with the quest as intended. This will only work for as many times as you can continue to trigger the mining animation, so you should either cancel the animation before the vein is completely emptied or make sure you have completed everything before heading back up this path — as soon as you have walked through the location of the wall the iron vein will reappear, making the rest of the mine unreachable.
- The Miscellaneous Quest objective "Investigate the Boethiah cultist" may not ever be marked as completed, even after completing the main Boethiah's Calling mission.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.10, fixes this bug.
  - Looting the book from the body **before** reading it will prevent this.
- The [Champion of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Champion of Boethiah") will re-equip his armor if he is killed and revived with [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall"), which can be exploited for infinite gold and powerful armor for your followers.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
- Upon talking with Boethiah your vision field may be stuck in the distorted oval it creates when talking to the daedric prince.
  - Completing the quest might fix this.
  -  Opening the console and typing `rimod 00106a73` or `rimodcf` might also fix it.
- Your follower's inventory will be reset upon being used by Boethiah, and any items you gave them will be removed.
- The Champion of Boethiah may disappear after being killed. His body passes through the ground beyond the wall, making it impossible reach it and retrieve the Ebony Mail.
  -  By using the console commands `prid 000834FF` followed by `resurrect` the champion will be resurrected but still be stuck in the ground. He will eventually free himself and can then be killed again (e.g. with the console command `kill`).
- When Boethiah's conduit is killed after she's done "using it", you may incur a bounty.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you use beast form and eat the Champion of Boethiah the game may glitch making it impossible to collect the Ebony Mail. **?**
- During the step of Retrieving and Equipping the Ebony Mail, if you equip it right away from the body of the Champion, or have it sent to secondary storage after looting and then get the armor from there, the quest will not proceed.
  - If you are using mods with secondary storage disable them temporarily. Once you have, drop the Ebony Mail on the floor, then pick it up again and equip it. Afterwards the quest will proceed.
- After sacrificing your follower, upon being asked to slay the other cultists, one of the markers may appear inside the ground or the mountain. A cultist may have spawned underground and the quest cannot be completed past this point.
  - One possible fix is reloading to a save prior to the fight and affixing your follower to the Altar of Sacrifice. The cultists will all gather around the altar waiting for you to strike the killing blow. Engaging the cultists before killing your follower in this manner is a possible fix.
  -  Another possible fix is to use the `resurrect` console command on one of the cultists and kill them again. This should trigger the next step of the quest and Boethiah should talk to you through the cultist's corpse and continue the quest as normal.

## Quest Stages

| DA02 Hook (WEDA02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 10:* Investigate the Boethiah cultist |
| Boethiah's Calling (DA02) | | |
| 1 |  | I found a book that mentioned a cult of Boethiah in the mountains near Windhelm. *Objective 1:* Find the shrine of Boethiah |
| 5 |  | I have discovered a shrine to Boethiah in the mountains near Windhelm. *Objective 5:* Find the cult of Boethiah |
| 10 |  | I am to lead someone to the Shrine of Boethiah, instruct them to touch the Pillar of Sacrifice, and once trapped by it's *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* magic, slay them. If I do this Boethiah will appear. *Objective 10:* Lead someone to become trapped by the shrine and slay them |
| 15 |  | Boethiah has appeared using <Alias=DeadFriend>'s corpse as a vessel. She will give a special task to whichever of her cultists are left alive after we fight to the death. *Objective 15:* Slay the other cultists |
| 17 |  | *Objective 101:* Speak to Boethiah's Conduit |
| 20 |  | Boethiah revealed herself to me. I am to slay her previous champion, and having done so, don the Ebony Mail. So doing, she will make me her champion. *Objective 20:* Slay everyone at Knifepoint Ridge stealthily |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Retrieve and equip the Ebony Mail |
| 31 |  | *Objective 30:* Retrieve and equip the Ebony Mail |
| 40 |  | I have proven myself to Boethiah, and she has made me her new champion. |
| 50 | ☑ |  |
| 100 | ☑ |  |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 50:* Slay the Jarl of Solitude  *Objective 100:* Speak to Boethiah's Conduit |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - WEDA02: 0, 1, 255.
  - DA02: 0, 4, 6, 7, 9, 11, 12, 21, 41, 60, 70, 80, 81, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA02`.

Bolar

**Bolar** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") and wise woman of [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur"), the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch").

She offers apothecary services from 8am to 8pm, not far from the [longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Mauhulakh%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Mauhulakh's Longhouse") of the stronghold. After 8pm she heads back inside to eat until midnight.

As the wise woman of the Narzulbur tribe, Bolar is counted upon by the [chieftain](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Mauhulakh "Skyrim:Chief Mauhulakh") to communicate with the gods to figure out why all his wives have died. She's not in any rush though, because as far as she's concerned, as long as he has [Yatul](/wiki/Skyrim:Yatul "Skyrim:Yatul") and herself, he doesn't need anyone else and she thinks he's showing signs of weakness by being sentimental over their deaths. She raised his children, [Urog](/wiki/Skyrim:Urog "Skyrim:Urog") and [Dushnamub](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnamub "Skyrim:Dushnamub"), after each of their mothers died during childbirth while she was the midwife.

## Dialogue

When approached she can say:

:   *"I've read the entrails many times, but can't fathom why Mauhulakh's wives keep finding tragedy."*
:   *"Mauhulakh was such a darling boy. Until he got older, and started having opinions."*
:   *"Urog and Dushnamub were such lovely children. I held them as they watched their mothers die after birth. They know me best, now."*
:   *"Yatul and I tend to dote on Mauhulakh. You know how aunts can be with their favorite nephew."*

## Conversations

She can often be seen conversing with either her sister Yatul, or her nephew Mauhulakh:

:   **Yatul**: *"I hear Mauhulakh is wandering again. He's after a new woman."*
:   **Bolar**: *"He's lonely. What do you expect?"*
:   **Yatul**: *"No matter. You'll take care of things like you always have."*
:   **Bolar**: *"Please, let's not have it come to that."*
:   **Yatul**: *"True... we could simply make sure she never reaches Narzulbur."*
:   **Bolar**: *"That wasn't what I meant."*

:   **Yatul**: *"If he does show up with a bride, we'll have to move quickly."*
:   **Bolar**: *"Once she's with child, I will not harm her."*
:   **Yatul**: *"Yes, you've made that quite clear in the past. And now we have Urog and Dushnamub because of your weakness."*
:   **Bolar**: *"They are good, loyal children."*
:   **Yatul**: *"They squander their father's love. We can't dally this time."*

:   **Yatul**: *"Have you scried anything new in the entrails?"*
:   **Bolar**: *"Very little. It's an uncertain time."*
:   **Yatul**: *"Not for us, it isn't."*
:   **Bolar**: *"For all of us."*
:   **Yatul**: *"Come back to me when you have something useful."*

:   **Bolar**: *"He's been spending a lot of time at the graves again."*
:   **Yatul**: *"Good. The more time he pines for the dead wives, the less time he spends finding a new one."*
:   **Bolar**: *"Be careful. The spirits can speak to the living if there's a strong connection."*
:   **Yatul**: *"Bah. He never had a connection with any of them beyond what his loins told him."*
:   **Bolar**: *"Maybe, but..."*
:   **Yatul**: *"We're the ones he loves. Me, and you."*

:   **Mauhulakh**: *"Bolar, I must ask you something."*
:   **Bolar**: *"Yes, child?"*
:   **Mauhulakh**: *"Have the spirits told you where I may find a wife? One who will be safe from this curse?"*
:   **Bolar**: *"Oh, all things in time, my boy. All things in time. What more do you need that Yatul and I cannot provide?"*
:   **Mauhulakh**: *"I need more children."*
:   **Bolar**: *"Well, that's a different matter..."*

:   **Mauhulakh**: *"Are the gods angry with me?"*
:   **Bolar**: *"Why do you ask me that?"*
:   **Mauhulakh**: *"Why else have they cursed me? Killed all my wives?"*
:   **Bolar**: *"Perhaps it's actually a sign of their love for you. They don't want to see you with unworthy mates."*
:   **Mauhulakh**: *"Then they should send one they consider worthy."*
:   **Bolar**: *"Patience, boy."*

## Spells

Bolar knows the following spells:

- [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")
  - [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt")
- [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")
  - [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing")
  - [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward")

## Notes

- Bolar has an additional dialogue line which she was supposed to say after having completed [unfinished quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests") `NarzulburFreeFormWifeQuest`, which involved getting an [unused NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:Uglarz "Skyrim:Uglarz") to marry Mauhulakh. She could have been heard greeting you with: *"All my auguring never predicted this. A woman for Mauhulakh, eh? We'll see how this goes."*
- In the game's DialogueViews files, there is dialogue for a favor quest known internally as `Favor016Quest`. In the finished game's files seen through the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), only a single basic script remains of this quest. But the DialogueViews show all the dialogue that was attached to it:

:   **Anything I can do to help?**
:   *"I am the wise woman. I guide our tribe and make sure we stay strong. I also make poisons for our hunters' arrows, and potions to keep our fighting spirits high. How about I give you something for your blade, to welcome you to our people? I just need a Skeever Tail and a Falmer Ear.*

:   **I have the Skeever Tail and a Falmer Ear.**
:   *"Good. Let me mix those for you. Here. A poison that will squeeze the life out of your enemies. And some coin, for your trouble. Mauloch smile on you, outlander.*

- This dialogue doesn't specify a speaker, so it's unknown which stronghold's wise woman would've given this quest. It's also unclear what would've triggered the line differences. One possibility is that one variant would've been used for Orcs and one for non-Orcs, though it seems more likely that one was an early, basic version, with the other being the more finalized one.

Bolfrida Brandy-Mug

Faryl talking with Bolfrida

**Bolfrida Brandy-Mug** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") who lives and works at [Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm"), a short distance east of [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables"). She lives with a [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") and two [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken"). She grows [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") in the field beside her small cottage and will [pay you](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat") five gold for every piece of wheat you bring to her.

She gets up early at 6am and eats a one-hour breakfast. She then goes out at 7am to her farm, and works for eight hours. When she is done at the farm for the day, at 3pm, she heads back to her house. She then hangs out in her house for a couple of hours, eating a two-hour dinner at 5pm, and going to bed at 11pm.

She wears some farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothes"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"), and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#000209aa "Skyrim:Hat"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farmhouse_Key "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farmhouse Key") to her farmhouse and some [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

Bolfrida is friendly to visitors. She also seems to love her job and keeps a positive attitude. She'll greet you with one of the following lines:

:   *"Welcome, welcome, welcome! Don't see many strangers out here. Come to get your hands dirty on a real farm?"*
:   *"Nothing tastes better than food you've grown yourself. Something magic about dirt and sunshine making food."*
:   *"The weather's harsh, but I like to think my sunny personality is what helps the grain grow."*

### Conversations

She can be seen conversing with her one employee, [Faryl Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Faryl_Atheron "Skyrim:Faryl Atheron"), about the farm.

:   **Faryl:** *"I don't think we're going to get those potatoes to come in."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Well of course, not with an attitude like that!"*
:   **Faryl:** *"The ground is practically frozen. We can't dig down far enough."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Come on, we just need a little elbow grease."*

They'll talk about what it would be like to try growing crops in [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind").

:   **Bolfrida:** *"I'll bet this is better than trying to grow something in Morrowind, though, isn't it?"*
:   **Faryl:** *"Firstly, I've never even seen Morrowind. Secondly, in volcanic soil the plants practically grow themselves."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Oh, my, I hadn't thought of that."*
:   **Faryl:** *"There are places in the world that aren't wrapped in ice, you know."*

They'll also talk about growing crops in permafrost.

:   **Bolfrida:** *"Now, I've been reading about the best ways to grow corn in permafrost..."*
:   **Faryl:** *"I keep telling you, without a warming enchantment, it will never grow past your ankles."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Right, but if you plow the soil with [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts")..."*
:   **Faryl:** *"Then you've salted it and nothing will grow at all. Genius."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Oh dear, I hadn't thought of that."*

Bolgeir Bearclaw

**Bolgeir Bearclaw** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") and [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") to [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), never leaving her side when she holds court in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

As housecarl for the newly appointed Jarl Elisif, Bolgeir spends the majority of his life looking after her. He sleeps in the northeastern room on the ground floor every night from 2am until 6am, when Jarl Elisif enters the throne room. He then spends the entire day by her side and only allows himself a quick one-hour meal at 6pm. When the court ends at 10pm, Bolgeir takes the opportunity to relax and just wanders around near the throne room until he heads back downstairs and goes to bed.

He carries three weapons, all crafted in [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish") quality, including a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger") and two [swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Sword "Skyrim:Orcish Sword"). He wears a set of [steel plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Plate Boots") and [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Plate Gauntlets"). He only carries a spare [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic").

## Dialogue

When approached he can say:

:   *"Please address all questions to the Steward, [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard")."*
:   *"My duty is to keep the Jarl safe. Not play nursemaid to you sycophants."*
:   *"Keep your weapon out of your hands, and we'll get along just fine."*
:   *"The Jarl has advised me not to talk about which court attendants I'd like to punch in the face. More's the pity."*

## Conversations

Even if he prefers to keep quiet, there are times when Bolgeir has to protest Jarl Elisif's rushed decisions:

:   **Elisif**: *"Steward, I have an idea that might help to bolster the morale of our people in this difficult time. I think we shall have a grand parade, and let [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") march his troops from the Blue Palace to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") in all their finery."*
:   **Falk**: *"What a... fine idea, my Jarl. However, I would suggest we wait until the [war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") has ended. After all, the General needs his soldiers out in the field, fighting battles against the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")."*
:   **Bolgeir**: *"I must protest, my Jarl. A parade would make you an easy target for a Stormcloak assassin. You're safer here in the palace."*
:   **Elisif**: *"Oh, very well. I can see there's no changing your stubborn Nord minds. But when this war is won, I will have my parade!"*
:   **Falk**: *"Yes, my Jarl."*

:   **Bolgeir**: *"We lost another five guardsmen, my Jarl. If General Tullius continues to conscript our men and send them off to battle, we'll have none left to protect the city."*
:   **Elisif**: *"Yes, I know. The general acted with my blessing. It is vital that we bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice, but that cannot happen until his army of Stormcloaks is defeated utterly."*
:   **Bolgeir**: *"Told you that, did he? I'm sworn to protect you, my Jarl, but I'm the last line of defense. The first line is the walls around this city and the men who patrol them. Men who, I might add, we're precious short on."*
:   **Elisif**: *"I'm aware of that, Bolgeir, and I appreciate your dedication. However, if we lose the war, the guardsmen of Solitude will make little difference in the end."*
:   **Bolgeir**: *"No disrespect toward the general, but sometimes I wonder if he's got your best interests at heart. In any case he won't be turnin' me into no Imperial soldier. I know my place, and it's at your side."*
:   **Elisif**: *"It comforts me to know that, Bolgeir."*

## Notes

- Unusually in the game, when he speaks, it says "Bearclaw" in the subtitles, not "Bolgeir". In almost every other instance the speaker is denoted by either their first or full name.
- You will receive a [*Letter from Bolgeir Bearclaw*](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Bolgeir_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Letter from Bolgeir Bearclaw") as part of the [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), which will begin the quest [Let Sleeping Wolves Lie](/wiki/Skyrim:Let_Sleeping_Wolves_Lie "Skyrim:Let Sleeping Wolves Lie").

# Skyrim:Bolli's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

Bolli's House

**Bolli's House** is a small, two-story residence with a cellar, near the city gates in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). It is owned by [Bolli](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli "Skyrim:Bolli"), who lives there with his wife [Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor"). It is the first house on the left when entering Riften from the north. It consists of only one zone, which is the [interior](#Bolli.27s_House).

## Related Quests

- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bolli](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli "Skyrim:Bolli")  [Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor") |

## Bolli's House

Upon entering there is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") on a stand to your left against the north wall, with a small square wooden table and two chairs to the right along the same wall. On the table are two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). In the northeast corner, under the stairs that lead to the top floor, is a food barrel. There are stairs up and down to the basement, both against the east wall. Against the south wall is a long end table holding a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender").

Bolli and Nivenor's bedroom

The stairs leading up take you straight into Bolli and Nivenor's bedroom, which consists of a double bed coming out from the middle of the west wall, with a dresser at the foot of the bed that holds a bunch of lavender and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Requested_Report "Skyrim:Requested Report") that discusses Bolli's suspicions regarding his wife cheating. To the left of the bed, against the south wall, is a wall shelf holding a wooden bowl containing three [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"). Under this is a basket containing three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), which is next to a fireplace. On the mantel are copies of *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")* and *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")*. There are two chairs pulled up in front of the fireplace. Opposite, against the north wall, is an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing gold, with a tall wardrobe to the left along the same wall.

Descending the stairs to the basement brings you to a storage area with a set of shelves against the north wall. They hold a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), several pieces of cheese, four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). A round wooden table is to the left with a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") underneath it, and hanging from a rack above are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). There is a doorway in the middle of the west wall, with a cupboard of clutter and a large vat to the left of it and a pile of firewood under the stairs opposite. Through the doorway there are several bales of straw against the south wall and several food barrels against the north wall. Hanging from the doorway are three more salmon.

## Notes

- The front door has an adept lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Bolli's House Key") to which is carried by Bolli and Nivenor.
- There is a "Loot" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the left of the entrance door.
- All containers in the house, with the exception of most barrels and sacks, are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- The Requested Report letter here may only display partially.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. It required a manually inserted pagebreak to make the whole letter readable.

Bolli

**Bolli** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who lives in his [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), and works at the [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery"). He owns the fishery, and has a charitable nature, giving away much of his wealth. He is married to the unfaithful [Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor") and has, at least on one occasion, had an extramarital affair with [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga").

He wakes up at 9am, then eats breakfast in his house for an hour. Then, at 10am, he heads outside and browses the market stalls for five hours. After that, at 3pm, he heads to the fishery to work in his office for five hours. After work, he heads to [the Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") at 8pm to eat dinner. He stays there, eating and drinking, for seven hours, until he finally heads home at 3am to go to sleep.

He wears some merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006ff45 "Skyrim:Clothes"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"), and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#0004223b "Skyrim:Hat"). He wields a leveled dagger (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality), and carries a leveled [gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Leveled_Gems "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), a fishery [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery_Key "Skyrim:Riften Fishery Key"), a house [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Bolli's House Key"), and a selection of [upper-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Caught Red Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_Red_Handed "Skyrim:Caught Red Handed")**: Gather three marks of Dibella to help [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") against [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga").
- **[Special Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Delivery_(Bolli) "Skyrim:Special Delivery (Bolli)")**: Deliver a purchase agreement to [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").
- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

## Dialogue

He's a fish-oriented man, and can greet you with:

:   *"New in town, eh? Here for the fishing I'd guess."*
:   *"There's nothing like fishing on Lake Honrich, you should try it sometime."*
:   *"If you're hungry, [Marise](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel") sells fresh fish... caught by yours truly."*

If spoken to directly he can be asked questions about himself and his work:

:   **Are you a fisherman?**
:   *"Only the best in all of Riften! I own Riften Fishery. Started out with a single fishing pole and now I have an entire building and two boats to my name. Not bad for a middle-aged Nord, eh? Too bad I haven't had the same success helping this city shed its poverty. Nivenor thinks I'm wasting my time trying, but I disagree."*

    :   **You mentioned Nivenor.**
    :   *"Nivenor is my wife. How I was ever able to meet such a gorgeous creature is one of life's mysteries. We're... at odds about my charity. She thinks the people in this town have become lazy and expecting a handout. I try to include her in my lessons from [Maramal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maramal "Skyrim:Maramal") over at the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara"), but she prefers to shop instead. Different strokes, eh?"*

:   **You sound quite charitable.**
:   *"Yes, I suppose someone has to be around here. Have you seen the condition of this sorry excuse for a city? Beggars roam the streets, crime runs rampant and the threat of war is driving away business. The paltry amount of coin that I place in the charity box at the temple is the least I can do to help."*

When exiting conversation, he will say:

:   *"Remember to give at the temple."*

### Caught Red Handed

During [Caught Red Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_Red_Handed "Skyrim:Caught Red Handed"), you'll be told by [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") that he slept with [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga"). When you confront him with this information, he'll act shocked:

:   **Haelga gave you a Mark of Dibella. I want it.**
:   *"I have no idea what you're talking about. I'd never sleep with anyone besides my good wife, [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa")."*

You will now have to persuade him:

| Option | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| Hand it over and no one has to know.  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: "*Look, it was one night, okay? I think she slipped something in my drink. I haven't even been back to the Bunkhouse since. Just take this damn thing. I never want to see it again.*" **Failed**: *"Hand what over? I have no idea what you're talking about."* |
| Give it to me or else!  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: *"Look, it was one night, okay? I think she slipped something in my drink. I haven't even been back to the Bunkhouse since. Just take this damn thing. I never want to see it again.*" **Failed**: *"Or else what? You don't scare me."* |
| Never mind. My mistake. | *"I should say so."* |

### Special Delivery

When asked who buys his fish, he'll present an offer:

:   **Who buys all your fish?**
:   *"I sell my catch across a good portion of Skyrim... it's worth its weight in gold to me. The only untapped market left is [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). However, I just got word that [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr") at the [Silver Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn")*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *might be interested. If you're headed that way, I would appreciate you delivering a [purchase agreement](/wiki/Skyrim:Purchase_Agreement_(Bolli) "Skyrim:Purchase Agreement (Bolli)") for me. You'd be paid, of course."*

:   :   **Okay, I'll do it.**
    :   *"Good. Kleppr will pay you as soon as you arrive with the letter. Here you are."*

:   :   **Maybe another time.**
    :   *"Certainly."*

If you have yet to deliver the letter, he may ask:

:   *"Did you get that purchase agreement to Markarth yet?"*

Once you have delivered the letter to Kleppr, he'll say:

:   *"Thanks again for the delivery to Markarth. What can I do for you?"*

### Spread the Love

He will accept a pamphlet:

:   **Here, brother. Blessings of Mara upon you.**
:   *"Thank you. Blessings of Mara upon you as well."*

## Conversations

Bolli can often be seen talking to his wife or other Riften citizens:

**Bolli**: *"Nivenor, my darling. What a pleasant surprise."*
**Nivenor**: *"Oh! Bolli... yes, hello."*
**Bolli**: *"Will we be dining together this evening after my work at the fishery?"*
**Nivenor**: *"(Sigh) Yes, as usual. I'll be there."*

**Bolli**: *"Decided to show up for work today, eh?"*
**Nivenor**: *"And just what's that supposed to mean?"*
**Bolli**: *"It means I have a business to run, I need to have the books straight and you're barely ever here!"*
**Nivenor**: *"For goodness sake, Bolli! You barely lift a finger yourself when you're here except to point at things for your workers to do. Let them do the work, that's what you pay them for!"*
**Bolli**: *"(Sigh)"*

**Nivenor**: *"Bolli, I was looking at the finances and I noticed you've been donating gold to the Temple of Mara. Are you out of your mind?"*
**Bolli**: *"Maramal's been helping me through a rough patch. I just wanted to pay him back. It's not like he's keeping it!"*
**Nivenor**: *"Uh huh. I'm sure he runs outside with the coin and throws it up in the air so Mara herself can catch it. Come off of it, Bolli."*
**Bolli**: *"You may be my wife, but this is my business, so just do your job. Don't worry, you'll still have plenty of gold left over to waste on trinkets."*

**Bolli**: *"[Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi"), what's this bill for 300 septims!"*
**Madesi**: *"Begging your pardon, milord. Your wife has run up quite an account in the last few months."*
**Bolli**: *"Outrageous! Who does she think she is?!"*
**Madesi**: *"I believe she's trying to look as ravishing as possible for you, milord."*
**Bolli**: *"Oh, well... I suppose that's a noble cause. I'll settle this bill at the end of the day. Thank you."*

**Bolli**: *"[Grelka](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelka "Skyrim:Grelka"), I wanted to talk about that suit of leather armor you sold me. The fasteners are already coming loose."*
**Grelka**: *"Fine. It'll be five septims to repair it."*
**Bolli**: *"Why should I pay for a repair on something I just bought?"*
**Grelka**: *"All right, all right. Just bring it to me tomorrow and I'll fix it for you."*

**Bolli**: *"So while I was in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), I heard news that something terrible happened at [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen")."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"You've heard too? They say the town was completely destroyed by a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin")."*
**Bolli**: *"If that's true, then we have much more to fear than the Thieves Guild."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"I'd still keep an eye on my purse if I was you."*

**Bolli**: *"I have two more bushels for you, Marise. That should keep you well-stocked."*
**Marise**: *"Sounds good. May I owe you for them?"*
**Bolli**: *"Of course. Say, how are you going to sell all those fish before they spoil?"*
**Marise**: *"You know I can't tell you that. As soon as I do, and you have a few meads in you, everyone will know."*

**[Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa")**: *"Hello Bolli. How's the fishing?"*
**Bolli**: *"Bountiful. Although I would like to have anchored a bit closer to [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate")."*
**Drifa**: *"Why didn't you then?"*
**Bolli**: *"When I got close, the [mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercenary_(Goldenglow) "Skyrim:Mercenary (Goldenglow)") [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth") hired to protect the estate just waved me off. I don't think he wants visitors anymore."*

**Bolli**: *"[Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta"), we need to talk."*
**Wujeeta**: *"I know, I was late. I'm sorry."*
**Bolli**: *"I don't know what I'm going to do with you. I can't just let this go unpunished."*
**Wujeeta**: *"Please, don't get rid of me! I need the coin. I... I'll work for free for the rest of this week. Please!"*
**Bolli**: *"(Sigh) Very well. You're lucky Maramal has placed me in a very forgiving mood."*

**Bolli**: *"[Talen](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei") my friend, up for some fishing this week?"*
**Talen**: *"I don't know Bolli. It's getting dangerous outside the walls."*
**Bolli**: *"Oh come now, what's a dragon or two compared to a day full of fishing!"*
**Talen**: *"That's not funny, Bolli. People are scared."*

At the Bee and Barb, he can be seen talking to Haelga about their affair:

**Bolli**: *"Haelga, we need to stop seeing each other."*
**Haelga**: *"Oh, Bolli you silly man. You weren't saying that when you were licking that [honey](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey "Skyrim:Honey") off my..."*
**Bolli**: *"Haelga! That's just it. I can't keep up with you. Your Dibellan techniques... they're exhausting."*
**Haelga**: *"Is it really me, or is it your wife? You need to make a choice Bolli. The honey or her."*

**Haelga**: *"When are you going to take me away from here Bolli?"*
**Bolli**: *"I told you, I can't just pick up and leave. I have my wife, my business... not to mention you have the [Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse")."*
**Haelga**: *"That old place? I could care less about it. Its*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *you I want, Bolli."*
**Bolli**: *"I... I'm sorry Haelga, I can't. Not yet."*

## Notes

- On the second floor of his house there's a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Requested_Report "Skyrim:Requested Report") regarding his marriage.
- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* (and a single internal name) refers to Bolli as **Bolli Trout-Purse**.

## Bugs

- During "Caught Red Handed", when asking Bolli about his relationship with Haelga he will remark that he has never slept with any woman other than his wife [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa"). However, Bolli's wife is [Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Find [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") and recruit him into the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard") |
| Location(s): | [Ruunvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Excavation "Skyrim:Ruunvald Excavation") |
| Reward: | [Staff of Ruunvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ruunvald "Skyrim:Staff of Ruunvald") Master trainer in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") |
| ID: | DLC1HunterBaseStage2 |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** Reach [stage 60](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard)#Quest_Stages "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") of [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)"). | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Reach [stage 60](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard)#Quest_Stages "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") of [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)"). | | |

Rescue [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius")!

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard").
2. Speak with [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran").
3. Travel to [Ruunvald Excavation](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Excavation "Skyrim:Ruunvald Excavation").
4. Find [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius").

### A Secret Request

*"Gunmar and I have been talking"*

After recruiting [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard") and [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") into the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") during the quest [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order"), [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") will send you on a hunt for [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus"), a [Moth priest](/wiki/Lore:Cult_of_the_Ancestor_Moth "Lore:Cult of the Ancestor Moth") traveling around Skyrim, starting the quest [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)"). During your search for the priest, you will find that [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") have taken Dexion hostage inside [Forebears' Holdout](/wiki/Skyrim:Forebears%27_Holdout "Skyrim:Forebears' Holdout"). At that point in the quest ([stage 60](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard)#Quest_Stages "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")), Sorine and Gunmar will have settled down in [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard")'s western area, and while keeping up appearances, they have secretly discussed the vampire threat. Sorine will ask you directly: *"Do you have a moment? Gunmar and I have been talking and, well, we're slightly worried. We both realized that if Isran's even allowed us in here, he must be really concerned. And if he's that concerned, the situation must be pretty bad. Make sense?"*

She then admits that she and Gunmar agreed that they could use the help of one 'Florentius', a former priest of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay") and quite eccentric. The problem is Isran and Florentius have a past, and Isran obviously dislikes the priest. Another problem is that Isran is the only one who knows the location of Florentius, and she leaves it to you to get the information. This starts the quest and you will have to seek out Isran, although Sorine encourages you to keep her involvement a secret. When confronted with the request, Isran will immediately guess the persons responsible: *"Who said something, Sorine or Gunmar? I thought they'd have learned their lesson by now. I don't trust that man, and I don't want him here."* He then reckons the Dawnguard can use all the help they can get and will point you towards [Ruunvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald "Skyrim:Ruunvald"), an excavation site recently explored by [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilant of Stendarr"), including Florentius, with the comment: *"If he can maintain some appearance of normalcy, I'll allow him to stay."*

### The Charmed Vigilants

A [Charmed Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Charmed_Vigilant "Skyrim:Charmed Vigilant")

The [Ruunvald Excavation](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Excavation "Skyrim:Ruunvald Excavation") is located on the mountainside east of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") and consists of a tent and what appears to be a mine entrance. Examine the tent for a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Volk%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Volk's Journal"), the personal observations of a Vigilant named [Volk](/wiki/Skyrim:Volk "Skyrim:Volk"). The journal mentions that Volk and Florentius both had the tiresome job of guarding the entrance, until they were finally invited to join the dig by a Vigilant named Apa. Although the two guards were beginning to find the whole situation suspicious, they clearly ventured into the mines as ordered, and you will have to do the same.

***I am certain we are digging in the right place. I can feel it in my bones, and I dream of finding Ruunvald at night. Even in my waking hours, I can almost hear a reassuring voice telling me we are going the right way.***

Upon entering, you can hear digging noises from below, so head down the slope to the woodworks set up by the Vigilants and notice the person standing on the adjacent platform, without moving at all. As you get closer you will see an odd red fog covering his face, and when he notices you he will immediately attack and identify himself as a [Charmed Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Charmed_Vigilant "Skyrim:Charmed Vigilant"). From the chamber behind you, another Vigilant will rush to his aid, so dispose of them both and examine the first chamber for a locked chest with minor loot and, on a crate next to the northern tunnel, *[Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Discovering_Ruunvald,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. I")*, a detailed journal written by [Moric Sidrey](/wiki/Skyrim:Moric_Sidrey "Skyrim:Moric Sidrey"), the Vigilant who discovered the place.

### Dream of Ruunvald

[Husky](/wiki/Skyrim:Husky "Skyrim:Husky") attacks!

Proceed through the northern tunnel until you reach an intersection with a patrolling Vigilant and a [booby-trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"). Use the oil to your advantage or pick the fight and beware of another Vigilant near the [malachite vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Malachite Ore Vein") to the northwest. Head down the southern tunnel and claim the contents of a minor loot chest. Proceed forward until you reach a large room with two Vigilants and a [husky](/wiki/Skyrim:Husky "Skyrim:Husky"). Take them all down and examine the southwestern corner for several useful potions near a bedroll. In the center of the room, on a crate near another bedroll, sits *[Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:Discovering_Ruunvald,_Vol._II "Skyrim:Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. II")* with more of Moric Sidrey's detailed observations on the dig, along with some unsettling personal issues.

***It must have something to do with the cramped spaces, but I have found myself prone to aches in my head. While these hardly deter me from my leadership role, I have found myself distracted at times. I have had many a conversation with the workers where I drift off, only to have them call me back to reality. Sometimes I lose small amounts of time and can't remember what I've done.***

Locate the narrow tunnel to the east and proceed forward as it twists and turns. A locked chest can be found under the woodworks ahead, and, further down the tunnel, yet another Vigilant accompanied by a husky. A huge wooden scaffold leads down into the next chamber, obviously used by the hardworking Vigilants as storage, as several crates and barrels are stacked up, along with a bookshelf with common books. On the table near the shelf, guarded by a Vigilant, is [volume III](/wiki/Skyrim:Discovering_Ruunvald,_Vol._III "Skyrim:Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. III") of the journal, detailing not only his own recurring headaches, but headaches among his crew of Vigilants as well. However, despite the pain and blackouts, the dig continued, even if Moric Sidrey's attention turned away from Ruunwald towards something else in the depths of the mine.

***I dream we'll finally reach Ruunvald, and I can't help but reflect on what this will mean to my reputation! My family will be so proud, especially my father, Minorne. He and mother have always been interested in my studies, even if my sister Minorne was not. But I'm most excited to reveal my findings to my colleagues, Minorne and Minorne, and perhaps my mentor Minorne. Oh, won't they all be pleased?***

### Discovering Ruunvald

The entrance to [Ruunvald Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Temple "Skyrim:Ruunvald Temple")

The next area contains more crates and barrels, along with three [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") triggering [mounted crossbows](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow_Mount "Skyrim:Crossbow Mount"), so dodge the plates and proceed through the northern tunnel into a huge chamber filled with Nordic architecture, a hanging bridge, and several Charmed Vigilants. After fighting your way over the bridge, one of the attackers will have a familiar name, specifically [Volk](/wiki/Skyrim:Volk "Skyrim:Volk"), who initially guarded the entrance with Florentius but was charmed along with his colleagues. Before heading downstairs, examine the enclosed western room for a chest. At the bottom of the large chamber, examine the northeastern corner for an owned bed, a chest, and some food. This chamber also marks the spot where Moric and his crew finally broke through the right wall and found the entrance to [Ruunvald Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Temple "Skyrim:Ruunvald Temple"). However, the [fourth and final volume](/wiki/Skyrim:Discovering_Ruunvald,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. IV") of Moric Sidrey's journal, which can be found on a barrel near the entrance to the Temple, reveals that Moric and his workers were all led to the Temple by a strange voice that slowly seduced them all.

***I have found my muse and her name is [Minorne](/wiki/Skyrim:Minorne "Skyrim:Minorne"). Reading back over old journals, I realize she has called to me from deep inside Ruunvald. She is the voice I've been hearing, the one who has called me ever downwards into the mountain. The Vigilants, the workers, they hear her too! What joy to learn that I am not alone in her love! Oh, Minorne, how would we have ever found this place without you!***

As expected, Ruunvald Temple is a typical [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins"), although no draugr enemies can be found here. Proceed down the first hallway to a table holding the book *[Minorne](/wiki/Skyrim:Minorne_(book) "Skyrim:Minorne (book)")*, the ramblings of former Vigilant of Stendarr [Moric Sidrey](/wiki/Skyrim:Moric_Sidrey "Skyrim:Moric Sidrey"), and a love letter to his new mistress in the depths of the ruin, [Minorne](/wiki/Skyrim:Minorne "Skyrim:Minorne"). It details his eternal love and how he managed to lure even more Vigilants into the ruin, simply by lying. It also contains a clue to the whereabouts on your target, [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius"), and his hatred towards anyone who would harm his mistress: *"There are fools in this world that do not heed to her beautiful voice. The guard, Florentius, sent from the Beacon, he still prays to [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay"), an absentee god who pales in comparison to Minorne! I will pray to the goddess I can see! May he rot in his cage!"*

### The Mistress

Minorne attacks

Proceed down the available path until you reach a large chamber, with stairs leading up to an altar and a cage, and three shadowy figures wandering around. They turn out to be another Charmed Vigilant, Moric Sidrey himself, and his godly mistress Minorne, who is actually just an ordinary [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), who is busy torturing the imprisoned Florentius for no apparent reason, using her leveled [Destruction spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells#Destruction_Spells "Skyrim:Spells"). All three will attack you on sight, so take them down and loot Minorne's corpse for the unique [Staff of Ruunvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ruunvald "Skyrim:Staff of Ruunvald") and the [Ruunvald Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Key "Skyrim:Ruunvald Key").

*"Isran? My help? Is this... some kind of a joke?"*

Inside the cage, Priest of Arkay Florentius Baenius will show little of the normalcy requested by [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") when he shows his gratitude: *"I knew you had it in you! Arkay wasn't so sure. Between you and me, I think he didn't expect you to make it. But not me! I knew it all along!"* He will then ask how he can repay you, so ask him to meet you at [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") and he will ask why. When you explain Isran needs his help he will be quite surprised: *"Isran? My help? Is this... some kind of a joke? Did Arkay put you up to this? Isran's done nothing but mock me. He's never given me the respect I deserve."* After you beg for his help, he will finally agree, but only due to strange voices in his head: *"Look, I've just gotten myself out of quite a mess here, in case you haven't noticed, and while I appreciate your help, I... What's that? No, that's not what I... Yes, but... Are you sure? Really? Fine. Arkay says it's a good idea for me to go. I don't agree, but he's not the sort of fellow you can just ignore. I'll see you at Fort Dawnguard, then. Don't worry, Arkay will show me the way."* He will then leave the ruin and the quest will finish. While Florentius takes the long way back through the mine, locate the southern door and unlock it with the key. It leads to the deceased warlock's private quarters and contains a boss-leveled chest, the [quest-related](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages") book *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a handle which reveals a hidden pathway back to Skyrim. The next time you visit Fort Dawnguard, Florentius will have changed into Dawnguard armor, opened up his shop as an alchemist, will be available as a master trainer in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), and an alchemy lab will be found across from the arcane enchanter.

## Notes

- If you have access to [invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility "Skyrim:Invisibility") (potions or spells), and/or the [Throw Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Throw_Voice "Skyrim:Throw Voice") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shouts "Skyrim:Shouts"), you may be able to bypass all of the Charmed Vigilants and only kill Minorne if your [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill is high enough.
- Any Charmed Vigilants that are still alive when Minorne dies will also die instantly; this also counts for the ones that are raised with the [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") spell.
- Completing this quest unlocks the radiant quests [Rescue](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue "Skyrim:Rescue") and [Lost Relic](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Relic "Skyrim:Lost Relic"). See the quest articles for more information.
- If you finish this quest while [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") is still active, Florentius may also be present when [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") reads [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana")'s [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll_(Sun) "Skyrim:Elder Scroll (Sun)").
- This quest can be completed at any time, even after finishing the main quest line for the Dawnguard.
- If you talk to Florentius through the gate without unlocking it, he will still show up at Fort Dawnguard later, making good on his parting words of "*Don't worry, Arkay will show me the way.*" [*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Bolstering_the_Ranks)*]

## Bugs

- Florentius may sometimes turn hostile and attack you, thus not letting you initiate conversation with him.
  - Possible fixes include loading a previous save and waiting outside the cave for 24 hours before going back in, using a [Pacify](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(effect) "Skyrim:Pacify (effect)") spell or the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") shout to calm him long enough to initiate conversation, or trying to initiate conversation when he is kneeling in recovery.
  - One of the possible causes is having a high bounty in the Reach (possibly in other holds as well).
- The Dawnguard may try to kill you if you fail to rescue Florentius. **?**
- If you have already completed [Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky"), talking to Isran will automatically trigger the start of [Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment"). You will not be able to get information on Florentius. **?**
  -  You can circumvent having to talk to Isran using the command `setstage DLC1HunterBaseStage2 20`. Note that Florentius is spawned during stage 10 of the quest, so you need to complete that first, or use `setstage DLC1HunterBaseStage2 10`. Don't skip straight to stage 20.
- If you feed on Charmed Vigilants while in werewolf form, you will get a red aura around your head. The red aura will not leave you even if you change to human form, and will cause laggy graphics on weaker systems.
- Florentius may not follow you to Fort Dawnguard after he is rescued. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Bolstering the Ranks (DLC1HunterBaseStage2) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | It's been suggested that the Dawnguard could use the help of a man named Florentius, a former Priest of Arkay. I need to speak with Isran to find out if he knows where Florentius might be. *Objective 10:* Speak with Isran |
| 20 |  | I've been asked to find a man named Florentius in the hopes that he can assist the Dawnguard. I've learned that he was last seen helping the Vigilants of Stendarr in Ruunvald. *Objective 20:* Find Florentius |
| 200 | ☑ | I've rescued Florentius Baenius from Ruunvald, where he was being held captive. He's agreed to return to Fort Dawnguard and aid our cause. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1HunterBaseStage2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1HunterBaseStage2`.

# Skyrim:Bolund

## Overview

| Bolund (RefID: 0001981F) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionFalkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionFalkreath "Skyrim:CrimeFactionFalkreath"); [FalkreathGrayPineGoodsFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FalkreathGrayPineGoodsFaction "Skyrim:FalkreathGrayPineGoodsFaction"); [JobLumberjackFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:JobLumberjackFaction "Skyrim:JobLumberjackFaction"); [TownFalkreathFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownFalkreathFaction "Skyrim:TownFalkreathFaction") | | |

Bolund working at the lumber mill

**Bolund** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") that owns and operates [Falkreath's](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") lumber mill. He lives in the general store [Gray Pine Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Pine_Goods "Skyrim:Gray Pine Goods") with his brother [Solaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Solaf "Skyrim:Solaf"). He tends to have a rather rude personality. He will sell [lumber](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") to you if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.

From 7am to 8pm, he wanders around the sawmill, cutting wood. At other times he will wander the town, sometimes being in the store and sometimes visiting the [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink"). He never sleeps.

He wears farmer attire, including [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006c1d9 "Skyrim:Clothing") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a5 "Skyrim:Clothing") and carries his copy of the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Gray_Pine_Goods "Skyrim:Key to Gray Pine Goods") to Gray Pine Goods, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

If you are a Nord he will greet you with:

:   *"A hearty welcome to Falkreath! All of Skyrim's true sons are welcome here!"*

If you are not a Nord he will simply say:

:   *"I can't believe we let provincials like you wander Skyrim."*

If you play as an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") he will be downright hateful and say:

:   *"Stay out of my way, boot."*

He may further demonstrate his dislike of outsiders and [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") sympathizers when he remarks:

:   *"You'll find my brother Solaf and I are the only true Nords in Falkreath."*

He also dislikes local innkeeper [Valga Vinicia](/wiki/Skyrim:Valga_Vinicia "Skyrim:Valga Vinicia") and will say:

:   *"That Valga Vinicia is a gossip and a troublemaker."*

### Conversations

When Bolund meets his brother meet inside their store, they may engage in conversation:

:   **Bolund**: *"Another day in this graveyard."*
:   **Solaf**: *"Falkreath is a fine place to be, Bolund."*
:   **Bolund**: *"Falkreath is where people go to die. We could be fighting, taking back Nord land!"*
:   **Solaf**: *"Falkreath is our home, a place where we have good jobs under a good Jarl. Until the war comes to us we stay put."*

At the inn, he can be observed being his usual blunt self while talking to serving girl [Narri](/wiki/Skyrim:Narri "Skyrim:Narri"):

:   **Bolund**: *"Hey gossip, bring me a drink."*
:   **Narri**: *"Bolund, you're going to die of thirst if you keep calling me that."*

He was also originally intended to be rude towards [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod"), although the latter never sets foot inside the inn in the final game, making the scene go unused:

:   **Bolund**: *"Hey, Lod, how is the worst farmer in the hold doing?"*
:   **Lod**: *"The Gentle Repose is barren, it was barren the day my father claimed the land and it's barren now."*
:   **Bolund**: *"Sure it is, Lod. Sure it is."*

## Notes

- His brother Solaf is a true [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), although much more forgiving than Bolund. When asked about his brother he will say: *"His name's Bolund. He's the one who works the lumber mill down by the river. If you meet him, don't expect much in the way o' conversation. He ain't one for talking, especially with folk he don't know."* and *"Don't mind Bolund. He's young and gets riled easily."* Even when you enter Gray Pine Goods for the first time, he will make excuses for his brother: *"Well met. Unlike my brother, I've no dislike of strangers."*

## Bugs

- He will only exit Gray Pine Goods if you enter the shop, and therefore will not be found at the mill when entering Falkreath.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- Bolund has no sleep package, making it impossible for him to do so.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
