# Skyrim:Bonechill Passage

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Bonechill Passage ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bonechill+Passage)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |

| Location | |
| East of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") Southwest of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") | 1 |

Bonechill Passage

**Bonechill Passage** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). It contains only one zone, *[Bonechill Passage](#Bonechill_Passage)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Ruined shack

Following a dirt path south from the road between Falkreath and [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") east of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch") will take you past an unmarked [ruined shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Falkreath#Prospector.27s_Shack:_Bonechill_Ridge "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Falkreath") that was attacked by the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") occupying [Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent") to the south. The path curves east around an outcrop of rock before proceeding south to a large stone square arch over the steps leading up to the cave entrance. A [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is just west of the base of the steps.

### Bonechill Passage

Interior

Upon entering, you are in an ice tunnel heading south. To the left is a skeleton with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") beside it and a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") opposite. A leveled snow animal or creature (which may be a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"), [ice wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"), [ice wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), or [snowy sabre cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowy_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Snowy Sabre Cat")) guards the path ahead. Moving forward, to the right is a mammoth skull with a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") lying beside it. Farther along and also to the right is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") next to another skeleton and a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, MidYear, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_MidYear,_v6 "Skyrim:2920, MidYear, v6")*.

The tunnel narrows and bends to the east, then opens into an unroofed section with a bridge across a chasm and a leveled snow animal or creature on the far side. To the left at the start of the bridge is a dead [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"). Under the bridge are two lootable skeletons and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Across the bridge, the tunnel rises quite sharply, turns twice, and leads to the exit near Ancient's Ascent.

## Notes

- Among other items described on the [dedicated page](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Falkreath#Prospector.27s_Shack:_Bonechill_Ridge "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Falkreath"), the ruined shack contains a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill book *[Purloined Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Purloined_Shadows "Skyrim:Purloined Shadows")*.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

-  Some users have experienced a crash to desktop after entering Bonechill Passage. This crash appears to have been fixed in an early patch, though there is no mention in any patch notes.
  -  The issue can be worked around by playing in windowed mode while inside the cave.

## Maps

- 

  Bonechill Passage

# Skyrim:Bones for a Crow

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: *not written*  **Reward**: *not written* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Hunt down the Forsworn Crowstooth.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Ask an innkeeper for work |
| Location(s): | [Crowstooth's Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth%27s_Camp "Skyrim:Crowstooth's Camp"), [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point") |
| Reward: | [Dragonbone Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbone_Mail "Skyrim:Dragonbone Mail"), [Dismal Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismal_Visage "Skyrim:Dismal Visage"), [Namira's Itch](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Itch "Skyrim:Namira's Itch"), [Tyrant's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Tyrant%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Tyrant's Bane") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE059\_Quest, ccBGSSSE059\_MiscQuest , ID: FExxx824 |
| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragon_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") |

Forsworn have been pushing their presence further and further east. (Crowstooth's Tower)

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to an innkeeper to receive the *[Bounty for Crowstooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_for_Crowstooth "Skyrim:Bounty for Crowstooth")*.
2. Locate [Crowstooth's Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth%27s_Camp "Skyrim:Crowstooth's Camp") near [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower"), and kill the hagraven [Linelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle "Skyrim:Linelle").
3. Learn a potential location of [Crowstooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth "Skyrim:Crowstooth") by reading *[Linelle's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle%27s_Note "Skyrim:Linelle's Note")*.
4. Travel to [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point") and find the tower to the right of the north staircase. Kill [Crowstooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth "Skyrim:Crowstooth").
5. Search the tower and find the body of [Bjormund Wind-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjormund_Wind-Strider "Skyrim:Bjormund Wind-Strider").
6. *(Optional)* Read *[Bjormund's Diary](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjormund%27s_Diary "Skyrim:Bjormund's Diary")*.
7. Take Bjormund's [Dragonbone Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbone_Mail "Skyrim:Dragonbone Mail") and other [Dragonplate Insulated](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Items#Dragonplate_Insulated "Skyrim:Dragon Items") armor pieces to complete the quest.

## Detailed Walkthrough

To begin this quest, speak to an innkeeper for work and receive the *[Bounty for Crowstooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_for_Crowstooth "Skyrim:Bounty for Crowstooth")*. This bounty states that [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") raiding parties have been pushing further and further east, along the Jerall Mountains. It also states that Crowstooth has been separated from her forces, and that she is believed to have fled with considerable spoils. In an effort to put an end to this threat, anyone killing Crowstooth may claim her stolen loot.

Head to [Crowstooth's Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth%27s_Camp "Skyrim:Crowstooth's Camp"), south of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur"). Here you will have to fight two Forsworn, a witch and [Linelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle "Skyrim:Linelle"), a hagraven. Search Linelle's body to find her [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Linelle%27s_Note "Skyrim:Linelle's Note"), which reveals that Crowstooth has headed to [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point").

Travel to Arcwind Point, and head up to the tower, where you will have to fight Forsworn. Inside the tower on the ground floor is [Alvasorr the Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvasorr_the_Rat "Skyrim:Alvasorr the Rat"), a Namira-worshipping Khajiit. Loot Alvasorr after defeating him for the [Dismal Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismal_Visage "Skyrim:Dismal Visage") and [Namira's Itch](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Itch "Skyrim:Namira's Itch"). At the upper part of the tower is Crowstooth, who wields [Tyrant's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Tyrant%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Tyrant's Bane"). After killing her, go to the very top of the tower to find the body of [Bjormund Wind-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjormund_Wind-Strider "Skyrim:Bjormund Wind-Strider") who wears the [Dragonbone Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbone_Mail "Skyrim:Dragonbone Mail"), [Dragonplate Insulated Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonplate_Insulated_Boots "Skyrim:Dragonplate Insulated Boots"), [Dragonplate Insulated Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonplate_Insulated_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dragonplate Insulated Gauntlets") and a [Dragonplate Insulated Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonplate_Insulated_Helmet "Skyrim:Dragonplate Insulated Helmet"). He also has [Nord Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), an [Amulet of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Amulet of Akatosh"), a random selection of loot, and *[Bjormund's Diary](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjormund%27s_Diary "Skyrim:Bjormund's Diary")*, which recounts the origin of the dragon bone armor.

An additional item can be found within [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") in Solitude. *[Guard's Dossier: Bjormund Wind-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Dossier:_Bjormund_Wind-Strider "Skyrim:Guard's Dossier: Bjormund Wind-Strider")* is on a table in a side room off of the War Room.

## Notes

- An easy way to reach [Crowstooth's Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth%27s_Camp "Skyrim:Crowstooth's Camp") is to travel through [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower"). After making it to the tower apex, pull the lever and head right over to the camp.
- The [Dragonbone Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbone_Mail "Skyrim:Dragonbone Mail") found in this quest has 100% fire resistance. It is impossible to induce this perk onto a torso piece via enchanting. This is no accident, though. [According to Nordic legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjormund%27s_Diary "Skyrim:Bjormund's Diary"), the original Bjormund, who wore a dragonbone cuirass, strode through fire as if it was wind.
- Crowstooth may detect you before you reach the tower and descend to attack you. She can join forces with the high-level draugr at the top of the stairs, making for a difficult fight.

## Bugs

- [Bjormund Wind-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjormund_Wind-Strider "Skyrim:Bjormund Wind-Strider")'s body might not be found atop the tower. This could be caused by killing [Crowstooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth "Skyrim:Crowstooth") via ranged attacks before entering the tower.
- Once started, you can shortcut the quest by simply going straight to Arcwind point and climbing up the tower to find Bjormund's body and the armor.
- In case the body is not found on top of the tower, it can be spawned with the following command: `player.placeatme FExxx81C`.

# Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Dragon Lair.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Dragon_Lair.png) | Dragon Lair: Bonestrewn Crest ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bonestrewn+Crest)) | | |

| # of [Orichalcum](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore") | 1 |

Bonestrewn Crest

**Bonestrewn Crest** is a mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") south of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Frost Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The lair is riddled with mammoth bones, hence the name "Bonestrewn". It has a blueish mist, and a number of [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plants grow here. It can be accessed via a slope on the south side. The word wall is found at the top of the hill.

Before the [dragons' return](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the word wall will be guarded by three [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton").

After the dragons' return, the word wall will be guarded by a leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon").

Regardless of whether [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") has been completed, the boss chest is north of the word wall.

## Notes

- There are two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") here; one is on the right just before reaching the top of the slope, and the other is to the right just after reaching the top.
- One [orichalcum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") can be found 140 ft west-southwest, at the bottom of the mountain.
- The dragon that spawns here does not rest on the word wall or the ground before it; instead, it constantly circles the mountain until it detects you or a follower, whereupon it will initiate combat.
- Due to the location's proximity to [Steamcrag Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamcrag_Camp "Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp") and another [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") herding two [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") in the tundra below, the dragon might choose to fight them during its battle with you.
- Bonestrewn Crest also [appears](/wiki/Online:Bonestrewn_Crest "Online:Bonestrewn Crest") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

# Skyrim:Boneyard

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Worldspace: Boneyard | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Bonemen](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneman "Skyrim:Boneman"), [Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(dragon) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (dragon)") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC01SoulCairnBoneyardEntrance | |
| Location | |
| [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") | |

Boneyard

The **Boneyard** is an enclosed graveyard in the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn").

You will have to enter the Boneyard as part of the quest [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death"). You cannot wait or fast travel inside.

## Walkthrough

Upon entering the Boneyard, you will pass along a narrow passage before it opens into a large courtyard. Surrounding the central courtyard are raised sections, with stairs leading up to healing wells. As soon as you enter, [Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(dragon) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (dragon)") will be flying around in the sky, and bonemen will begin to rise. It is best to concentrate on fighting the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"), as bonemen will continue to rise to replace their fallen until you defeat Durnehviir, at which point any remaining bonemen will immediately die.

When you have defeated Durnehviir, you will not absorb his soul like other dragons. You will only be able to loot his body if you activate it quickly, before it burns to nothing; even if you do manage to loot the body, you will obtain [dragon bones](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bone "Skyrim:Dragon Bone"), but no dragon scales or heartscales. You can now either follow [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica"), or investigate the alcove to the southeast on your own. Valerica will be surprised when you vanquish Durnehviir, since from what she's read, he couldn't be slain by normal means. She then considers that you may have only displaced his physical form while he reconstitutes himself; she has no idea how long that process might take.

In the alcove, you will find an ornate box that contains the [Elder Scroll (Blood)](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll_(Blood) "Skyrim:Elder Scroll (Blood)"). You cannot interact with the box, but by speaking to Valerica, she will open it, enabling you to pick up the scroll. To the left is an alchemy lab, and on either side of the box are the ingredients, potions, and books listed below. Once you have the scroll, the exit is to the southwest.

Upon exiting after defeating Durnehviir and retrieving the Elder Scroll, you will find Durnehviir reforming ahead on a small structure. Don't attack him if you want to acquire his dragon shouts. He will teach you the [Summon Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Durnehviir "Skyrim:Summon Durnehviir") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") right away, which lets you summon him to fight for you anywhere in [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"), provided you're outdoors. Then, each of the first three times he's summoned in Tamriel, he will also teach you a word of the [Soul Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Tear "Skyrim:Soul Tear") shout. Alternatively, you can attack him immediately, before he has a chance to speak; once you defeat him again, you can loot five dragon bones from him, but you will still not absorb his soul, and you will miss out on the two dragon shouts. While traveling back toward the portal, you may be ambushed by several bonemen, who rise from piles of bones on your left as you proceed south.

## Notes

- None of the items here are considered owned, making them free to take anytime.

## Bugs

- The entry way from the Soul Cairn into the Boneyard may lack finalization on the navmesh under the door which can result in NPCs being unable to follow you in.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Books

## Overview

Hundreds of **books** can be found in Skyrim. Most books provide backstory or cover [lore](/wiki/Lore:Main_Page "Lore:Main Page") material. However, there are three special types of books:

- [Skill Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books"): opening the book for the first time gives you a one point increase in a specific [skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills")
- [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"): opening the book for the first time teaches you a [spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells")
- [Quest Books](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Quest_Books "Category:Skyrim-Quest Books"): books that are needed for or related to [quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Quests "Skyrim:Quests")

These special books are each listed on their own individual page.

Other types of reading material found in the game include [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls") and [notes and letters](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes "Skyrim:Notes"). For books and notes added by [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club_Books "Skyrim:Creation Club Books"). A list of books broken down by subject can be found [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Books_by_Subject "Skyrim:Books by Subject").

## Book Types

Standard books in the game are all placed in one of five leveled lists, as provided on each individual book page.

The primary use of the book type is for books found in randomly-generated loot, including [containers](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers "Skyrim:Containers") and some enemies (in particular, [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [Warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock")). These random books are level-dependent, as specified in the following table. The selection is also weighted to make List 0 books the most common books even at high levels. For example, at level 15 you have a 4 in 9 chance of finding List 0 books, a 3 in 9 chance of finding List 1 books, and a 2 in 9 chance of finding List 2 books.

In addition, the books stocked by [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") are determined by the book type. His inventory is not level-dependent; even List 4 books can be purchased from him at level 1. However, he only stocks a fixed number of books of each type, meaning that the chances of finding any specific List 4 book are very small.

| Book Leveled List | Level | Chances | Out of | [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [List 0](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_0 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 0") | 1 | 4 | 4 | Stocks 10 |
| [List 1](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_1 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 1") | 6 | 3 | 7 | Stocks 5 |
| [List 2](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_2 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 2") | 12 | 2 | 9 | Stocks 3 |
| [List 3](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_3 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 3") | 18 | 2 | 12 | Stocks 1 |
| [List 4](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_4 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 4") | 18 | 1 | 12 | Stocks 1 |

Most books sitting out on bookshelves or lying around are randomly-generated. They are usually generated from a list named LItemBookClutter, which represents a combination of lists 0-2 with equal chances, but without *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* from list 2. [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")* to it.

## Dragonborn Book Types

Standard books new with Dragonborn are placed into one of four lists ([1](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List_1 "Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List 1"), [2](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List_2 "Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List 2"), [3](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List_3 "Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List 3"), [4](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List_4 "Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List 4")). Most random books found in the open are either from one of those lists, or a combination of those lists and a list from the basegame with the same number. Randomly generated treasure uses an evenly weighted combination of all four lists and lists 2-4 from Skyrim. The books sold by [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor") are drawn from Dragonborn lists 1-4.

## Achievements

[Achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") related to books are:

-  **[Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:Reader "Skyrim:Reader")** (20 points/Bronze) — Read 50 [Skill Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books")

## Notes

- [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") is one of the few merchants who regularly sells books.

## Bugs

- When an NPC reads a book for an idle animation, pages the reader turns would go dark on one side before being flipped.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

Bor

**Bor** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who lives and works in [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur") at [Gloombound Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloombound_Mine "Skyrim:Gloombound Mine"). She spends her time mining the [ebony ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore") there.

Like her fellow workers, Bor spends all her time inside Gloombound Mine, mining the ore inside. She may occasionally stop to relax, drink, or eat.

Bor wears a set of [ragged robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Robes "Skyrim:Ragged Robes") along with a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Boots "Skyrim:Ragged Boots"). She wields a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") which can be up to [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish") in quality and carries a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe").

## Dialogue

:   *"I'm here to mine, outlander. So unless you want to dig, get out."*
:   *"I have metal to dig."*
:   *"Malacath has given me the task to mine. Good ore brings strength to our people."*
:   *"Every Orc learns the heavy labor of mining. All spend years in the caves."*
:   *"The mines are hard, but Malacath rewards those who rise to the challenge."*

Borgakh the Steel Heart

**Borgakh the Steel Heart** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardOrc1H "Skyrim:GuardOrc1H") and potential [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") found in [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur"). During the day, she can be found using the training dummy in front of [Larak's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Larak's Longhouse"), and at night, sleeping inside. Although she is proud of Orc traditions and willing to abide by them, she seems uneasy about what her future may hold.

She wears [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Armor_2 "Skyrim:Armor"), including [heavy boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots_2 "Skyrim:Armor") and [heavy gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Gauntlets_2 "Skyrim:Armor"), and she keeps a set of [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers") for sleeping. She carries a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Shields_2 "Skyrim:Armor"), a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") with 20 [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrow "Skyrim:Arrow"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Key to Larak's Longhouse") to the longhouse, and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). Her armor and weapons are leveled, and can be up to [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish") in quality.

## Related Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Dialogue

Her greetings:

:   *"I envy you, outlander. You can choose to leave if you wish."*
:   *"Soon, I will be of age. The taste is bitter."*
:   *"Perhaps I'll join the Legion one day, as my father had done."*

When spoken to:

:   **What do you do for the stronghold?**
:   *"I am [Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak")'s daughter. Soon, I'll be of age and will be sent to marry an Orc chief in some distant stronghold. Until then, I train. My new home will need strength, and my new sisters will know I'm not weak when I arrive."*

:   **You don't know who you'll marry?**
:   *"No. A chief's daughter marries who her chief wishes. It ensures the stronghold receives a fair trade in goods for my absence. I used to look forward to the day when I was of age, to see new places and people, but now it feels like a cage."*

:   **You want to leave the stronghold?**
:   *"I couldn't. It would shame my chief, and mother, and foremothers."*

| Option | Dialogue | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| They'll understand. Trust me.  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: You're right. [Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:Malacath "Skyrim:Malacath") teaches us to meet our fate. Perhaps this is mine. **Failed**: What do you know about my people, outlander? | | | |
| What if I pay off your dowry?  **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: That is a fine idea. The stronghold would need the gold when I am ready to marry anyway. **Failed**: No. That won't be enough. | | | |
| You're weak.  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: I am not weak. Very well, outlander, I will go with you whenever you are ready.  **Failed**: You dare challenge a child of Malacath? | | | |
| Fine, then. | Thank you for asking. | | | |

If you are successful, she becomes a potential [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), as well as a candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage"), and can be recruited into the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Unused Dialogue

The game's DialogueViews files include an early iteration of her response to you persuading her. Said line notably includes the term **Mauloch**, instead of Malacath. Both names are in use by the Daedric Prince, but Malacath is much more prominently used:

:   *"You're right. Mauloch teaches us to meet our fate. Perhaps this is mine."*

## Notes

- Once she is following you, you can simply take back the gold you gave her for the dowry if you are in need of it.

## Bugs

- When married, she lacks most of the store dialogue, leaving it unvoiced.
- If you marry Borgakh and [adopt](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") a [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), she cannot be asked how the children are doing as she has no recorded dialogue for it.
- Borgakh's confidence level is so high, you cannot intimidate her no matter how high your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill is.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Her class, `GuardOrc1H` incorrectly levels her Magicka instead of Stamina.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 2.3.1, addresses this issue. Changing it to level her and other Orc Warriors' Stamina rather than Magicka.

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Level | 6 | Class | [Miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") |

| Voice Type | [MaleEvenTonedAccented](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenTonedAccented "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenTonedAccented") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionPale](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionPale "Skyrim:CrimeFactionPale"); [DawnstarQuicksilverMinerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DawnstarQuicksilverMinerFaction "Skyrim:DawnstarQuicksilverMinerFaction"); [TownDawnstarFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownDawnstarFaction "Skyrim:TownDawnstarFaction") | | |

Borgny mining in Quicksilver Mine in Dawnstar

Borgny is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)"), and one of the many people who work in [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

He works inside the mine around the clock and never even sees the light of day. Occasionally, he sits down on one of the available chairs and rests. He never pauses to eat or sleep.

He wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"), and is equipped with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). He carries a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

Borgny will only ever speak about work if spoken to.

:   *"Plenty of iron to dig."*

:   *"Mining's an honest trade. No real tricks to it."*

## Bugs

- He speaks about digging iron, even though he works in Quicksilver Mine.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Borkul the Beast

## Overview

| Borkul the Beast (RefID: 00019915) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | | |
| Location | [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), then [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") | | |

Borkul the Beast

**Borkul the Beast** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardOrc1H "Skyrim:GuardOrc1H") who is found inside [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"). He is considered to be the toughest prisoner in the mine and guards the door leading to [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach"). During [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine"), you need to convince him to let you pass in order to gain your freedom.

Once outside the city, he will run all the way to [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") where he will start his life anew as part of the Forsworn. He will now spend his time either patrolling the path by the river, or wandering around inside the cave, occasionally eating, relaxing, or sleeping. His only dialogue at this point will be about him refusing naming you as [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the Orcs.

He is only armed with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and wears [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers") and a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets").

## Related Quests

- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!

### No One Escapes Cidhna Mine

When first encountered, he will not leave his spot near the door, though he is quite talkative. When you approach him he will say:

:   *"The new meat. So soft. Tender. What was it like killing your first one, huh?"*

| Option | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **Exciting. I felt the rush of blood... and smiled.** | *"A true killer, like me. The gods put us here to fill their halls with souls. You'll fit in fine down here."* |
| **Horrible. My soul is heavy with guilt.** | *"Pah. The gods have a place for killers. You can't carry the burden? You're weak."* |
| **I'm not a murderer.** | *"Liar."* |

You will then get the option to ask him a couple of simple questions:

:   **What are you in for?**
:   *"Murder. Banditry. Assault. Theft. And lollygagging."*
:   **How long have you been here?**
:   *"Guards brought me in about 12 years ago. Was running a good group of bandits up until then. But these Forsworn. They're nothing like the men I cobbled together. They're real killers."*

This conversation will also unlock some new greeting when he sees you:

:   *"You serve your time by digging. So dig."*
:   *"Prison's not so bad. Less complaints when I kill people."*

There will be no further dialogue options until you have spoken to fellow prisoner [Uraccen](/wiki/Skyrim:Uraccen "Skyrim:Uraccen") about Madanach.

When you return to Borkul you can ask him to see Madanach:

:   **I need to see Madanach.**
:   *"You want to talk to the King in Rags? Fine. But first you got to pay the toll. How about you get me a shiv? Not that I need one, but it's nice to have in case I need to do some "shaving." Ha ha."*

This opens five different dialogue options, with five different outcomes:

**NOTE**: Please see the [related quest page](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") or the [shiv page](/wiki/Skyrim:Shiv "Skyrim:Shiv") for information on how to get the dialogue.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I don't have a shiv. | *"Then find one. That dung heap [Grisvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Grisvar_the_Unlucky "Skyrim:Grisvar the Unlucky")'s been known to make a few."* | | | | Find a shiv |
| Here's your shiv. | *"All right, head on in. But don't try anything in there. Madanach is smarter than you think."* | | | | Pass the door |
| Madanach is expecting me. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"Hmph. Fine. Go on in. But don't try anything in there. Madanach knows more than you think."* **Failed**: *"The only thing Madanach expects is a bottle of Skooma in tribute every so often. You're not getting through."* | | | | **Passed**: Pass the door **Failed**: Nothing |
| How about some skooma instead? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: *"Ah, now that's a good idea. Head on in. But don't try anything in there. Madanach is smarter than you think."* | | | | **Passed**: Pass the door |
| Let me through, pig-face. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: *"Those eyes. All right, killer, go on through. But don't try anything. Madanach knows more than you think."* **Failed**: *"That's what I was hoping you'd say."* | | | | **Passed**: Pass the door **Failed**: Turn hostile |
| How about I fight you for it? **(Brawl)** | **Brawl**: (Start a brawl)  - **Victory**: *"It's been so long since I tasted my own blood. Sour."*   - **You'll let me through now?**   - *"Yeah, yeah. Go on in."* - **Failure**: (Nothing) | | | | Brawl |
| I'll pay the toll later. | *"That's right. Turn around and leave."* | | | | Nothing |

After he lets you in, he will wait by the door until you prove your loyalty to the King in Rags. When you follow Madanach out to the main chamber, Borkul will stand in the crowd and listen to the speech and shout:

:   *"The Reach belongs to the Forsworn!"*

He will then run through the secret tunnel with the rest of the Forsworn and enter [Markarth Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Ruins "Skyrim:Markarth Ruins"), saying nothing except:

:   *"Get going."*

Once outside, he will don a full set of [Forsworn Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Armor "Skyrim:Forsworn Armor") and fight for his freedom like everyone else, battling his way through the city towards the gates.

## Notes

- Borkul is the only member of the Forsworn that isn't a Breton/Reachman.
- Borkul will always call you a liar if you tell him you're not a murderer, even if that's the truth.

## Bugs

- Borkul's sleep package is blocked by his other Cidhna Mine packages.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- During No One Escapes Cidhna Mine, it is impossible to intimidate Borkul, due to the confidence level bug.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, addresses this issue. His confidence value has been lowered one notch to "Brave" instead of "Foolhardy".
- When you try to brawl with Borkul, he may equip his pickaxe during the fight.

## Overview

Borri

**Borri**, an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest"), is one of the reclusive [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") in [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar") who refuses to speak, lest a mere whisper of their voice unleashes destruction. Borri teaches you a word of the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout "Skyrim:Shout") during [The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice"). He will react when interacted with, greeting you with a muttered "Dovahkiin" and causing the surroundings to rumble in doing so.

Borri wears a set of [Greybeard's robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Greybeard's Robes") with the matching [hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Hood "Skyrim:Greybeard's Hood") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Boots "Skyrim:Greybeard's Boots"). He carries a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), one sample of [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), an [amulet of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Talos "Skyrim:Amulet of Talos"), and one sample of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries").

He will start his day at 4am, rising from bed to meditate inside facing the windows, on the mats, changing to a different window each hour. At 12:30pm, he will meditate in the courtyard, as well as in the courtyard tower, occasionally using the [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") shout while up there. At 4:30pm he will meditate in front of the shrine in the main entry hall, and at 8pm he will meditate in the main entry hall, rotating positions in a clockwise direction every hour until retiring to his sleeping quarters at 12:30am to read; finally retiring to bed at 2am. He will then sleep for two hours and repeat his daily routine.

Borri knows the following shouts: [Disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarm "Skyrim:Disarm"), [Dismay](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismay "Skyrim:Dismay"), [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury"), [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath"), [Frost Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath"), [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form"), [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), and [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint").

Aside from his greeting to you, the only other word ever heard by Borri is the shout *"Bex!"* during the quest The Way of the Voice. The shout in English means *open*.

## Related Quests

- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").
- **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
- **[The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World")**: Receive a lesson from [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").
- **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)")**: Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").

## Notes

- Borri is one of only two NPCs in Skyrim that are level 100, the other NPC being the Greybeard [Wulfgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulfgar "Skyrim:Wulfgar").

# Skyrim:Borvir

## Overview

| Borvir (RefID: 000D5048) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Journeyman's Nook](/wiki/Skyrim:Journeyman%27s_Nook "Skyrim:Journeyman's Nook") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000D5048 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00013BC2 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| Voice Type | [MaleEvenTonedAccented](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenTonedAccented "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenTonedAccented") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Frost River Farm Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_River_Farm_Faction "Skyrim:Frost River Farm Faction") | | |

Borvir's corpse

**Borvir** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") mage found dead at [Journeyman's Nook](/wiki/Skyrim:Journeyman%27s_Nook "Skyrim:Journeyman's Nook"), killed by a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [Borvir's dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Borvir%27s_Dagger "Skyrim:Borvir's Dagger") can be found right next to his body, suggesting he tried to defend himself. He has been killed by three arrows piercing his back. If you carefully search the room, you can find a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbalist%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim")* on a crate nearby as well as [Treasure Map II](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_II "Skyrim:Treasure Map II") inside the knapsack next to the door.

Borvir only has his clothes on him, a set of [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes"). His [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0006b46c "Skyrim:Boots") can be found next to a fire close to his corpse.

He and his twin brother [Rundi](/wiki/Skyrim:Rundi "Skyrim:Rundi") are mentioned by [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") as two of the missing apprentices from the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"): *"And then there's Borvir and Rundi. Twins, though they rarely agreed on anything. Those two boys were obsessed with mead. Convinced they could concoct something to compete with Honningbrew. Something about using frost magic to chill the mead for a certain period of time. I felt it was a waste, but the Arch-Mage let them proceed."*.

## Notes

- Borvir was to be included in two [unfinished quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"). In the first, you are tasked with finding him and the three other missing apprentices. In the quest, you bring [Borvir's Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Borvir%27s_Dagger "Skyrim:Borvir's Dagger") back to Phinis Gestor, who will say, *"Yes, I recognize it. Well, I suppose I needn't wonder where he is anymore."* In the second, he and his twin brother would open up a popular meadery in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), and you would be tasked with bringing their mead to either [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"), [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") or [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth").
- Similar to Rundi, Borvir still has a complete AI schedule present. Unlike Rundi, however, Borvir is also still part of the related Frost River Farm faction.
-  Version 3.0.6 of [The Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch") removes Borvir from the Frost River Farm Faction as a precaution. This update of the patch removes many crime factions that were leftover on corpse NPCs, as resurrecting and then re-killing them could net you bounties in holds that were completely removed from your current location. However, the faction in question is not a standard crime faction. Due to Borvir not being a part of any, crimes committed against him, even if registered, would technically not result in you getting a bounty.

## Bugs

- Borvir's dagger might clip beneath the floor, making it unreachable.
  -  You can access the dagger by using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `tcl` to move through the floor and find the dagger.

# Skyrim:Bothela's Discreet Delivery

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Deliver the [Stallion's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion") to [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") or [Reburrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela") |
| Location(s): | [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure") |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela")) |
| ID: | FreeformMarkarthJ |

Bothela inside The Hag's Cure

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Obtain the [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion") from [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela").
2. Go to [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") (or the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), see below).
3. Deliver the potion to [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") or [Reburrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius").

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela"), an elderly Breton alchemist, can be found in her shop, [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure"), located in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") just west of [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"). When asked about her shop, Bothela will say that the people of Markarth will often come to her, secretly, for cures. Bothela will go on to explain that she has [a potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion") for the Jarl's steward, which she asks you to deliver.

*"Still, a little knowledge of plants and potions can get you by. Not that anyone likes to admit buying things from you. See? I even have a little potion for the Steward. Mind handing it over to him? Just say it should solve that problem he has."*

After accepting this task, the Stallion's Potion will be placed in your inventory. If declined, however, selecting the initiating dialogue will prompt the conversation again, giving you another opportunity to accept the quest.

The steward can be found in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") (or the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") control the Reach and the potion is for Raerek). Approaching and informing him of Bothela's delivery will prompt this line from him:

*"Oh... yes... um... thank you. Here you go. Some gold for your assistance and your, discretion."*

After speaking with him, the Stallion's Potion will be removed from your inventory and Raerek will reward you with a leveled amount of gold. Bothela does not give you a reward, unless a friendly disposition counts.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- In most cases, Raerek will be the target of this quest. But it is possible, although highly unusual, to be directed to [Reburrus Quintilius](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius") once he's the steward. In order to do so, however, you must have handed The Reach over to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") without ever having entered Markarth or the immediate vicinity. If you've already entered the area around Markarth, Bothela will still refer to Raerek as the steward and expect you to deliver the potion to him. Note that [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)") forces you to enter Markarth to talk to Raerek, so Season Unending is the only way to get Reburrus.

## Bugs

- If spoken to during the quest, Reburrus' dialogue has no actual audio.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=15612)) A line variant for Reburrus didn't exist and has been spliced from other pre-existing lines.
- The Stallion's Potion is marked as stolen when it is in your inventory, which means if you get arrested and decide to pay off your bounty or go to jail, it will disappear from your inventory and the quest will get stuck unless you steal it back from the evidence chest in the hold's jail.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=17520))
  - For best results if you don't have the patch installed, make sure you don't have a bounty in the Reach and deliver the potion to Raerek as soon as you get it.
- Bothela still targets Raerek even if the quest is started only after the Stormcloaks take over.

  **Mod Notes**: The quest is started invisibly and aliases filled upon entering the Markarth region and the target never gets updated after that.
- You can complete the quest by giving the potion to [Reburrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius"), even if he isn't the current steward and target of the quest.
- Completing this quest may allow you to freely take things from [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House"), [Erikur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House"), the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines"), and [Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon") due to improper ownership settings. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Bothela's Discreet Delivery (FreeformMarkarthJ) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Deliver the Stallion's Potion to <Alias.ShortName=Steward> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformMarkarthJ stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformMarkarthJ`.

# Skyrim:Bothela

## Overview

| Bothela (RefID: 000198F7) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | | |

Bothela in her store

**Bothela** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:VendorApothecary "Skyrim:VendorApothecary") merchant who lives in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). She owns and runs [the Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure") with her assistant and friend [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri"). She expresses regret at the situation of the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [Odvan](/wiki/Skyrim:Odvan "Skyrim:Odvan") in [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine") is her grandson.

Bothela begins her day at 8am when she gets out of her bed to open her shop. She will spend her entire day inside her shop handling customers. After twelve hours of work, she will lock up the shop for the night and head to bed. She will wake up at 8am to repeat her schedule.

Bothela wears [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_the_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:Key to the Hag's Cure") to the Hag's Cure and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She knows a few spells from various schools. From the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") school she knows [Conjure Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar"); from the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") school she knows [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"); she can use the spell [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") from the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") school.

## Related Quests

- **[Bothela's Discreet Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela%27s_Discreet_Delivery "Skyrim:Bothela's Discreet Delivery")**: Deliver the [Stallion's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion") to [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") or [Reburrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius").
- **[Further Study](/wiki/Skyrim:Further_Study "Skyrim:Further Study")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Collect a fish to help an alchemist experiment with potions. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

Approaching Bothela while her shop is open will have her greet you in a number of ways:

:   *"The Hag's Cure is here for all your discreet needs..."*
:   *"I have potions for disease, love sickness, irritating children..."*
:   *"A little bit of old Reach magic can cure whatever ills*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *you...."*
:   *"Oh yes... you'll need one of my special brews..."*
:   *"Not scared of an old woman now, are you?"*

On ending a conversation with Bothela, she will offer two unique remarks:

:   *"Now you let me know if you need a cure... or anything else."*
:   *"I have herbs to mix."*

When spoken to directly:

:   **What's your opinion on Markarth?**
:   *"We'd be better off without the Silver-Bloods. They send their brute, [Yngvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvar_the_Singer "Skyrim:Yngvar the Singer"), to shake some coins from me every few days. And [Betrid Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Betrid_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Betrid Silver-Blood") is always asking for more potions to fuel [Thonar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood")'s 'ambitions.' Gives him a temper fiercer than any bear."*

:   **What do you know about the Forsworn?**
:   *"Only that they break an old woman's heart. So many friends, so many kin, all lost trying to rebuild a past that was over long ago."*

### Bothela's Discreet Delivery

Asking her about her shop's unique name will have her offer you a job to [deliver a potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela%27s_Discreet_Delivery "Skyrim:Bothela's Discreet Delivery"):

:   **The "Hag's Cure." That's a unique name.**
:   *"Comes with living to a ripe old age, people start thinking there's something magical about you. Then, the insults. Still, a little knowledge of plants and potions can get you by. Not that anyone likes to admit buying things from you. See? I even have a little [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion") for the [Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek"). Mind handing it over to him? Just say it should solve that problem he has."*

:   :   **I'll make sure he gets it.**
    :   *"Thank you."*

:   :   **I don't have time right now.**
    :   *"Pity."*

Should you initially deny the request, asking her about her shop again will provide you with another chance to take it.

## Unused Dialogue

Bothela has unused dialogue tied to multiple [quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests") she was once meant to partake in. This dialogue can only be found in the game's DialogueViews files, and not the Creation Kit.

### FreeformMarkarthI

In this quest, you would've been sent by [Uaile](/wiki/Skyrim:Uaile "Skyrim:Uaile") to pick up a potion for [Nepos the Nose](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos_the_Nose "Skyrim:Nepos the Nose").

:   **I'm here for Uaile's potion.**
:   *"Ah, yes. Clever way of keeping that lecher's hands away from her. But you didn't hear that from me."*

This reply from Bothela would be your first hint as to Uaile and Nepos' real relationship.

### FreeformMarkarthM2

This quest, despite its name, is actually related to The Forsworn Conspiracy. Originally, [Eltrys](/wiki/Skyrim:Eltrys "Skyrim:Eltrys") was meant to give you the names of three people he suspected of having Forsworn ties, and [Nana Ildene](/wiki/Skyrim:Nana_Ildene "Skyrim:Nana Ildene") would be among them. If you went to investigate Ildene, you would come across her switching notes with Bothela. Afterward, you could confront Bothela about this:

:   **What were you and Ildene talking about?**
:   *"That's between two old women to know. Stay out of business that isn't yours."* (Failed)
:   *"My nephew Odvan is in Cihna Mine. I've promised to pass along her notes if she promises the Forsworn help him get out. Look at me, almost 80 and still playing these games. I don't even know who's involved anymore, really. So many dead drops and messengers just to get so much as a note out."*

:   **I need that note, Bothela. The Forsworn have to be stopped.**
:   *"You won't stop them, dear, but if it'll make you feel better. Here. It's yours."*

The contents of this note are unknown.

## Conversations

Bothela and Muiri speaking at their shop

Bothela can be seen having random conversations with Muiri which show her concern and care for her:

:   **Bothela**: *"No, no girl. It's the pickled spider tongue and then the decayed taproot. Do it the other way, and your cure turns into a poison."*
:   **Muiri**: *"There's just so much to memorize. How am I supposed to remember what goes where for every single herb?"*
:   **Bothela**: *"You will. Until then, you'll taste every potion you make before you sell it."*

:   **Bothela**: *"You should be more careful with the men you pick, dear."*
:   **Muiri**: *"He said he loved me..."*
:   **Bothela**: *"Real men prove their love. Words are as empty as the air they run through."*

:   **Bothela**: *"Stop moping about, girl. Tears won't change what you've done."*
:   **Muiri**: *"I was such a fool. How could I let him use me like that?"*
:   **Bothela**: *"We all get used, dear. It's living with it that makes you a woman."*

:   **Muiri**: *"Bothela, I have a question...."*
:   **Bothela**: *"You want to know a secret of mine, young girl? The most effective poison to kill a man? A potion to make others fall in love, perhaps?"*
:   **Muiri**: *"I was actually just wondering if you had any family...."*
:   **Bothela**: *"Oh. Oh, I see...."*
:   **Muiri**: *"I'm sorry. You don't have to tell me if you don't...."*
:   **Bothela**: *"I have one. A nephew. He's in prison for being a member of the Forsworn."*
:   **Muiri**: *"I'm sorry, I didn't realize."*
:   **Bothela**: *"Don't be. We all make mistakes."*

## Rumors

Her grandson Odvan will voice a thought about his grandmother:

:   *"I wonder how grandma Bothela is doing. She's probably worried sick about me."*

The [Markarth City Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_City_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth City Guard") will also talk about her abilities as a healer:

:   *"Caught a case of [Rockjoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockjoint "Skyrim:Rockjoint"), once. Bothela at the Hag's Cure fixed me right up."*

If Bothela is killed, Muiri will take over the Hag's Cure and will occasionally make a comment about her late employer:

:   *"I've taken over the Hag's Cure, since Bothela is gone."*
:   *"I wish Bothela was still running the store. I'm not ready for this."*

## Notes

- Bothela has a face tattoo that's normally only seen on members of the Forsworn (it's also unavailable to you in character creation). She and Eltrys are the only named NPCs with this trait, yet neither person's tattoo will ever get addressed.
- There is some confusion about her relationship to Odvan. In all of Bothela's dialogue, she refers to him as her nephew. But in Odvan's dialogue, he once refers to her as his grandma and once implies her to be his aunt. Meanwhile, their relationship data has them set up as grandchild and grandparent, adding confusion.

## Bugs

- Bothela's corpse will never disappear.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Bothela doesn't sleep properly due to a missing package.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- Completing Bothela's delivery quest may allow you freely to take things from [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House"), [Erikur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House"), the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines"), and [Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon") due to improper ownership settings. **?**

# Skyrim:Boti

## Overview

| Boti (RefID: 00019E05) | | | |

| Level | 6 | Class | [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") |

Boti

**Boti** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") who lives at [Fellstar Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm") in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), together with her husband [Jofthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Jofthor "Skyrim:Jofthor") and daughter [Fastred](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastred "Skyrim:Fastred"). She and her husband keep a close eye on Fastred, being with her nearly all day. Arguments frequently arise in the family concerning Fastred's future, in which Boti tries to persuade her husband to give Fastred the freedom she wants. During [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love"), she will help you unite her daughter with [Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius").

She wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a5 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and has a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0001b1ea "Skyrim:Clothing") for sleepwear (though she won't wear it). She is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm_Key "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm Key") to the farmhouse, as well as a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She and the family wake up early at 6am in the morning to have breakfast for an hour. They will go out to work at the farm for a good 8 hours, when she can be found raking the ground or picking the harvest. She'll go back inside with her family to have an early dinner at 3pm. An hour later, she'll spend the next 7 hours watching over the house, which is when she may take the opportunity to eat or take a nap. At 11pm, she rejoins her family at the farm for a quick check before heading to bed at 12am. At any time of the day (unless you're trespassing), she will buy all [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and/or [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") you've gathered.

## Related Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

Her greetings:

:   *"You must be another pilgrim on the way up to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"). No other reason to pass through here."*
:   *"You better not be here to stir up any trouble."*
:   *"Pilgrim or not, if I were you, I'd move right through our backwards little town."*
:   *"And to think that we've been supplying the Greybeards with our own food supplies. What have they ever done for us?"*
:   *"I hope Fastred's doing well in Riften. I miss her."* **(Told Bassianus to take Fastred to Riften)**

If spoken to:

:   **Anything you can tell me about High Hrothgar?**
:   *"It's frightening living below their monastery. Sometimes I swear I can hear strange noises rolling down from up there. It sounds like thunder, but there's never any rain. What do you make of that?"*

When exiting conversation:

:   *"Sure, leave. Everyone else does."*

### Conversations

*"You have to let Fastred follow her heart."*

*"While you're under our roof, I need you to pitch in a little more."*

She can often be found talking to either her husband or her daughter. As Jofthor berates their daughter for straying too far away from the farm to talk with strangers, Boti is most likely closeby and able to hear the conversation. Regularly, she will confront her husband concerning his attitude towards their daughter:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Boti**: | *"You have to let Fastred follow her heart. You can't tell her what to do."* |
| **Jofthor**: | *"She's our only child, Boti. Am I to throw her to the wolves?"* |
| **Boti**: | *"You're hardly throwing her to the wolves. She just wants to see the world... just like I did when I was her age."* |
| **Jofthor**: | *"And if she decides to leave Ivarstead, what then? No, no... I can't bear the thought."* |

In turn, she will ask her daughter to focus on working on the farm, likely to keep her distracted and productive:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Boti**: | *"I need you to pitch in a little more around here, dear."* |
| **Fastred**: | *"I help, I do the chores. What else would you have me do?"* |
| **Boti**: | *"I know your sights are set beyond this town, but for now, while you're under our roof, I need you to pitch in a little more."* |
| **Fastred**: | *"Yes, mother."* |

## Quest-Related Events

It is during [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love"), when you're sent to unite Fastred with her love, that you'll put an end to the drama. When Fastred asks you to speak to her mother, you can tell Boti about it:

:   **Your daughter asked me to speak to you.**
:   *"Oh my. Probably something about the men. We all wish we had her problems. Now, don't tell my husband, but I don't have any problem with Bassianus. Even if it means her leaving Ivarstead, I want Fastred to be happy. If they just snuck out of town together, I could manage my husband."*
:   **What would inspire them to leave?**
:   *"Bassianus is still so terrified of Jofthor. If he knew that I'd keep him from hunting the poor boy down, he'd take Fastred to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") without a second thought. Let him know that I'll watch out for them. I just want my daughter to be happy."*

## Notes

- During [Hunt and Gather](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunt_and_Gather "Skyrim:Hunt and Gather"), Riften court wizard [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah") reveals she's good friends with Boti: *"Last time I used the Dwemer Spoon was at my dear friend Boti's house in Ivarstead... Fellstar Farm I believe it's called."*

Bottar

**Bottar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who can be [encountered randomly](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Dwemer_Junk_Peddlers "Skyrim:World Interactions") out in the wilds. He wears green colored [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Shoes"). He is accompanied by his friend [Sond](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(child) "Skyrim:Sond (child)"), who will sell you a waypoint to [Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing") for one septim.

# Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Boulderfall Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Boulderfall+Cave)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbalist%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim")* | |

| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |
