Boulderfall Cave

**Boulderfall Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). It contains only one zone, *[Boulderfall Cave](#Boulderfall_Cave)*.

Alchemy laboratory

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The cave is fairly remote in the wilderness. There is a small game trail that runs north-southeast near the cave, and a path leads from this to the entrance that is marked with several piles of rocks. Above the entrance is a flag post with a flag fluttering in the breeze. By the base is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"); these may have been knocked off and be found on the ground beneath the flag. A few paces to the northwest of the flag, nestled among the rocks is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with a corpse beside it. There is a leveled, hostile necromancer near the entrance that acts as the apprentice for the master within. He may be found sitting on the rock by the flag post above the entrance, and may raise the corpse to help with the fight upon detecting you.

### Boulderfall Cave

The entrance leads into a tunnel descending to the southwest with two barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") on the left where it opens onto some wooden scaffolding at the entrance to a small chamber. Be careful, as there are three sets of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") lining the passageway to navigate, and avoiding setting one of these off can be quite a challenge. Any noise will alert the necromancer that is toiling away at an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") in the chamber. The necromancer will be of the highest level possible for your level, and will immediately attack if alerted to your presence. Once past the bone chimes, there is a ramp that descends to the cave floor. Two patches of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus can be found growing in the chamber.

There is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") on the northeast wall, to the right of the ramp. Against the north wall is a wooden table with three whole [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") and five [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks on top and barrels on either side, one of which contains [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), and the other ingredients. To the left are a stack of three open crates holding [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), with more on the ground in front. Beside these are two baskets, one containing [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and the other [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). More barrels are to the left, with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on one of them and a pile of firewood and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") beside them. Behind the firewood is a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") on the ground, which presumably has fallen from one of the five racks hanging from the ceiling above. These hold a further three pheasants and seven [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). Finally, against this wall is a novice-trapped chest.

At the rear of the chamber on a low platform is an alchemy lab with a bucket containing five bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") beside it. Along the wall to the right is a set of shelves with three baskets around; one of these holds potatoes, another many bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), and the third three [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). The shelves hold three bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a bottle of wine, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), three bottles of Nord mead, a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbalist%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim")*, a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). To the left of the platform is another table with three more bottles of Nord mead on top and an open crate containing two more cabbages underneath.

## Notes

- Several internal game data references suggest Boulderfall Cave was originally the site of the quest [The Savior of Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Savior_of_Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:The Savior of Selveni Nethri"), which was ultimately moved to [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") in the final game.
- Some internal game data refers to the location as "Boulderfall Pass".
- Boulderfall Cave also appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as [Boulderfall Pass](/wiki/Online:Boulderfall_Pass "Online:Boulderfall Pass").

## Maps

- 

  Boulderfall Cave

The Bouncer

The **Bouncer** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") guarding [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern"). He must be killed to complete [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand").

## Related Quests

- **[Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand")**: Clear [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

## Dialogue

Upon seeing you, he will draw his weapon and warn you away, saying:

:   *"These fights are invite only. And you're not invited. Slag off."*

He will attack if you approach too closely.

## Notes

- Before version 1.9 of the [Official Skyrim patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch#Version_1.9 "Skyrim:Patch") the bouncer was simply named 'Bandit'.
- Another bouncer can be found during a random encounter finding a dead body near two dead pit wolves. A [small note](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Note "Skyrim:Small Note") can be found on this dead bouncer which leads to [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern").

## Bugs

- In Patch 1.9, he displays no name and cannot be looted.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- The bouncer may unexpectedly disappear from the area. **?**

  **Mod Notes**: See talk page.

  - Travel away from the area and then back again and he should reappear.

# Skyrim:Bound Until Death

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Assassinate [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") at her own wedding.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") |
| Location(s): | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") |
| Reward: | [Summon Spectral Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Spectral_Assassin "Skyrim:Summon Spectral Assassin"), leveled gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =-2 ([Asgeir Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Asgeir Snow-Shod")) |
| ID: | DB05 |
| Difficulty: | Hard |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken") | **Next →** [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken") | | → Next | [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security") | | |

Vittoria Vici addresses her guests in Solitude

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Attend the wedding at the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
2. Assassinate [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici"). For a bonus, kill her during her speech.
3. Return to [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid").

### Let the Festivities Begin

Vittoria and Asgeir at the wedding

After the [Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken") quest, the first part of the Dark Brotherhood's biggest contract is set in motion. At Astrid's behest, travel to the courtyard of the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Here you will find the small wedding reception you were directed to attend. Your target is the bride, [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici"). If you approach Vittoria before she addresses the reception, she will exclaim: *"What an amazing day this has been. I hope you're enjoying the festivities. I'm... I'm just so overwhelmed. Such kindness... for me."*
You can choose one of three dialogue options in response:

:   **The Stormcloaks say hello!**
:   *"Oh! Well, you tell your Stormcloak friends "hello" right back at them! This is a day of healing! Legion, Stormcloaks - all are welcome here!"*
:   **Hail the Imperial Legion!**
:   *"Ha ha ha ha! Yes, yes indeed! Hail the Imperial Legion! Hail the Stormcloaks! Hail Solitude and the Eight Divines! On this glorious day, we honor everyone! Ha ha ha ha!"*
:   **(Remain silent)**
:   *"Oh, no need to be shy! My day is your day! Please - eat, drink, make merry! We're all friends here!"*

During the reception, she will also tell the guests: *"Please, enjoy the festivities! This is a day of peace and happiness, when Imperials and Stormcloaks join together, as equals!"* or *"Please, enjoy yourself!"* She will then stand up with her fiancé, [Asgeir Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Asgeir Snow-Shod"), and enter a door to reach the balcony, where she will begin addressing her guests. Assassinate her while she speaks to earn the bonus reward. There are several ways you can choose to accomplish the goal (see [this section](#Strategies) for more details).

#### Strategies

A loose gargoyle hanging over the balcony

A sniping spot opposite the balcony

There are many strategies you can use to kill Vittoria at her wedding. If you chose to speak to some of your fellow family members, they will give you advice on ways to kill her and what may happen afterwards:

- If you speak to [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette"), she will tell you about a loose gargoyle statue above the balcony: *"It's no fair. I love weddings. [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") should have given this contract to me. Instead, she's got me visiting cities, assessing security. How boring. But listen, I think I can help you. The wedding reception is outside the Temple of the Divines, right? In Solitude? If so, the bride will probably address the crowd from the balcony. It overlooks the courtyard. Well, there's an old statue there. I've seen it. Hanging right over where she'll be standing. Old means weak. Weak means it could fall. Hmmm?"* If you travel to the wall above the balcony, you can push a loose gargoyle statue when Vittoria makes her address to the wedding guests. To access this balcony, enter the Temple of the Divines, then go up the stairs to the right and through the door at the end of the corridor. You can also access this balcony by going up the stairs located to the right of [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour"). The gargoyle is there whether you talk to Babette or not.
- If you speak to [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella"), she will tell you: *"I hope you don't mind, but I took the liberty of surveying the site of the reception. There's a small parapet, just opposite the balcony, that would prove an excellent spot for a long-range kill. I left something there for you. If you're inclined to take that approach."* If you take the door to the northwest of the temple entrance, you will end up on a ledge located opposite the balcony where Vittoria addresses the reception. On the ledge are six arrows, an [Elixir of True Shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Elixir of True Shot"), and the unique magical bow [Firiniel's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Firiniel%27s_End "Skyrim:Firiniel's End"). You can simply shoot the bride from this spot; she is easily killed with a single sneak attack from the magic bow you are given. It is best to use these free items now to be sure she is killed immediately. This is especially important if you have a low [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skill and are planning a ranged attack. Like the gargoyle, the bow is there even if you haven't talked to Gabriella.
- [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") will warn you about the possible outcome of murdering Vittoria: *"Slaughtering the Emperor's cousin? At her wedding? Those guards will be out for blood. Wouldn't surprise me if the crowd jumped in too."*
- [Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara") will advise you to plan your escape route beforehand: *"Your contract sounds simple, which means it certainly will not be. Getting into that reception will be easy, but have you thought about getting out?"*

Other strategies for killing Vittoria include the following:

- Pickpocket a [Frenzy](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(effect) "Skyrim:Frenzy (effect)") poison into [the groom](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Asgeir Snow-Shod")'s inventory as Vittoria addresses the crowd. He will immediately drink it, turn, and kill her, provided that the poison is of sufficient strength. Casting a spell of Frenzy will achieve the same effect, though the [Quiet Casting](/wiki/Skyrim:Quiet_Casting "Skyrim:Quiet Casting") perk may be needed to avoid detection. To kill with a particular poison, you will need a poison of better than Weak strength and the [Poisoned](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisoned "Skyrim:Poisoned") perk.
- Turn into a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") or a [vampire lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") (without being seen and therefore incurring no bounty), and then use the door to the overhead balcony where she is located and kill her. A good spot to transform while Vittoria is speaking is the small nook behind the loose gargoyle. By crouching (sneaking) inside this nook, you can avoid incurring a bounty for transforming, and you can swiftly jump down on the bride before the crowd notices what's happening.
- Follow the happy couple to the balcony where the bride gives her speech. If you crouch down behind the couple you will not be seen by them or the guests. You can kill the bride and, by killing the groom as your last witness, you will get rid of the bounty as both are joined in death.
- Drop onto the balcony, crouch, and use Unrelenting Force.
- Purchase an invisibility potion and use it when killing Vittoria, guards shouldn't know that you did it.

### 'Til Death Do Us Part

Veezara coming to your aid

Once Vittoria is killed, pandemonium will break loose. Veezara will then appear, sent by Astrid to offer a distraction while you escape. Even if you weren't detected and got away with the assassination undiscovered, Veezara will still charge in and initiate combat with everyone, drawing attention away from you so you can simply walk out. Sometimes, the guests will still give chase, in which case you can escape the city quickly by using a stairwell under the [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") tower bridge, near the market. One way of avoiding a bounty is to fast travel to the Sanctuary to collect your reward as soon as Vittoria is killed and before the guests turn hostile.

### Summoning a Legend of the Brotherhood

Upon your arrival back to the [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), Astrid will congratulate you on your success: *"With Vici's murder, you've started us down a path the Dark Brotherhood hasn't traveled in centuries. The assassination of an Emperor. And now, your reward. A [unique spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Spectral_Assassin "Skyrim:Summon Spectral Assassin") to summon a legend of the Dark Brotherhood. His soul serves us now in death, as his body once did in life"*. This spell will allow you to summon the powerful spirit of an assassin to fight by your side. If you fulfilled the bonus requirements, she will also say *"Ah, and of course, a bonus, for killing Vici while she addressed her guests, as instructed. Gold... simple and pure. Spend it as you will."*, and give you a leveled amount of gold. Astrid will then carry on: *"Now then. Time to proceed to the next stage of the plan. Go and speak with Gabriella. She's been helping me arrange your next contract."* When you approach her again, she will tell you: *"As I said, go speak with Gabriella. She's been assisting me with your next contract. This Emperor business, well... it does involve everyone."* The next quest, [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security"), will now begin.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **Bound Until Death** (10 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- Completion of this quest will make another minor [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:The Spiced Wine") unavailable, unless you completed that one first.
- Some of the guests at the wedding include [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"), [Alexia Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Alexia_Vici "Skyrim:Alexia Vici"), [Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod"), [Nura Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Nura_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Nura Snow-Shod"), [Vivienne Onis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis"), [Kayd](/wiki/Skyrim:Kayd "Skyrim:Kayd"), [Rorlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorlund "Skyrim:Rorlund"), [Pantea Ateia](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia"), [Lodi](/wiki/Skyrim:Lodi "Skyrim:Lodi"), [Noster Eagle-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Noster_Eagle-Eye "Skyrim:Noster Eagle-Eye"), and a [Penitus Oculatus agent](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Agent "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Agent").
- After Veezara appears, if you are not being pursued, you can talk to all of the wedding guests to hear their individual reactions to Vittoria's murder.
- Even if you are not detected when killing the bride, the guests will still turn hostile, and attacking them will incur a bounty. Raising and lowering arms will count as yielding and will not earn you a bounty.
- [Plautis Carvain](/wiki/Skyrim:Plautis_Carvain "Skyrim:Plautis Carvain") and [his wife](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Carvain "Skyrim:Salonia Carvain") can be found traveling in the wilderness during a random encounter, and claim to be heading towards the wedding, although they will never appear there and are not mentioned by any of the other guests. After completing the quest, you may once more run into Plautis and Salonia, where they explain that they were robbed by bandits and missed the wedding.
- Using an [Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(effect) "Skyrim:Invisibility (effect)") potion, power, or spell may help you avoid a bounty if it is used right after the murder, although the guards may still locate and attack you, causing the bounty to be incurred.
- Vittoria can be looted for her unique [wedding dress](/wiki/Skyrim:Wedding_Dress "Skyrim:Wedding Dress"), [wedding sandals](/wiki/Skyrim:Wedding_Sandals "Skyrim:Wedding Sandals"), [wedding wreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Wedding_Wreath "Skyrim:Wedding Wreath"), and [her wedding band](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria%27s_Wedding_Band "Skyrim:Vittoria's Wedding Band") before it disappears. If the body is gone, you can find Vittoria's remains in the [Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Catacombs "Skyrim:Solitude Catacombs"), in a coffin on the northeastern side of the longest tunnel.
- Killing Vittoria by casting a Frenzy spell at her can cause her to leave the balcony, which would cause your bonus to be forfeit as she is no longer considered "speaking to the guests".

## Bugs

- After the disastrous wedding, the northwestern entrance to the temple courtyard remains closed for the rest of the game. The wedding decorations and Penitus Oculatus guard also remain permanently.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=7300))
- Any of the guests can be moved to the courtyard once the wedding scene is set up, regardless of whether they're alive or not. If they have died at some point, then their emptied bodies will appear instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") and [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") are set to lose their essential status once this quest is done, but they both have other quests they're involved in. If Erikur is dead but [The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload") is not finished yet, the entire [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild "Skyrim:Thieves Guild") questline will halt. He will be resurrected if this has happened. If Bryling dies before [Payment Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Payment_Delivery "Skyrim:Payment Delivery") is finished, that quest will be marked as failed in your journal and shut down.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Lodi the bard may not be able to play his flute because his 3D doesn't enable fast enough for the bard song scripts to catch up. Also, the two wedding guests coming in from outside Solitude need to be manually checked to make sure they're not dead and then moved into the city. Their AI will not get them to Solitude in time if you head there shortly after getting the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=15112))
- Lodi may continue to play after Vittoria is killed, despite the vocal reaction he gives.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=16072))
- Once Vittoria is dead and you reach the *Report back to Astrid* quest stage, the quest marker may erroneously point you to the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") in Solitude. Once you enter the temple, the quest marker is updated to correctly point you to the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary").
- Dropping the gargoyle statue may make Vittoria's body clip inside the balcony, preventing her body from being easily looted.
- Astrid sometimes doesn't give you the bonus reward even if you killed Vittoria while she was on the balcony speaking. This may occur if you're using the loose gargoyle method or by assassinating her at night.
  -  This bug can be fixed by entering `setpqv DB05 Bonus_var 1` in the console after killing the target.
- Vittoria sometimes may not start her speech and will only get up and walk to the tower entrance, turn around and then sit back down repeatedly. **?**
  - Reloading the game may fix this.
- If you kill her via an arrow shot without being detected (invisibility and line of sight breaking cover), you can escape the town without Veezara appearing. In this case, you will be attacked by guards the next time you visit Solitude and walk by the courtyard. **?**
  - To avoid this, double back and trigger Veezara before leaving town.

## Quest Stages

| Bound Until Death (DB05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I must journey to the Temple of the Divines in Solitude, attend the public wedding reception of Vittoria Vici and Asgeir Snow-Shod, and kill the bride. I'll receive a bonus if I kill Vici as she addresses the crowd. *Objective 10:* Kill Vittoria Vici |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Report back to Astrid |
| 200 | ☑ | I have killed Vittoria Vici, the Emperor's cousin, at her own wedding, and everyone will assume it's related to the ongoing war. The Emperor will now be forced to visit Skyrim to deal with the aftermath, paving the way for his assassination. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB05`.

# Skyrim:Bounty: Bandit Boss

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Eliminate a bandit leader for a bounty reward.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Any innkeeper, Jarl or steward |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | 100 gold |
| ID: | BQ01 |

Time to pay your bounty.

## Radiant Options

Any innkeeper, Jarl, or hold steward can give you this quest. You will be directed to one of the possible locations that contain bandits in the same hold, and you will then need to obtain your reward from the Jarl or steward of the hold.

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |

"Skyrim:Embershard") [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge") | [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto") [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear") | [Orotheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Orotheim "Skyrim:Orotheim") [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") | [Frostmere Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp") [Redoran's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Redoran's Retreat") [Silent Moons Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Moons_Camp Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowpoint_Beacon "Skyrim:Snowpoint Beacon") [Winter War](/wiki/Skyrim:Winter_War "Skyrim:Winter War") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the bounty from an innkeeper, Jarl, or steward.
2. Kill the bandit leader at the given location.
3. Return to the Jarl or steward for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Asking an innkeeper, Jarl's steward, or Jarl about work may lead them to give you a [letter of bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(bandits) "Skyrim:Bounty (bandits)") for a bandit leader, found in a location in the hold you are in. Head to the location and kill the bandit leader. There may be multiple bandits at the location, but you only have to kill the marked leader to mark this objective as complete. Once the bandit is dead, return to the Jarl or Jarl's steward for your reward of 100 gold.

## Notes

- The "bandit leader" might be a standard low-level bandit.

## Bugs

- If the ruins are cleared out before the quest is given to kill the bandit leader, the ruins may not repopulate, causing this quest to not be completable.
  -  To fix this, approach the boss and open the console. After clicking on him, type `resurrect 1`. This will bring him back to life and allow you to complete the quest.
  -  Another fix is to open the console and type `setstage bq01 100`  (if started by the steward) or `setstage bq01 101` (if started by the Jarl). This will clear the bandit leader and point you to collect the bounty.

## Quest Stages

| Bounty: Bandit Boss (BQ01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill the bandit leader located at <Alias=BountyLocation> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Collect bounty from <Alias=Steward>  *Objective 101:* Collect bounty from <Alias=Jarl> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BQ01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BQ01`.

# Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Chezburgar](/wiki/User:Chezburgar "User:Chezburgar"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | 500 gold |
| ID: | BQ04 |
| Required Level: | 10 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") | | |

The [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(dragon) "Skyrim:Bounty (dragon)") for the dragon. The location will vary.

## Radiant Options

Any [innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns"), [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"), or [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") can give you this quest. You will be directed to one of the possible dragon lairs in the hold.

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest") | [Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent") | [Eldersblood Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldersblood_Peak "Skyrim:Eldersblood Peak") [Skyborn Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyborn_Altar "Skyrim:Skyborn Altar") | [Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint") | [Dragontooth Crater](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragontooth_Crater "Skyrim:Dragontooth Crater") | [Autumnwatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnwatch_Tower "Skyrim:Autumnwatch Tower") [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook") [Northwind Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Summit "Skyrim:Northwind Summit") | [Mount Anthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Anthor "Skyrim:Mount Anthor") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with an innkeeper, jarl, or steward to receive the bounty.
2. Kill the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") at the indicated location.
3. Speak with the jarl or steward of the hold to receive your reward.

### Here There Be Dragons

After your adventures at [Whiterun's](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") [Western Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Western_Watchtower "Skyrim:Western Watchtower") during [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), a proliferation of dragons are about. In your travels, ask an innkeep, jarl or steward for some work. You may learn that a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") has been harassing travelers and citizens around its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"), and the jarl of the hold has put out a bounty on the dragon. You are an enterprising sort, with newly acquired [dragon soul absorbing powers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin") and [shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), so take up the job.

### The Dragon Hunter

Seek out the offending dragon in its lair. There is a [wide variety of dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon#Abilities "Skyrim:Dragon") that you may encounter in each lair you visit. Once defeated, and the dragon soul is absorbed, be sure to remove the [dragon bones](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bone "Skyrim:Dragon Bone") and [dragon scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Scales "Skyrim:Dragon Scales"). These are quite valuable in the local shops, and can be used to make and improve [dragonbone and dragonscale armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Armor "Skyrim:Dragon Armor").

### The Bounty

Once the dragon is dead, you will be directed to the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") or [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") of the hold to receive your payment.

## Notes

- If you are tasked to kill a dragon at a lair that you have already cleared, the dragon there will respawn. However, killing a respawned dragon (whether it has respawned because of this quest, or naturally after 10 or 30 days) will probably result in not getting a dragon soul.
- You need to have completed [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") first before receiving this quest.

## Bugs

- The dragon at Mount Anthor may not spawn, and the quest target will point to an incorrect location.
  -  Use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `setstage BQ04 100` to skip to the next stage, or `setstage BQ04 200` to jump directly to quest completion.

## Quest Stages

| Bounty: Dragon (BQ04) | | |

| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill the dragon located at <Alias=BountyLocation> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Collect bounty from <Alias=Steward>  *Objective 101:* Collect bounty from <Alias=Jarl> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BQ04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BQ04`.

# Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | 100 gold |
| ID: | BQ02 |

Kill a Man of the Reach

## Radiant Options

Any innkeeper in the Reach can give you this quest, as can [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek"). You will be directed to one of the possible [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") camps in the hold, and you will then need to obtain your reward from Jarl [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund").

| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") |
| --- |
| [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt") [Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt") [Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt") [Dragon Bridge Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Overlook "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Overlook") [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt") [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the [bounty letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(forsworn) "Skyrim:Bounty (forsworn)").
2. Go to the Forsworn camp and kill the leader (usually a [Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn#Forsworn_Briarhearts "Skyrim:Forsworn")).
3. Return to Igmund for the reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speaking with any innkeeper or Igmund about work may lead them to give you a letter of bounty requiring you to kill a Forsworn leader. Head to the camp specified in the letter and kill the marked Forsworn leader. Then return to Igmund for your reward of 100 gold.

## Notes

- This quest is contingent on Igmund being the jarl; it will not be given if the city has changed hands.

## Quest Stages

| Bounty: Forsworn (BQ02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill the leader of <Alias=BountyLocation> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Collect the bounty from <Alias=Steward>  *Objective 101:* Collect the bounty from <Alias=Jarl> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BQ02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BQ02`.

# Skyrim:Bounty: Giant

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | 100 gold |
| ID: | BQ03 |
| Required Level: | 20 |

Giants are troubling the Jarl's hold.

## Radiant Options

Any innkeeper, [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") or Jarl's [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") can give you this quest. You will be directed to one of the [giant camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") in the hold, where you will then need to kill a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") there to obtain your reward from the jarl or steward of the hold.

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Broken Limb Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Limb_Camp "Skyrim:Broken Limb Camp") [Cradlecrush Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradlecrush_Rock "Skyrim:Cradlecrush Rock") [Steamcrag Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamcrag_Camp "Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp") | [Secunda's Kiss](/wiki/Skyrim:Secunda%27s_Kiss "Skyrim:Secunda's Kiss")[†](#intnote_secunda) | [Talking Stone Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Talking_Stone_Camp "Skyrim:Talking Stone Camp") | [Blizzard Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Blizzard_Rest "Skyrim:Blizzard Rest") [Red Road Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Road_Pass "Skyrim:Red Road Pass") [Stonehill Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehill_Bluff "Skyrim:Stonehill Bluff") [Tumble Arch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Tumble_Arch_Pass "Skyrim:Tumble Arch Pass") | [Bleakwind Basin](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Basin "Skyrim:Bleakwind Basin") [Guldun Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Guldun_Rock "Skyrim:Guldun Rock") [Sleeping Tree Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Camp "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Camp") |

[†](#note_secunda)This location appears as "Secunda's Shelf" in your quest log.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the bounty letter from an innkeeper, Jarl, or steward.
2. Go to the giant camp and kill the giant.
3. Return to the Jarl or the Jarl's steward for the reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speaking with any innkeeper, Jarl, or Jarl's steward about work may lead them to give you a [letter of bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(giant) "Skyrim:Bounty (giant)") requesting you to kill a giant. This will give you a miscellaneous objective to kill the giant in a specific camp. Head to the camp specified in the letter and kill the marked giant (there may be multiple giants, but you only have to kill the marked one). Once the giant is killed, you can return to the Jarl or steward for your 100 gold reward.

## Notes

- Sometimes the Jarl may request to kill another giant in a camp previously cleared. This is not a bug. New giants will be spawned and will be correctly associated with markers, killing and quest updates.

## Bugs

- The objective "Collect bounty from Skald" may not clear from quest list. This bug is due to the quest pointer completing stage 100 when you talk to Skald instead of stage 101.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  -  A possible workaround is to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `setObjectiveCompleted BQ03 101 1` before turning in the quest to Skald, to clear the journal entry. Then just talk to Skald to get your bounty.

## Quest Stages

| Bounty: Giant (BQ03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill the giant located at <Alias=BountyLocation> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Collect bounty from <Alias=Steward>  *Objective 101:* Collect bounty from <Alias=Jarl> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BQ03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BQ03`.

# Skyrim:Bounty Collector

## Overview

| Bounty Collector | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | Radiant (6-28) | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000F812A |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | Radiant (155-497) | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | Radiant (25-40) | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | Radiant (95-258) | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Very Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [WEBountyHunter](/wiki/Skyrim:WEBountyHunter "Skyrim:WEBountyHunter") | | |

Bounty Collector

A **Bounty Collector** can be [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Bounty_Collector "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wilderness if you have accumulated a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Bounties "Skyrim:Crime") of more than 1000 gold in any [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds"). Unlike city [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards"), he will ignore the distinction between holds and will attempt to track you down regardless of which hold you are in. He will demand from you payment equal to 1.2× your current bounty. If you refuse, he will attack.

He wears a set of leveled [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Heavy Armor (item)") (up to [steel plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate "Skyrim:Steel Plate") in quality), including the boots, gauntlets, and helmet. He always carries at least one leveled [heavy shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Shields_2 "Skyrim:Armor") (up to [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") in quality), a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality), and 50-250 gold, dependent on his level. He will also carry either a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") or a leveled [two-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:Two-Handed Weapons") (up to [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") in quality).

## Dialogue

When he sees you in the wilderness, he will approach you and will tell you not to move:

:   *"Stop right there."*
:   **What do you want?**
:   *"You have quite the bounty on your head in [hold]. You pay me, and I see that your name is cleared."*

:   :   **I don't have the gold.**
    :   *"Then you are worth more to me dead!"* **(Becomes hostile)**

:   :   **Pay (Gold).**
    :   *"I will make sure this gets back to the Jarl. Minus my cut, of course. Consider your name cleared, for now."*

If you speak to him after handing over the gold, he will tell you:

:   *"I have no more business with you."*
:   *"People think they can run away from their crimes, but I will always catch up with them and make them pay."*

## Notes

- If you have the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on installed, the bounty collector, like other high-level NPCs that use the same template, may be wearing [Nordic carved armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Armor "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Armor").

## Bugs

- Paying the bounty collector may fail to clear your bounty.
  -  Find a guard for the hold you have the bounty in, open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), click on the guard, and use the command `paycrimegold 0 0` to pay off your bounty. Make sure you are close enough to the guard that his proper [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID#RefID.2C_BaseID "Skyrim:Form ID") appears when you click on him, or else the command won't work.
- Rather than approach you and demand payment, the bounty collector may simply attack you instead.
  -  Open the console, click on the bounty collector (his RefID will appear, with 'ff' as the first two digits), then type `scaonactor` followed by <enter>. This will remove his aggression towards you and start his normal dialogue about clearing your bounty.
- The bounty collector may charge you 0 gold in Falkreath Hold due to a typo in the script.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Bounty Hunter

## Overview

Three **Bounty Hunters** can be [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Bounty_hunters_vs_Player "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wilderness after they track you down to kill you by [order of the jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(player) "Skyrim:Bounty (player)") from a hold where you have accumulated a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Bounties "Skyrim:Crime") of 1000 gold or higher. Their inventories are fully leveled.

All three Bounty Hunters will attack you at once. There is no way to pay them, as they will try to kill you without hesitation.

They will also carry the [bounty note](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(player) "Skyrim:Bounty (player)") for you.

# Skyrim:Bounty Quests

## Overview

These **bounty quests** can be given to you by any innkeeper in any [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds"), or you can receive them directly from the hold's [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward"). When you ask for one, you'll be given a bounty letter. They are called bounty quests because, upon completion, you are given a bounty, or reward. Once you have taken care of the requested target, you can return to the hold's [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") or steward for a reward. Bounty quests can be repeated indefinitely, up to a point: you can have 1 each of the quests below active at the same time (for a total of 4 concurrently running bounty quests), which must also originate in separate holds. And when one is completed, it cannot be replaced by the same one in the same hold. But sometimes they may bug and don't show at all despite having no other bounty quest. No solution is known.

Bounty quests, when acquired, may send you to a previously "Cleared" location, even if there has not normally been the requisite 30 days for respawning. The monster(s) in the zone should respawn at once.

- **[Bounty: Bandit Boss](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Bandit_Boss "Skyrim:Bounty: Bandit Boss")**: Eliminate a bandit leader for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Notes

- Each bounty letter has a job description with details on where you need to go, who you need to eliminate, and who you need to report to when you're done. There are bounty letters for [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(bandits) "Skyrim:Bounty (bandits)"), [forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(forsworn) "Skyrim:Bounty (forsworn)"), [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(giant) "Skyrim:Bounty (giant)"), and [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_(dragon) "Skyrim:Bounty (dragon)").
- Bounty quests are an excellent way to help you get the [Delver](/wiki/Skyrim:Delver "Skyrim:Delver") achievement faster, as they usually involve clearing out dungeons.
- The bounty quests involving bandits, forsworn, and giants will pay you 100 gold each. The ones involving dragons will pay you 500 gold each.
- You must be at least level 20 for the quests involving giants to be available, and you must finish [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") to gain access to the quests involving dragons. Likewise, the ones involving forsworn are exclusive to the Reach.
- It has been reported that it is possible to have a second Bandit Leader quest active instead of the Forsworn quest.
- A random Forsworn bounty quest can run concurrently with the non-repeating quest from Jarl Igmund, [Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)"), which is part of the process of earning the title of Thane. The two quests appear very similar in the journal, but completing the wrong one will of course not give any progression towards Thaneship, nor will it unlock Igmund's second quest to find Hrolfdir's Shield: the quest given by Jarl Igmund directly is the one in the Thane sequence, whereas the one given in an inn or by the steward is the random one.
- If no eligible bounty is available, there will be no bounty rumors in the inns or given by the steward or jarl. For instance, if you have a Bandit, Forsworn and Giant quest active while finishing off the Dragon bounty in Eastmarch (at the only possible eligible location, Bonestrewn Crest), then no bounty quests will be available in either Eastmarch (since the Dragon quest cannot be repeated there until it has been done somewhere else, and all the other types are already spoken for) or Haafingar or Whiterun (which both have no Dragon bounty quests at all, and all the other types are already spoken for): you will have to travel to another hold, or complete one of the other existing bounty quests to free up another space.
- If you are offered a particular bounty, and reload from a prior save, there is a chance that the same innkeeper or steward will have no bounty-related dialogue. There is also a chance that they may offer you a different bounty.
- If you exile the Jarl who issued the bounty before turning it in, you will need to visit them or their steward in exile to complete the quest. However, if you exile the Jarl during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and re-take their affected Hold later on, you can visit them and their steward in their default palace to finish the quest.

## Bugs

- Objectives to collect the bounty in Dawnstar may not finish properly if you collect the reward directly from the Jarl.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- Bounty quests don't clean up the generated letter if you leave the location without actually accepting the quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.3, fixes this bug.
- If your bounty requires you to kill a dragon in a dragon lair you already cleared out, the new dragon may not release its soul upon death. **?**
  - Push the corpse away from the lair with a spell that causes objects to fly around, such as [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), and you should now be able to absorb the dragon's soul.
- If your bounty quest sends you to a non-respawning dungeon, you'll be unable to finish the quest if you previously cleared it out. **?**
  - Reload a previous save and get a different location.

# Skyrim:Bow to the Master

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. | **Retrieve a [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravin_Llanith "Skyrim:Dravin Llanith")'s stolen bow.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |

| ID: | FreeformMerryfairFarm |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |

*"Not only did I*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *they take my bow, but they took all of our coin as well."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Dravin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravin_Llanith "Skyrim:Dravin Llanith") at [Merryfair Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Merryfair_Farm "Skyrim:Merryfair Farm").
2. Find [Dravin's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Dravin.27s_Bow "Skyrim:Quest Items") in [The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway").
3. Return to Dravin.

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Dravin Llanith](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravin_Llanith "Skyrim:Dravin Llanith") is a farmer who lives at [Merryfair Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Merryfair_Farm "Skyrim:Merryfair Farm"). Talk to him and he will tell you about his stolen family heirloom, a bow. A few days ago, some thieves from Riften broke into his house and stole it. He is quite sure those [lowlifes](/wiki/Skyrim:Lowlife "Skyrim:Lowlife") took the bow with them back to [The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"). If you can head into the Ratway and get his bow back, he would pay you what he can.

The Ratway is somewhere under Riften, these sewers and tunnels are inhabited by some [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") and thugs. Pay attention to the traps at the same time. In order to retrieve the bow, you have to get into The Ratway Vaults. The only way to get to the vaults is through [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") — the door is to the right of the bar. It's not necessary to join the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to get access to the entrance. However, it would be a good choice to do this quest during [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business"). You can find the bow in a chest in a room near the stairs, guarded by a Vagrant and a Lowlife.

Return to Dravin after you get his bow. He will be very excited and reward you with five leveled gems. *"I don't know how you got it back, and I don't want to know. Frankly, I don't even care... I'm just so glad to see it again."*

## Notes

- Several side quests require a certain type of gem(s) so it may be worth making a save point just before talking to him. Loading a previous save will change the gems rewarded thus allowing you to choose, as long as you meet the level requirement for gems.

## Bugs

- If you enchant (and possibly also rename, confirmation needed) the bow, it may lose its quest item tag, and thus you can drop it normally. **?**
  - This might only apply to Special Edition.
- If you enchant and rename the bow, its name may revert back to "Dravin's Bow." The enchantment remains unaffected. **?**
  - This might only apply to Special Edition.
- If you find Dravin's Bow before being assigned the quest, you may be unable to return it to him even if he tells you about his stolen bow after you have found it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, addresses this issue. You may need to save and reload to get the fix to work—using "Continue" from the main menu may not work.
  -  If this occurs, you can use the console command `setstage FreeformMerryfairFarm 30` to advance the quest to the correct stage, allowing you to complete it.

## Quest Stages

| Bow to the Master (FreeformMerryfairFarm) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Retrieve Dravin's Bow |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return Dravin's Bow |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformMerryfairFarm stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformMerryfairFarm`.

Bradyn

**Bradyn** is a dead [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") miner found in [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow") during the quest [Unearthed](/wiki/Skyrim:Unearthed "Skyrim:Unearthed"). He wears [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), and [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves#000261c1 "Skyrim:Gloves"). He carries a copy of the book *[Ahzidal's Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Descent "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Descent")*, a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and other minor items and gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Unearthed](/wiki/Skyrim:Unearthed "Skyrim:Unearthed")**: Assist [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys") in his search for the relics of [Ahzidal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(creature) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (creature)") in [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow").

Outside of Braidwood Inn

**Braidwood Inn** is an inn at the center of the small settlement of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove").

The inn was built next to the mine and serves as dining hall, shop and everything else for those who live in Kynesgrove. It's not far due south of Windhelm, but the residents act like it's miles away from anywhere else.

[Iddra](/wiki/Skyrim:Iddra "Skyrim:Iddra") and her husband, [Kjeld](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjeld "Skyrim:Kjeld"), run the inn together. However, Kjeld is more interested in the running of the mine and will buy any malachite ore you have.

It only consists of one zone, which is the [interior](#Braidwood_Inn).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver") [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Alteration (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Alteration (Expert)")  [Iddra](/wiki/Skyrim:Iddra "Skyrim:Iddra") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Kjeld](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjeld "Skyrim:Kjeld") \*  [Kjeld the Younger](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjeld_the_Younger "Skyrim:Kjeld the Younger") |

\* Kjeld will take over as innkeeper if Iddra is dead.

## Exterior †

The inn is set near [Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine"), which has a camp set up outside the inn consisting of three small tents with bed rolls in them around a central campfire. There are a couple of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and a rack with nine [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging from them. There are also a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and a small vegetable garden with ten [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), four [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), six [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and eight [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants. Of all the items only the salmon are owned, and taking them is considered stealing. Next to the inn itself is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), plenty more barrels of foodstuffs and just down the road to the west is a chicken coop housing two [chicken nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"). There is a flight of steps up to the porch on the front of the inn, with a wooden bench just to the right of the entrance.

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 10 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  4 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd")  6 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  8 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 9 [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

[†](#note_Note)Including [Steamscorch Mine Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine")

## Braidwood Inn

Braidwood Inn common room

The front door of the inn, as with most in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), leads directly into the common room which consists of a central long fire pit with five long wooden tables and benches against the side walls and the counter at the far end. On the tables are a selection of bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), with the exception of the table in the southwestern corner which also has a couple of [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and several pieces of cheese. The room has three doorways off of it, two to the west and one to the east. On the counter is a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, several pieces of cheese and two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), while under the counter two bottles of alto wine, six bottles of wine, fourteen bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), three small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer") and five [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins. Behind the counter, against the north wall are five large vats and several food barrels. In front of these are racks hanging from the ceiling holding eleven [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), with two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") also hanging from the ceiling. Either side of the doorway to the east are sets of shelves that hold two bottles of alto wine, six bottles of wine, seven bottles of Nord mead, four loaves of bread and three bunches of elves ear. In the northwest corner, next to one of the vats is a flower basket holding two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and a pine thrush egg.

A bedroom in Braidwood Inn

The largest of the three bedrooms is the one to the east, it is also the one you are given and shown to if you rent a room at the inn. It contains a double bed coming out of the south wall with an empty unlocked long [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the left, with a large coin purse hidden to the left of it, in the southeastern corner. Against the east wall are two dressers containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and having a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), two bottles of alto wine, three bottles of Nord mead, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and a copy of the uncommon book *[Songs of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Songs_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Songs of Skyrim")* on top. To the right of the bed, in the southwestern corner is a small square wooden table and chair with a fancy [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") and [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") on the top of the table. Against the north wall are a pile of three food sacks.

Opposite this bedroom are two more, with the left-hand one containing a single owned bed in the northwestern corner and a round wooden table and chair to the right of it. On the table is a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and three common books. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked chest containing leveled items, with a tall wardrobe against the north wall. The right-hand room contains two single owned beds against the south wall, separated by an unlocked chest containing leveled items and a round wooden table and chair in the northwestern corner, with two common books on top.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from either Iddra; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 4 | [Honningbrew Meads](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |
| 7 | Random [Drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn Food |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- Once you have [helped](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You#Iddra_and_Roggi_Knot-Beard "Skyrim:A Few Words with You") Iddra by speaking to Roggi, the beds in the small bedrooms become free to use.
- [Kjeld the Younger](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjeld_the_Younger "Skyrim:Kjeld the Younger") won't take over as publican of the inn if his parents are dead.
- Other than most barrels and sacks, all containers in the inn are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- If anything happens to Iddra, Kjeld will take over room rentals, but not merchant services. In the absence of Iddra, it is impossible to buy or sell things in Kynesgrove.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. Kjeld can now sell innkeeper merchandise as well if he takes over as the publican of Braidwood Inn.
- The music that plays inside is incorrectly set to environmental exploration music, rather than the standard tavern music.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The AI counter markers in Braidwood Inn have no ownership assigned which can cause NPCs other than the vendors to use them.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.
