| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionCidhnaMine](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionCidhnaMine "Skyrim:CrimeFactionCidhnaMine"); [DruadachRedoubtFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction "Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction"); [TownCidhnaMinePrisonerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownCidhnaMinePrisonerFaction "Skyrim:TownCidhnaMinePrisonerFaction") | | |

Braig

**Braig** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [witchblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchblade "Skyrim:Witchblade"), held prisoner in [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"). He has been imprisoned longer than anyone else in the mine with the exception of [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach").

He wears a [roughspun tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Roughspun_Tunic "Skyrim:Roughspun Tunic") and [footwraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Footwraps "Skyrim:Footwraps"), and carries a bottle of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") and a [shiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Shiv "Skyrim:Shiv"). He knows the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") spell [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie"), and the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spell [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames").

During the day, he can be found mining in various areas of Cidhna Mine, going to sleep at 10pm and waking at 4am the next morning.

## Related Quests

- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!

### No One Escapes Cidhna Mine

Once you tell him that Madanach has sent you he will be more open:

:   **Madanach asked me to hear your story.**
:   *"My story, huh? Everyone in Cidhna Mine has a tale. Let's hear yours first. When was the first time you felt chains around your wrists?"*

You can then reply in three ways:

| Option | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **It was at Helgen. I was being sent to the executioner.** | *"So you know what it's like to have your life in someone else's hands. Why should they get to decide? Isn't judgment for the gods?"* |
| **Young. I've always been known to get into trouble.** | *"Then you know the hard looks as judgment gets set upon you. The sneers of people who never had to face sentence."* |
| **None of your business.** | *"Fine. Don't tell me. But I know that look in your eyes. Someone who's faced death at the hands of the law."* |

:   *"Do you have any family? Anyone waiting for you on the outside?"*
:   **Yes, but they're far from Skyrim.**/**I have friends. Only family I need.**/**None that I care to talk about.**
:   *"I had a daughter, once. She'd be 23 this year. Married to some hot-headed silver worker or maybe on her own learning the herb trade. The Nords didn't care who was and who wasn't involved in the Forsworn Uprising. I had spoken to Madanach once, that was enough. But my little Aethra didn't want to see her papa leave her. She pleaded to the Jarl to take her instead. And after they made me watch as her head rolled off the block, they threw me in here anyway, to dig up their silver."*

:   :   **You think your story justifies the murders the Forsworn committed?**
    :   *"I'm not Madanach. I was never a leader of the Forsworn. The only anger I can justify is my own. But every family in the Reach has a story like mine. There are no innocent onlookers in this struggle. Just the guilty, and the dead."*

:   :   **I'm sorry to hear what happened to you.**
    :   *"My daughter is the one who needs your pity. I'm just a poor Forsworn whose only regret is not killing more Nords before I was locked up."*

## Dialogue

His potential greetings are:

:   *"What do you want? Have digging to do."*
:   *"Don't reach for a shiv around me, or we'll both regret it."*

If you try to talk to him before starting the quest it becomes clear that he doesn't want to talk:

:   **How long have you been here?**
:   *"Long enough."*

:   **What are you in for?**
:   *"Don't want to talk about it."*

## Conversations

Throughout the day, Braig can be seen talking to his fellow prisoners:

:   **Braigh**: *"Think the guards will be coming down, soon?"*
:   **[Duach](/wiki/Skyrim:Duach "Skyrim:Duach")**: *"Ah, it's not been more than a few days since they came down the last time."*

:   **Braigh**: *"Nearly broke my back out in the mines today. Damn Nords should bleed for putting us through this!"*
:   **Duach**: *"Some day, brother. Some day."*

This scene, despite mentioning [Odvan](/wiki/Skyrim:Odvan "Skyrim:Odvan")'s alias in Braig's stead, is actually set up to work with Braig and Duach.

:   **Braig**: *"Have any skooma? I need to get something from Grisvar."*
:   **Duach**: *"You make one move towards my skooma, and I shiv you."*

:   **[Grisvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Grisvar_the_Unlucky "Skyrim:Grisvar the Unlucky")**: *"Hey, remember that girl, [Eisa](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa_Blackthorn "Skyrim:Eisa Blackthorn")? The one who sliced open that pickpocket they threw in here?"*
:   **Braig**: *"The Blackblood*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *girl? Now there was a fighter. If I didn't know better, I'd say she was a Forsworn woman."*

## Notes

- Braig mispronounces Madanach's name, calling him "Ma**na**danach" when asked if his daughter's death justifies the murders committed by the Forsworn.
- Some internal data, such as the name of the scene between him and Grisvar, identifies Braig as **Blathloc**.
- In the scene between Grisvar and him, they are actually talking about Eisa Blackthorn, who, despite them misremembering her last name, can actually be found in-game. Her [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eisa's Journal") mentions having served in Cidhna Mine for a year.
  - The same scene is internally also number "**02**", but there is no previous scene between the two men to be found.
- Although Braig says that his daughter would have been 23 this year, the Reach was retaken in 4E 176, 25 years prior to the events of the game.

Braith

**Braith** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child"), and the daughter of [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren") and [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir") living in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). The family is clearly dysfunctional, with Saffir buried in books all day long and Amren worrying about nothing but his lost family sword. As a result, the lonely Braith has turned into the local bully, her favorite target being [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born"). During the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bullying_Braith "Skyrim:Bullying Braith"), you will help Lars get rid of his bully, and find out Braith's true intentions.

The family lives in [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") in the Wind District of Whiterun and Braith sleeps in her room on the second floor every night between 9pm and 9am. Immediately after waking up, Braith leaves the house and spends three hours fooling around with the other children of Whiterun, until she returns home at noon. At 3pm she exits the house again, this time for four hours of playing. The last two hours are spent inside the house, eating, relaxing, or trying to communicate with her distracted parents.

She wears [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Shoes"). She carries her [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Amren's House"), a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Bullying Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Bullying_Braith "Skyrim:Bullying Braith")**: Convince Braith to stop bullying Lars.

## Dialogue

You can see her walking around town with a chip on her shoulder, saying:

:   *"Boys, girls, dogs, elders - there's nobody I won't fight!"*
:   *"What're you lookin' at? I'm not afraid of you, ya know. Even if you are my elder."*
:   *"I don't fight Lars no more, if that's what you're worried about."* (heard only after you've convinced her to leave him alone)

## Conversations

When you first enter Whiterun, you will not find Braith fooling around in the streets, nor will you find Lars Battle-Born. However, if you visit the Wind District, near the [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born"), you will find Braith, who obviously managed to corner Lars. The first conversation will always play out first, with the next two appearing randomly:

*"Battle-Born! Give me your money!"*

:   **Braith**: *"Battle-Born! Give me your money!"*
:   **Lars**: *"I... I don't have any money."*
:   **Braith**: *"You'd better give me five septims, right now, or I'm going to bloody your nose..."*
:   **Lars**: *"No! Please! I really don't have any money, Braith! I'll give you ten septims tomorrow. Just don't hit me."*
:   **Braith**: *"Ten septims tomorrow, baby Battle-Born. Or I'm gonna bloody your nose and your lip."*

:   **Braith**: *"Oh look, it's little baby Battle-Born."*
:   **Lars**: *"Leave me alone, Braith..."*
:   **Braith**: *"What are you gonna do if I don't? Huh? Gonna cry to your papa?"*
:   **Lars**: *"Just go away!"*

:   **Lars**: *"Braith. I.... I've come to tell you that I'm not afraid of you anymore."*
:   **Braith**: *"Don't make me laugh, baby Battle-Born. You'll be afraid of me till the day I kill you."*
:   **Lars**: *"You... You're wrong! You can't hurt me anymore..."*
:   **Braith**: *"Oh no? So you're gonna fight back if I punch you? Huh? You're gonna hit a girl?"*
:   **Lars**: *"Well, no... I... I mean..."*
:   **Braith**: *"That's what I thought. Now get out of my way, baby. I got things to do."*

She will then proceed with her daily routine, playing with [Mila Valentia](/wiki/Skyrim:Mila_Valentia "Skyrim:Mila Valentia") and even Lars, until it is time to go back inside her home, where her mother resides, always with her nose in a book.

Back in the house, Braith will randomly attempt to make a connection with her distracted mother, but will find no help. She will also be keen on talking about her victim, but even then, Saffir will not even look up from her book.

*"Not now, Braith. Go... go ask your father."*

:   **Braith:** *"Mother? Can I talk to you?"*
:   **Saffir:** *"Not now, Braith."*
:   **Braith:** *"But..."*
:   **Saffir:** *"Not now, Braith."*

:   **Braith:** *"Mother?"'*
:   **Saffir:** *"What?"*
:   **Braith:** *"I wanted to ask you something. It's about a boy..."*
:   **Saffir:** *"Not now, Braith. Go... go ask your father."*

*"Why don't you talk to your mother about this, okay?"*

While Saffir ignores her daughter completely and is rather annoyed by her presence, Amren proves to be somewhat more talkative. Unfortunately, when it comes to boys, Braith will not find much help from him either:

:   **Braith:** *"Papa, the next time you go away, I want to come with you."*
:   **Amren:** *"When I go away, I go to war. That's no place for a little girl."*
:   **Braith:** *"Every knight needs a squire. I could help you with your sword, things like that."*
:   **Amren:** *"Nice try, blossom, but I'm not a knight, I'm a mercenary. The answer's still no. Besides, your mother would miss you too much."*
:   **Braith:** *"Yeah. Right."*

:   **Braith:** *"Papa, I want to talk to you..."*
:   **Amren:** *"Hmm? What about?"*
:   **Braith:** *"Well, there's this boy, and..."*
:   **Amren:** *"Listen, Braith... Why don't you talk to your mother about this, okay? There's a good girl."*

## Quest-Related Events

When you think it is time to rid Lars of the bully, seek out Braith and talk to her. She will now skip her usual greetings and instead say:

:   *"Stupid Lars Battle-Born. I fight him almost every day, but it's not much of a fight, 'cause he don't fight back."*
:   **You need to stop bullying Lars Battle-Born.**
:   *"Yeah? Why?"*

You can now choose between three options:

:   **I'm Lars' bodyguard. Mess with him and you mess with me!**
:   **He has a disease. It's very contagious.**
:   **You want to be shipped off to the [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage")?**

All three choices will lead to the same response:

:   *"Okay, okay! I'll leave him alone! I was just kidding around. Besides, if he'd only kiss me, I wouldn't have to beat him up all the time..."*

## Notes

- Your [adopted](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") girls may complain about her: *"Braith is a big meanie. She keeps telling Lars'n me what to do. I don't wanna play with her anymore."*
- If Saffir is dead, Amren will change his last response during conversation to: *"I wish your mother were still alive. She could answer you much better. Let me think on it and we'll talk later."*

## Bugs

- In the game, during the opening conversation with Lars, Braith will say: *"You'd better give me five septims, right now, or I'm going to bloody your nose... Ten septims tomorrow, baby Battle-Born. Or I'm gonna bloody your nose and your lip."*, making Braith undecided on the amount of septims she wants. The conversation was supposed to play out as shown above.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.

Bralsa Drel

Bralsa Drel working on Miraak's shrine

**Bralsa Drel** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who lives in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). She has fallen on hard times since [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") closed and has spent all of her fortune made in the mine on drinking, to the point where she was kicked out of the [Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch"). During the quest [Feeding the Addiction](/wiki/Skyrim:Feeding_the_Addiction "Skyrim:Feeding the Addiction") you will have to convince innkeeper [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") to let her back in.

She is initially found at the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone") where she works in a state of hypnosis while chanting the rants of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)"). She will do this work around the clock until you free her and the other Raven Rock citizens from the spell by [cleansing the stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"). Once freed, she will return to her normal, albeit sad, existence in Raven Rock. Due to her drinking she even lost her home but has been allowed to sleep in the [Abandoned Building](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Building "Skyrim:Abandoned Building") which she does every night between midnight and 6am, right next to another poor soul, namely local beggar [Rirns Llervu](/wiki/Skyrim:Rirns_Llervu "Skyrim:Rirns Llervu"). After waking up she strolls around inside the house until 8am when the shops at the local market open up. She then spends the next eight hours at said market, trying desperately to get some gold out of her fellow citizens. At 4pm she returns to the abandoned house where she wanders around until her bedtime.

As you complete quests and Raven Rock starts to bloom again, Bralsa will see two major changes in her daily routine. Once you have reopened [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") during the quest [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent"), Bralsa will finally see her life get back on track and she will start working inside the mine again, every day between 4pm and midnight, although her thirst will conquer her new work: After helping her out during [Feeding the Addiction](/wiki/Skyrim:Feeding_the_Addiction "Skyrim:Feeding the Addiction") she will enter the Retching Netch every day between 6pm and 10pm and down ale with the other regulars.

Bralsa wears a [Dunmer outfit](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Outfit "Skyrim:Dunmer Outfit") with matching [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Shoes "Skyrim:Dunmer Shoes"), and she carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Feeding the Addiction](/wiki/Skyrim:Feeding_the_Addiction "Skyrim:Feeding the Addiction")**: Convince an [innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") to let a drunken miner get back to [the bar](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch").
- **[It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste")**: Distribute [Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")'s [Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") to the citizens of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

## Dialogue

When you free her from Miraak's spell by using the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") shout, a confused Bralsa will wake up and will have normal greetings:

:   *"I lost my house, my family, my life... and then I lost my mind. How could it have gotten any worse?"*
:   *"Don't pity me. And don't look at me like that. I know what I am."*
:   *"I could swing a pickaxe better than any man in the mines. Made thousands of coins. Now it's all gone."*
:   *"How are you supposed to live when your only means of trade is yanked out from under you?"*
:   *"The voices in my head are gone now thanks to you. Now I can finally get some rest."*
:   *"Look at me, I'm a different person. And I have you to thank for it."*

If directly spoken to:

:   **You appear to be in dire straits. What happened?**
:   *"I was one of the wealthiest miners in town... I could haul up almost three or four times what the average digger could. I never saw the end coming like it did... the mine running out of ebony. Unlike most of my fellow miners, I was too foolish to save enough coin for that day. The rest I spent on sujamma to drown my sorrows. Councilor Morvayn was kind enough to allow Rirns and I to live in one of the abandoned buildings. At least it keeps the ash out of our eyes."*

Once the mines are reopened:

:   **How are things now that the mines are open again?**
:   *"Couldn't be better. The sections that are being opened up have revealed some huge deposits of ebony. Old Crescius has a nose for exactly where to dig. If they'd only listened to him years ago, the town wouldn't have been in such dire straits. At this rate, I'll be able to put a roof over my head in just a few months."*

Her goodbyes:

:   *"Don't waste your life like I did."*
:   *"See you in the mines!"*

### Conversations

Bralsa begging in the market

She can be overheard begging with multiple residents of Raven Rock:

:   **Bralsa:** *"I know things are tough, but at least you have a roof over your head. Please, help me."*
:   **[Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory"):** *"Don't let me catch you spending it at the Netch."*

:   **Bralsa:** *"Please, I'm starving. Any help will do..."*
:   **Rirns** *"Bralsa, I can barely feed myself..."*

:   **Bralsa:** *"Is a single coin too much to ask for?"*
:   **[Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth"):** *"I'm sorry, I don't carry coin. Perhaps next time."*

:   **Bralsa:** *"Is a single coin too much to ask for?"*
:   **[Garyn Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Garyn_Ienth "Skyrim:Garyn Ienth"):** *"Here, have some food instead."*

### It's All In The Taste

When local innkeeper [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") wants you to promote his new batch of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") during the quest [It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste"), Bralsa will be really excited and take it off your hands with:

:   *"The day I refuse sujamma from Geldis is the day I sprout wings and fly off of this rock."*

### Reluctant Steward

When you are supposed to find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") during the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") she will have a quite unique response:

:   *"Would he give me skooma? I might do it for some skooma."*

However, it is not possible to give her any [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") (see [notes](#Notes)) - you can only tell her that you don't have any, which will make her say:

:   *"Come back when you do."*

### Feeding the Addiction

*"If I want to spend my last bag of coins getting drunk, that's my business."*

:   **Why should I pity you?**
:   *"Doesn't everyone pity the hopeless? Look at me... I'm no better than a beggar. I used to be a miner, a good one too. I made more gold digging up ore in a month than some people earn in a lifetime. When the mine dried up, I was lost. I have no other trade, so I spend my time drinking my fortune away at the Retching Netch... or I used to anyway."*
:   **Used to? What happened?**
:   *"That fetcher Geldis won't even allow me inside. Said I was bad for business. If I want to spend my last bag of coins getting drunk, that's my business. What does he care?"*

:   :   **I could talk to him for you.**
    :   *"You can try... If you can get that stubborn mule to let me into the Netch, I'll make sure you get what's coming to you."*

:   :   **Sorry to hear that.**
    :   *"Sure, I bet you are. Everyone's always sorry."*

Once you have convinced the concerned innkeeper to let Bralsa drink again, return to her and tell her the news:

:   **You're welcome at the Retching Netch anytime.**
:   *"Well then, I suppose I'm off to do what I do best. Here. This was something I carried around in happier times. Maybe you can find a use for it."*

She will then hand you an enchanted weapon of the best possible quality as a reward. After that, Bralsa can be found at the Retching Netch every day between 6pm and 10pm, doing what she does best.

## Notes

- According to the game data, Bralsa was not always intended to work the Earth Stone. As a result, the questions you can ask most other citizens will be missing and her responses will never be heard: *"Miraak? The name sounds familiar... Or does it? I can't remember."*, *"A shrine for... Well, it's... I think it's important."* and *"Did we build that, or did I imagine that?"*

## Bugs

- During [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward"), Bralsa will ask for some skooma. However, even if you have some in your inventory, you will not be able to give it to her. Her dialogue related to receiving skooma will therefore never be heard: *"Skooma! Lovely skooma. But I'd sooner give it up than go work for her*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*. That dunmer is crazy!"*
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- She was supposed to begin working the mine in Raven Rock once it is back in operation.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Brand-Shei

## Overview

| Brand-Shei (RefID: 00019DDC) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Brand-Shei

Brand-Shei stays in the background while [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") makes a distraction.

**Brand-Shei** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") trader within [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). He was orphaned at a young age and was raised by [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") in [Black Marsh](/wiki/Lore:Black_Marsh "Lore:Black Marsh"). He owns a stall in Riften Grand Plaza and specializes in selling [goods](#Standard_Merchandise) from [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"). Like other vendors of the plaza he is suspicious of [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") and his actions have earned Brand-Shei the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)")'s ire.

Brand-Shei is a permanent resident at [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse") and sleeps there every night between midnight and 6am. He starts the day with a one-hour breakfast then heads down to his market stall at Riften Grand Plaza. He works there for a solid thirteen hours before he returns to the bunkhouse for another meal at 8pm. After eating for four hours, he heads to bed at midnight and sleeps for six hours.

He wears a set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothes") and matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality at level 20).

## Related Quests

- **[A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement")**: Help teach a merchant to mind his own business.
- **[Distant Memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Distant_Memories "Skyrim:Distant Memories")**: Help Brand-Shei uncover his past.

## Dialogue

When you meet him in the market he will try and sell his wares by shouting:

:   *"Rare trinkets and the finest oddities from Morrowind!"*
:   *"Gems, potions, exotic ingredients... I have them all!"*
:   *"The fairest prices and the highest quality in Skyrim!"*

When you talk to him he will continue:

:   *"Can I interest you in some fine goods from Morrowind?"*
:   *"Have anything you wish to sell? I pay fair prices for all sorts of goods."*
:   *"If there's anything you wish to purchase, just let me know."*

If you meet him outside his working hours he may greet you with:

:   *"If you're ever in the market, I deal in specialty goods from Morrowind at one of the stands."*

### A Chance Arrangement

When you meet Brynjolf in Riften, it soon becomes apparent that Brand-Shei is in bad standing with the Thieves Guild. Brynjolf has set up a scam and you're supposed to plant [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi")'s [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi%27s_Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Madesi's Silver Ring") in Brand-Shei's pocket. Brynjolf will not provide much explanation about what Brand-Shei has done. When Brynjolf starts his distraction, Brand-Shei will leave his stand and express his doubts about yet another product from Brynjolf:

:   **Brand-Shei**: *"Come on, Brynjolf... what is it this time?"*
:   **Brynjolf**: *"Patience, Brand-Shei. This is a rare opportunity, and I wouldn't want you to get left out."*
:   **Madesi**: *"That's what you said about the Wisp Essence and it turned out to be crushed nirnroot mixed with water!"*
:   **Brynjolf**: *"That was a simple misunderstanding, but this item is the real thing. Lads and lasses I give you, Falmerblood Elixir!"*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"Oh come on, are you talking about the Snow Elves?"*
:   **Brynjolf**: *"The one and only."*

Brynjolf will then continue his prank while you steal the ring. Brand-Shei, on the other hand, will become quite tempted by Brynjolf's sales speech and will even ask:

:   **Brand-Shei**: *"How much does it cost?"*

While Madesi remains skeptical, Brand-Shei will decide that Falmerblood Elixir may be a good investment, and chooses between a few random lines:

:   **Brand-Shei**: *"I dunno, sounds like I should try it."*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"What if he's right? Maybe I'll buy one."*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"I could get rich and stop selling these trinkets."*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"This is just what I need right now."*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"I can't afford to get one, but can I afford not to?"*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"That Wisp Essence didn't help, but maybe this will."*

Once you plant the ring on Brand-Shei, Brynjolf will end the prank and a disappointed Brand-Shei will return to his stall with the words:

:   **Brand-Shei**: *"Damn. I knew I shouldn't have waited."*

However, Madesi will soon find out about the theft from his lockbox, and alert a guard who will confront Brand-Shei:

*"This is insane! I didn't steal anything!"*

:   **Guard**: *"All right, Brand-Shei. Turn out your pockets, we know you have it."*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"Have what? What in blazes are you talking about?"*
:   **Guard**: *"Don't play stupid. I said turn out your pockets... now!"*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"I'm telling you, I don't... wait, what's this ring? This isn't mine!"*
:   **Guard**: *"That's right. It isn't yours. You're under arrest, Brand-Shei."*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"This is insane! I didn't steal anything! I never saw this ring before in my entire life!"*
:   **Guard**: *"We can do this one of two ways. You can walk with me up to the keep, or I can drag your lifeless body. Your choice."*
:   **Brand-Shei**: *"But... I... very well."*

The guard will then escort Brand-Shei to [Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail") where he will be put in one of the cells, stripped of his belongings, and clad in a belted tunic:

:   *"Who did this to me?"*
:   *"This city is corrupt! You're all corrupt!"*
:   *"This is unfair! I'm innocent!"*

### Distant Memories

*"We're just going to make sure he sits in the prisons for a few days."*

Whether or not he is in prison, Brand-Shei has another problem, namely his past. When you point out that Brand-Shei is an odd name for a dark elf, he will agree:

:   *"I may be dark elf by birth, but I was raised Argonian. Through reasons I'm still trying to discover, I ended up orphaned then taken in by a kindly Argonian family in Black Marsh. I hope one day to find out what happened to me... how I ended up like that."*
:   **Do you have any clues about your past?**
:   *"Just one. I know when I was found by my Argonian father, I was wrapped in a blanket bearing the symbol of [House Telvanni](/wiki/Lore:House_Telvanni "Lore:House Telvanni"). It was one of the great houses in Morrowind long ago. Whether that means I was one of them or not, I'm uncertain. If you come across anything in your travels that might provide me with the answers I'm looking for, I'd be grateful."*
:   **I'll keep an eye open.**

    :   *"Thank you."*
:   **Why were you searching in Skyrim?**

    :   *"I learned that a matron who had served for House Telvanni had escaped Morrowind during the [Accession War](/wiki/Lore:Accession_War "Lore:Accession War"). Records showed her buying passage aboard a sailing vessel named 'The Pride of Tel Vos,' but that's where the trail ran cold. I spent years looking for what became of the ship, but I ended up empty-handed."*

A [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Lymdrenn_Tenvanni%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Lymdrenn Tenvanni's Journal") found in the wreckage of the ship reveals that Brand-Shei's true name is Brandyl Tenvanni. When you return from the [Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_The_Pride_of_Tel_Vos "Skyrim:Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos") with the journal, Brand-Shei will be most interested and hand you a reward:

:   **I found a book that might help your search.**
:   *"Let me see that! Yes... yes. This is it! I don't know how you found this stranger, but you've obviously succeeded where I had failed. Please, let me offer you this [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei%27s_Strongbox_Key "Skyrim:Brand-Shei's Strongbox Key"). It unlocks my strongbox under my stand in the marketplace. Help yourself to anything inside."*

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Brand-Shei's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ~3 | Leveled [Animal Parts](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Parts "Skyrim:Animal Parts") | Max 4 (4@75%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") | Max 2 (2@25%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingots "Skyrim:Ingots") | Best-quality; Max 2 (2@25%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Ore "Skyrim:Ore")/[Charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") | Max 2 (2@50%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 2 (2@50%) |
| ~8 | Leveled [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") (empty and full) | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~6 | [Lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") | Max 8 (7@75% + 1@100%) |
| ~2 | Low-level [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") (unenchanted) | Max 2 (2@75%) |
| ~2 | Low-level [Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (unenchanted) | Max 2 (2@75%) |
| ~3 | [Miscellaneous Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items") (clutter) | Max 4 (4@75%) |

## Conversations

**Brand-Shei**: *"[Svana](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield"), I heard that [Sibbi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") was put in jail. What happened?"*
**Svana**: *"They say... well, they say he murdered someone. Something to do with [Svidi](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynly_Star-Sung "Skyrim:Lynly Star-Sung")."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"Come to think of it, I haven't seen Svidi in a while. Wait... he didn't..."*
**Svana**: *"No, it was Svidi's brother, Wulfur. She's in hiding now. Somewhere far from here I'd suspect."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"If he wasn't a Black-Briar, I'd march right over to the jail and teach Sibbi some manners... but then I suppose I'd end up like Wulfur."*

**[Bolli](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli "Skyrim:Bolli")**: *"So while I was in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), I heard news that something terrible happened at [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen")."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"You've heard too? They say the town was completely destroyed by a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon")."*
**Bolli**: *"If that's true, then we have much more to fear than the Thieves Guild."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"I'd still keep an eye on my purse if I was you."*

**[Tythis Ulen](/wiki/Skyrim:Tythis_Ulen "Skyrim:Tythis Ulen")**: *"Brand-Shei... have you managed to find those boots for me?"*
**Brand-Shei**: *"What's with all the boots and shoes you keep buying? You must have bought twenty pairs in the last two years."*
**Tythis**: *"Always be prepared. You never know if you might get a split in one, or lose one, then where would you be? No sir, that's not happening to me."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"Um... okay. Well, the boots aren't here yet. Hopefully on the next [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") [caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders")."*

**[Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr")**: *"Brand-Shei, did you hear about Helgen? It's... it's gone! A dragon burned it to the ground!"*
**Brand-Shei**: *"Yes, I heard. I think all of Skyrim knows by now."*
**Shadr**: *"Do you... do you think that could happen here? I mean, could a dragon come here and burn the city down?"*
**Brand-Shei**: *"I don't know. All we can do is hope the [Eight](/wiki/Lore:Eight_Divines "Lore:Eight Divines") will favor us and have these creatures stay far away from Riften."*

**[Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar")**: *"I don't like being made a fool of, Brand-Shei. Not one bit."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"Maven, please. I didn't know it was your man. Had I known, I would have looked the other way, I swear."*
**Maven**: *"Turning him in to the guards? Have you joined Mjoll as official peacekeepers of Riften? You cost me a lot of coin."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"Maven, I... please, don't hurt me."*

**[Mjoll the Lioness](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness")**: *"Well met, Brand-Shei. I've come by to browse your wares today."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"Is it true you chased a thief from your home? I overheard [Aerin](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin "Skyrim:Aerin") mentioning it."*
**Mjoll**: *"It's true. Wasn't much of a thief though. Made enough noise to wake the [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain")."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"Good. Maybe that will teach them to leave honest citizens alone."*

**Mjoll**: *"I was hoping you could help me. It seems I've lost a ring that also means quite a bit to me. It's made of gold with an inscription on the inside that says 'sand elske.'"*
**Brand-Shei**: *"I'm afraid not. I don't deal in stolen goods."*
**Mjoll**: *"Stolen? How can you be certain? I may have just misplaced it somewhere in the city."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"Lady Mjoll, if you lost a gold ring anywhere in this city I'm afraid it's likely never to be seen again. I'm sorry."*

**[Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor")**: *"Brand-Shei, do you think you can find me some theilul?"*
**Brand-Shei**: *"The Argonian sugar-cane wine? It's pretty hard to get around here. Very expensive."*
**Nivenor**: *"That's fine. I have a special occasion coming up, and I'd like to have it."*
**Brand-Shei**: *"I'll see what I can do."*

## Notes

- There is a "Loot" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") on the front of his market stall.
- Both his [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Merchant_Chests "Skyrim:Containers") and his [service faction](/wiki/Skyrim:ServicesRiftenPlazaBrandish "Skyrim:ServicesRiftenPlazaBrandish"), as well as several object references in Riften, bear the name "Brandish". However, this has nothing to do with the [unrelated character of the same name](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandish "Skyrim:Brandish"). It instead refers to **Brandish Begin-Again**, an earlier (and possibly Nord) iteration of Brand-Shei's character. This name appears in the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* in Brand-Shei's place, and [unused dialogue for Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf#Unused_Dialogue "Skyrim:Brynjolf") similarly shows Brandish being mentioned in Brand-Shei's stead.
- Brand-Shei does not have a unique facial model, he instead uses the default male Dark Elf face. He shares this quirk with [Faldrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldrus "Skyrim:Faldrus").
- Although he advertises that he sells "exotic ingredients", Brand-Shei does not sell any ingredients.

## Bugs

- If you frame him during the quest A Chance Arrangement, he will be relocated to [Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail") and never return to his stall.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  -  Using the [console command](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") `set TG00BrandSheiJail to 0` fixes this.
- A second key with the same name as the key to his strongbox ([Brand-Shei's Strongbox Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei%27s_Strongbox_Key "Skyrim:Brand-Shei's Strongbox Key")) can be obtained through the "Wax Key" perk after installing [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"). The key opens a strongbox in [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") and all the [East Empire Company Strongboxes](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox"), but there is no apparent connection with Brand-Shei himself and the name seems to have simply been copied over without ever being changed.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19069)) The key gets renamed to East Empire Company Strongbox Key.
- His dialogue topic about the mystery of his birth no longer makes sense after you give him his journal during the quest Distant Memories.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. A condition check has been added to make this topic unavailable when Distant Memories is finished.

# Skyrim:Brandish

## Overview

| Brandish (RefID: 000CC5A1) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad") | | |
| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |

| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")**, [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [BanditFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BanditFaction "Skyrim:BanditFaction") | | |

Brandish

**Brandish** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [bandit wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") who resides in the library of [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad") while it is occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). Because of his involvement outlined in the [Bandit Chief's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit%27s_Journal_(Fort_Neugrad) "Skyrim:Bandit's Journal (Fort Neugrad)"), he is in the Fort Neugrad library most of the time. Otherwise, he roams outside near the wagon.

He wears a set of [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots"), and carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a leveled [health potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and a leveled amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

## Notes

- A lot of internal filenames refer to a "Brandish" in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), but these files have nothing to do with this NPC. The actual NPC that these files refer to is "Brandish Begin-Again", which was an earlier iteration/name for Riften marketplace vendor [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei"). For example, his [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Merchant_Chests "Skyrim:Containers") and [service faction](/wiki/Skyrim:ServicesRiftenPlazaBrandish "Skyrim:ServicesRiftenPlazaBrandish"), as well as several object references in Riften, are named after "Brandish" but assigned to, and used by, Brand-Shei.
- If you lockpick the door to the Library, but do not kill him after it, he may wander out.

# Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Settlement.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Settlement.png) | Farm: Brandy-Mug Farm ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brandy-Mug+Farm)) | | |

Brandy-Mug Farm

**Brandy-Mug Farm** is a [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") farm, a short distance east of [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables").

It is a modest single-roomed farmhouse, that is home to [Bolfrida Brandy-Mug](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolfrida_Brandy-Mug "Skyrim:Bolfrida Brandy-Mug"). It consists of two zones: the [exterior](#Exterior) and the [interior](#Brandy-Mug_Farm).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bolfrida Brandy-Mug](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolfrida_Brandy-Mug "Skyrim:Bolfrida Brandy-Mug") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

As you approach the farmhouse from the road there is a blue mountain flower to the right of the path to the front door. In the fenced off field beside the farmhouse [Bolfrida](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolfrida_Brandy-Mug "Skyrim:Bolfrida Brandy-Mug") cultivates eight bushels of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and a large number of [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes. In the field, there is a chicken coop, along with two [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken"), a [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") as well as a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") to the rear of the field and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") by the farmhouse.

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 8 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  10 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") | 2 [Chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  1 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") | 2 [Chickens coop](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Brandy-Mug Farm

Brandy-Mug farm interior

Upon entering there is a set of shelves on your left, against the north wall holding two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and several pieces of cheese on top. On the floor to the left is a basket containing two more leeks and hanging from the ceiling above are two garlic braids, three bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). In the northeastern corner there is a barrel containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and coming out from the center of the east wall is an owned double bed with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items at the foot of the bed.

In the southeastern corner is a round wooden table holding two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") anched against the south wall a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with a rack hanging from the ceiling to the right holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). In the middle of the south wall, opposite the entrance is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and on the mantelpiece is a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Daughter of the Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Daughter_of_the_Niben "Skyrim:Daughter of the Niben")*. To the right of the fireplace, also against the south wall is a long wooden table and bench with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a potato, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"). Under the table is a [potion of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor"). In the northwestern corner is a square wooden table and two chairs with four more sprigs of snowberries on top.

## Notes

- Other than most barrels and sacks, all containers in the farm are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.
-  Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the barrels outside the building as owned by the farm.

## Bugs

- Despite being nothing more than an average farm, Brandy-Mug Farm uses the map icon for "Settlement" rather than the expected "Farm".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

Gaius Maro at the start of his journey in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella") in the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary").
2. Travel to [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge").
3. *(Optional)* Steal [Gaius Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro")'s travel schedule.
4. Kill Gaius Maro and plant the [incriminating letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Incriminating_Letter_(DB) "Skyrim:Incriminating Letter (DB)"). For a bonus, kill him in a [major city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities").

### Sins of the Father

When you return from your fateful visit to [Vittoria Vici's wedding](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death"), you will find a gleeful [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") ready to move onto the next phase of the plan. She instructs you to visit with [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella") for the next mission. Gabriella informs you that with the Emperor traveling to Skyrim, the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") will be securing the way. In order to disrupt the security surrounding the Emperor, you will need to cripple its head, [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro"). The Brotherhood's plan to accomplish this is to kill [Gaius Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro"), the commander's son, and plant a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Incriminating_Letter_(DB) "Skyrim:Incriminating Letter (DB)") implicating him in a plot against the Emperor.

### Dragon Bridge

Gabriella has instructions on how to locate Gaius Maro, as well as how to earn a special bonus for this contract. To begin, travel to the town of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") and, if you choose, steal Gaius' [travel schedule](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro%27s_Schedule "Skyrim:Gaius Maro's Schedule"). This makes things much easier, and you really have no reason not to do it. Additionally, killing Gaius in any city other than Dragon Bridge will grant you the "reading of your future", according to Gabriella, but this is optional. To obtain the schedule, simply [sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") into the building where the schedule is located and nab it. Even if you are detected, with weapons sheathed and without casualties, a soldier will only yell, *"Hey, you won't get away with that!"*, one [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#BountiesBounty "Skyrim:Crime") is incurred and they do follow you. (To avoid a bounty, wait until the door shows as being unlocked to go inside. Then, once inside, look to see how many guards are inside. Usually there is only one awake and walking around. Wait for him to go outside and you can now take Gaius Maro's Schedule with no bounty, because the other guard(s) are asleep. Just to be safe, you can always sneak to take it.) Once outside, check what day of the week it is in-game, then read the schedule and travel to the appropriate city.
This is the schedule as it appears in game that you steal from the [Penitus Oculatus Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Outpost "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Outpost"):

| Day | Location | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Morndas | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), the [Emperor's Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour,_Emperor%27s_Tower "Skyrim:Castle Dour, Emperor's Tower") | - |
| Morndas evening | Solitude, [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") | Food and sleep. |
| Tirdas | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") | - |
| Tirdas evening | Windhelm, [Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Barracks "Skyrim:Windhelm Barracks") | Food and sleep. |
| Middas | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") | - |
| Turdas | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") | - |
| Turdas evening | Whiterun, the [Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") | Food and sleep. |
| Fredas | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") | - |
| Fredas evening | Markarth, [Guard Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Tower "Skyrim:Guard Tower") | Food and sleep. |
| Loredas | - | To be spent at your discretion. |
| Sundas | - | To be spent at your discretion. |

### The Stalker

Don't be afraid to simply wait for a day and follow Gaius around. There is no time limit on this quest, and when Gaius has completed his schedule, he will repeat the same schedule next week. It is much easier to assassinate him on the road when he is alone, but you forfeit your bonus reward by doing so. Wherever you kill him, loot his corpse and plant the incriminating letter on his body, then return to the Sanctuary. Alternatively, you can reverse-pickpocket the note prior to killing him.
Some strategies for completing the contract are to wait until he stays at the [Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). He will go to sleep in a room alone around midnight, allowing for an easy sneak attack. He might also be alone while he's eating in the [Windhelm barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Barracks "Skyrim:Windhelm Barracks"). Conversely, his notes suggest that he doesn't actually sleep in any of the inns or the barracks in Riften, and seems to spend most of his time in the main hall with plenty of watchful eyes, so it might be wiser not to bother him there. As with all the other targets from Nazir, you can alternatively speak to Gaius and provoke him into attacking you; this allows you to kill him in self-defense without a crime being registered.

### Solitude

Should it be Morndas as per Gaius' schedule seen in the Penitus Oculatus Outpost, he will be in Solitude overlooking Castle Dour's courtyard and the Emperor's Tower during the day. By evening, he will retire to the barracks below where [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") and [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") are normally found. This is a good spot to attempt to stealth kill him as he normally sits at the table just around the corner from the stairs. The guards will be asleep, and thus unaware of any attempt on Gaius, unless it is around 8:00 AM or 8:00 PM. Both these times are when the changing of the guard normally occurs, and the area will be full of guards retiring for some sleep while their relief gets up to head out on patrol. This is especially so if [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") is himself resting for the night, in which case he might see the murder and trigger a bounty. The chances of this happening are higher if sitting with Gaius when he is killed. A bow or crossbow may be the best option here by hiding in the shadows near the barrels in the kitchen area.

A good opening is when Aldis stands up to walk to the far end of the beds. With his back turned, an opening is made to stealth kill Gaius. Even if Aldis or the guards hear it, with a high enough Sneak, you will generally remain undetected. However, if Gaius is spoken to and made hostile, the guards will awaken and come to your aid, since they'll consider Gaius the criminal for attacking you first. In this case, you will need to deliver the final blow before Gaius becomes non-hostile again, risking a bounty should he not be killed and regains his health. Alternatively, the [Ebony Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Mail "Skyrim:Ebony Mail") acquired from [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") can be used to suck his health away with its [poison enchantment](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison_Damage "Skyrim:Poison Damage").

### Riften

In this particular city, if Gaius is there to do his rounds on Middas, the alleyway to the left provides an opportunity (the lock on the gate may need to be picked unless the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key") has been collected). As Maro leaves (around 1:00 A.M.), sniping him with an arrow will avoid detection and any bounty. If the archery skill is at a low level and/or the player does not have the appropriate perks, he may not die with one sneak attack, so there may be a prolonged fight. Another option is to wait in the corner of Riften Castle's courtyard, behind the small grouping of trees, and when he leaves (he exits that side every time at around 11:30 A.M., although the actual times may vary), he will be alone and far enough away from any guards to allow him to be killed without any worry about a crime.

### Palace of the Kings or Other Guard Barracks

Gaius will sleep in the barracks with the guards in Windhelm while there for his rounds on Tirdas. This can be one of the hardest places to get him without being detected. Around 10:00 P.M., in the corner by the sleeping guard, he can be sniped with a bow or crossbow (preferably after having coated the arrows with [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons")). Each time he is shot, he will get up and look around the room. He can be continually attacked without being discovered. The guards in the beds will sometimes get up and look as well, but with some luck and stealth, will ignore you, who should be in the shadows. After Maro is dead, once the guards settle down it is possible to creep over to his body and plant the Incriminating Letter. Sneaking back to the corner, then jumping over the beds with the guards in them until the doorway is reached, allows you to sneak out to freedom. Just as it is in Solitude, if Gaius is made hostile by speaking to him, the guards will awaken and support you since Gaius just made himself a criminal in their eyes by initiating an attack.

### The Bannered Mare

In Whiterun when he is there on Turdas, it is extremely easy to sneak into his bedroom in The Bannered Mare, as it seems to be the only time he is not bunking in a castle or in barracks. He can be killed in his sleep with the door shut, and then the letter planted. This does not result in a bounty.

However, there is a high chance that Maro might fall behind on his itinerary schedule and therefore only make a brief stop at The Bannered Mare, for some drinks, before continuing on to Markarth. In this case he normally arrives alone on Turdas evening (10:00–11:00 P.M.) and heads straight to the hearth in the middle of the inn for a drink, while enjoying the bard's performances.

With a high level of Sneak and the Ebony Mail, while sneaking he can be shot using a ranged weapon from the balcony of the room overlooking the hearth (it is the same room rented from [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda")). Since this balcony is full of shadowy spots it is possible to hide in one of those and wait for Gaius Maro to charge upstairs looking for his assailant. Once he has touched the shadowy tendrils of poison emitted by the Ebony Mail, it is just a matter of waiting for him to fall lifeless. Then the Incriminating Letter can be planted and the scene left with no alarm raised.

Obviously, this technique can also be used in other dark locations as well. A word of caution though: killing him in public usually leads to collateral damage, so there will be some bodies on the way out of the inn.

Sometimes, he can be killed in full view of guards and citizens. The guards will do their normal "What was that?" routine, but will not see him actually being slaughtered, even though they see you plainly. Citizens, however, will scold you and sometimes turn hostile when they see Gaius Maro killed.

### A Direct Provocation

Another alternative method is for you to approach Maro and use the option of telling him how he will be killed, and then the Emperor. After this, Gaius will begin to attack. Letting him strike the first blow, then fighting back and killing him will not cause a bounty. This method can be used in any major city in order to receive the bonus. If using this method, it is best to confront him in view of a guard – so that it is seen that Gaius attacks first, and the guards come to your defense. However, if a guard wanders into view of the fight as it is proceeding and the first blow he sees is struck by you, a bounty will be earned.

If you are a member of the Thieves Guild and happen to encounter Maro in Riften, he can be provoked, and fellow [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") members (and even [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar")) will come to your defense. They will finish him off. This can also be done in Whiterun, where the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") are available, or similarly, in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), where the mages will ally themselves with you, should you be part of their guild. More generally, if Maro is attacked in a town or city where friends are present, they will help to kill him. If he happens to enter your house or homestead, the [Housecarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") can also be immensely valuable, since they will fight him off too.

Alternatively, if he is killed anywhere in a city where you are Thane, your position as Thane can be used to remove the bounty.

### Dragon Attacks

The bonus can also be received just outside a city. If a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attacks just outside a city, he can be killed while the guards are fighting the dragon, resulting in no bounty. The bonus will still be counted.

### Dragonsreach

An easy way to kill Gaius without good combat skills is when he is in Dragonsreach, in Whiterun. He can be approached and provoked. Once he attacks, the entire court of Whiterun will assault him. However, they will not kill him, but rather, will lower his health down to the point that he falls to one knee. This allows you to slaughter him with an extra attack or two.

### Pickpocket

With a high enough [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill, it is possible to plant the Incriminating Letter on Gaius before killing him. This allows him to be killed at range and in the open, and the quest completed without approaching his body. With the pickpocket perk [Poisoned](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisoned "Skyrim:Poisoned"), poison can also be placed in his pocket along with the note. The stronger the poison the better.

### Beast Form or Vampirism

While in Whiterun, after planting the Incriminating Letter on Gaius, he can be murdered using [Beast Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form") or [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") form. Afterwards, escaping to The Companions' Underforge, it is possible to wait until returning to normal appearance.

### Immediate Hostility

Gaius can be attacked while outside a major city but not killed, by running away and losing him. Once he has entered a major hold, he will attack you on sight. Since he attacked first, he can be killed with impunity. The guards will either help you or ignore the scene.

### Markarth

At some point while in town on Fredas, Gaius will go to the guard tower in Markarth. Once he is back out of the tower, [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") (preferably all three words) will launch him off of the high point that the guard tower is on. The player can augment this with [Force Without Effort](/wiki/Skyrim:Force_Without_Effort "Skyrim:Force Without Effort") and/or [Dragonborn Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Force "Skyrim:Dragonborn Force") to enhance its effects. After following him down, Gaius will attack once he is back on his feet, causing the guards to see this as a crime and attack him until he yields. He can then be simply finished off, and the Incriminating Letter planted.

### Change of Schedule

Whenever Gaius sees you he begins taking an alternate route. This can make the quest quite hard as he will turn away from a city if he sees you anywhere near it. If this happens, waiting in a tavern in a city on his route will allow him to eventually resume his normal journey.

### Reward

For this assault on the emperor's security, you will be rewarded with leveled gold. Gaius himself carries a set of rare [Penitus Oculatus armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Armor "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Armor"). If Gaius died in a city, you will also receive [Olava's Token](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava%27s_Token "Skyrim:Olava's Token"). The token will give you a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Locate_the_Assassin_of_Old "Skyrim:Locate the Assassin of Old") to find an "assassin of old", which will lead you to a dead Dark Brotherhood member in a cave equipped with the [Ancient Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Shrouded Armor") set. This set is the best Dark Brotherhood armor that you can acquire. It has a higher armor rating, higher gold value, lower weight, as well as having a superior enchantment to the base Shrouded set.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- Since Dragon Bridge is part of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), the guards there will try to arrest you if you earned a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Bounties "Skyrim:Crime") in Solitude during the previous quest, which will interfere with this quest. If this is the case, make sure to clear your bounty first.

## Bugs

- [Olava's Token](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava%27s_Token "Skyrim:Olava's Token") is required to receive a fortune reading from her. However, it is not a true quest item and may get discarded or sold by accident.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- If you choose to follow [Gaius](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") he might get lost on his way to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), and simply walk or stand around by the water near Solitude (possibly anywhere in Skyrim), or even swim in it. Fast traveling or waiting should make him remember what he is doing, and he might suddenly travel at a higher speed than you until he has caught up with his schedule.
- Sometimes when at the Bannered Mare in Whiterun, Gaius will never enter his room at all, instead periodically getting up and changing chairs before he leaves in the morning.
- After killing Gaius Maro, you can report back to Gabriella and she'll just repeat the line *"Gaius Maro still lives. I am surprised. I had assumed you were more... competent."*
- Similarly, after killing Gaius and planting the letter, you can report back to Gabriella and she'll just repeat the line *"Why are you here? Killing Gaius Maro is but the first step of your contract - you must also plant the incriminating letter on his body..."*
- If you are apprehended in Dragon Bridge by a guard, and you have a bounty, Gaius may not leave the town.
- Gaius and his father may be hostile to you and other citizens without reason. Being essential until they finish their initial conversation, this may cause the deaths of many residents of Dragon Bridge.
- Sometimes you don't receive the Incriminating Letter from Gabriella. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Breaching Security (DB06) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | Astrid informed me that I should speak to Gabriella about my next contract, which has something to do with the Emperor's security. *Objective 5:* Speak with Gabriella |
| 10 |  | I must kill Gaius Maro, an agent of the Emperor's security force. Once he's dead, I must plant a letter on his body that will incriminate him in a plot to kill the Emperor. If I wish to earn a bonus, I must not kill him in Dragon Bridge, or on the road, but in one of the cities he visits. *Objective 10:* Kill Gaius Maro  *Objective 8:* (Optional) Steal Gaius Maro's travel schedule |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Plant the Incriminating Letter on Gaius Maro's body |
| 200 | ☑ | I have killed Gaius Maro, and planted the Incriminating Letter on his body. This will surely disrupt the security plan for the Emperor's visit, ruin Commander Maro emotionally, and make the Emperor believe the only plot to kill him has been foiled. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 30:* Report back to Gabriella |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 30, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB06`.

# Skyrim:Breezehome

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| # of Zones | 1 |

Breezehome

**Breezehome** is a house that can be purchased in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

Entryway and kitchen

Breezehome is the first home offered to you during the main quest. Breezehome is the cheapest [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), but it is also the only house in Skyrim that does not have an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters").

The house is conveniently located just inside the entrance to Whiterun, next to [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's"). This is useful for a character who frequently uses [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"), as a full set of the stations are right next door.

To purchase the home, you must first complete the [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") quest for the Jarl of Whiterun. Upon completion he will permit you to purchase the house from [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") for 5,000 gold. The total cost of the house (including all upgrades) is 6,800 gold, or 6,550 gold if you have [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed and choose to forgo the [alchemy laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") in favor of a children's bedroom.

If you are having trouble finding Proventus you can get a quest marker on him through a miscellaneous task given by his daughter [Adrianne Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adrianne_Avenicci "Skyrim:Adrianne Avenicci"), who can usually be found outside of Warmaiden's, just inside the gates to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

If you have completed [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), [Lydia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lydia "Skyrim:Lydia") will be appointed as your housecarl and a small bedroom will be added upstairs for her. Her bedroom includes a dresser, an end table, a sack, and an owned bed.

Once purchased, Proventus will provide a book, *[Whiterun Home Decorating Guide](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Home_Decorating_Guide "Skyrim:Whiterun Home Decorating Guide")*, which details the various house upgrades available from him. Proventus will only sell upgrades while actually inside [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"). If he is on the [Great Porch](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach#Great_Porch "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") or his bedroom, the option to decorate your house will not be available.

If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") take over [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), Proventus will move to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and no longer offer you any upgrades. Instead, [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill") will be able to sell you upgrades in Dragonsreach after that.

It consists of only one zone, which is the interior.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Lydia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lydia "Skyrim:Lydia") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") |

## House Items

Master bedroom from doorway

When first purchased, prior to any upgrades being bought, it is dirty, covered with dust and cobwebs. It has a double bed and an empty chest upstairs. Downstairs there is a long wooden table and bench. The only other items are crates, a couple of unusable chairs and an unlit fire pit. If you have already been made a [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Whiterun "Skyrim:Thane of Whiterun"), Lydia's room will already be fully furnished, cleaned and walled off from the rest of the loft. There are no other internal walls.
There are items that are in the house when you purchase upgrades (see below).

- The [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") contains some rare [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").
- Two [iron greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") and one [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") are placed on a shield plaque above the bed after you purchase the bedroom upgrade. The other plaque and racks are empty upon purchase.
