‡ These can be bought to replace each other at will, the option to replace with each other remains permanently available.
% The contents of the chest on the bookcase in the Alchemy Lab is retained in the chest on the wall shelf in Children's Bedroom and vice versa.
\* This is removed from the house if you install the Children's Bedroom and returned empty if you revert the room to an Alchemy Lab.

## Notes

Alchemy lab

Child's bedroom

- This is the only purchasable home in the base game that you do not have to purchase in order to become thane. If you complete the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") while [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") is [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"), you will become thane, with or without Breezehome.
- You may want to remove [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") from the bookcase in the Alchemy Lab before converting it to a Child's Bedroom with the Hearthfire add-on. Books will remain in the room and the ones from the bottom shelf will be under the bed, rendered inaccessible.
- The apothecary's satchel is safe. if you replace the Alchemy Lab with the Children's Bedroom, it will still hold the same items when reverted back to an Alchemy Lab.
- The contents of the chest on the floor in the Children's Bedroom are emptied onto the top chest and remain there, should you change back to a Child's bedroom.[*verification needed*]
- Other than exceptions outlined above, all other containers are safe and [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning").
- Adopted children living here will have unique dialogue comments about Whiterun:
  - *I like it here. The tree in the park is so pretty!* (girls)
  - *[Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith") is a big meanie. She keeps telling [Lars](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born")' n me what to do. I don't wanna play with her anymore.* (girls)
  - *I played with [Lucia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucia "Skyrim:Lucia") in the park today. I feel sorry for her.* (girls)
  - *Dragonsreach is so cool! All the kids there are mean, though.* (boys)
  - *Lars is such a milk-drinker. He can't even stand up to a girl.* (boys)
- If you ask your spouse "How are the kids?" they will reply with one of the following, depending on their [voicetype](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Adoption_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue"):
  - *As well as can be expected. Dear, this house would work for the two of us, but with children? We need to find a bigger place.* (Arrogant)
  - *Just fine. Whiterun is a lovely city, and there are so many other children here- they all love playing together.* (Neutral)
  - *Couldn't be better. Whiterun is perfect for a child- great weather, plenty of space, friends to play with. What more could you want?* (Nord)
  - *Fine, fine. Plenty of kids here to play and spar with. Plenty of trades to learn. It's a good place to raise a child.* (Orc)
- During [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun"), the house will be key-locked once again, and the Breezehome key won't work. You'll regain access once the battle is finished.
- Initially, you would've encountered a squatter, [Terek](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Terek "Skyrim:Unused NPCs"), in Breezehome, but he did not make it into the final game.

## Bugs

- There are a few bugs which affect all houses, see the [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses#Bugs "Skyrim:Houses") section of the Houses page for details and fixes.
- If you remove a book from the bookcase on the main floor (beside the firepit) that is already placed on this bookcase, the bookcase may freeze, leaving you without access to any books within the case.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.3.7, fixes this bug.
- Although, theoretically, Lydia is supposed to sleep in the housecarl's bedroom, she never seems to, and instead has the unfortunate habit of intruding upon your bedroom and using the chair inside.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- After installing [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), you may encounter a bug when purchasing decor for Breezehome. After initially purchasing the alchemy lab, it will not disappear from the list of available decor; it will remain constantly available for purchase and will not appear in Breezehome.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  -  You can also use the following console commands to fix the issue. Note that these commands do not require you to actually buy the alchemy lab upgrade.

    ```
    prid e4ef9
    disable
    prid e4ec8
    enable
    ```
- The weapon plaque in the loft and the weapon rack near the front door may be inaccessible.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0, fixes this bug.
- The apothecary's satchel in the alchemy room may respawn despite the house being a no-reset zone.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Upon completing the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun"), Breezehome will be unlocked even if you have not purchased the house. However, the steward still requires you to purchase the house for 5000 gold.
- The option to replace the alchemy laboratory with a child's bedroom may not disappear after being purchased, and the change will not take place.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- The option to purchase a child's bedroom as well as the bedroom may not be available while Avenicci is on the balcony.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.1.1, fixes this bug.
  - You can buy it from him when he enters [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleCommoner](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionHaafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar "Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar"); [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction") | | |

Brelas at the embassy

**Brelas** is a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [pawnbroker](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawnbroker "Skyrim:Pawnbroker") met during [Elenwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Elenwen "Skyrim:Elenwen")'s party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"). If you use [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") as a distraction option, he will attempt to seduce Brelas. Upon her rejection of his advances, he becomes angry and has her sent to the dungeons where [Etienne Rarnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Etienne_Rarnis "Skyrim:Etienne Rarnis") is also being held. You will have the option to free her.

Whether or not you freed her from the Thalmor Embassy Dungeon, she will join [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn") in Windhelm (see [Bugs](#Bugs)) during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin") and also accompany him to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind").

If Brelas was not involved in the distraction, she will not be sent to the dungeons, and will thus remain in the entrance hall of the Thalmor Embassy, where the party took place.

## Related Quests

- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin")**: The [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") are after [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn"). Help him get to safety.

### Diplomatic Immunity

During the party Erikur can be seen flirting with Brelas:

:   **Erikur**: *"There's a likely-looking filly. Even if she is an elf. You there! Serving girl! What's your name, dear?"*
:   **Brelas**: *"Uh, Brelas, sir. Did you need a drink? Something to eat?"*
:   **Erikur**: *"No, no, that's not what I'm interested in right now. I just wanted to get a better look at you. I like what I see, my dear. And believe me, I don't say that to everyone. I'm very discriminating when it comes to the female form."*
:   **Brelas**: *"Um, thank you. Sir. Was there anything else I can do for you?"*
:   **Erikur**: *"Oh... not at the moment. Maybe later. Don't go far."*
:   **Brelas**: *"Yes, sir."*

If Erikur is spoken to he can ask you to talk to Brelas for him:

:   **That fellow over there asked me to talk to you...**
:   *"Ugh. Erikur, right? He was talking to me earlier. I could tell what he was after. I hate working these parties. Some of the guests are nice, but there's always a few like Erikur. Please tell him to leave me alone. Politely. I'm sure you'll have better luck getting through to him than I would."*

She can also give you a drink:

:   *"I hope you're enjoying yourself, sir./ma'am"*
:   **I'd like a drink.**
:   *"Here you go, sir. Colovian brandy."*

After talking to Erikur he will walk up to Brelas and proposition her again. Their conversation will depend on what you told him earlier:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Lie** | **Truth** |
| **Erikur**: *"Hello, my dear. I got your message. Where shall we go?"*  **Brelas**: *"What? I'm sorry, sir, but you must have misunderstood. I'm not permitted to leave the party."*  **Erikur**: *"Oh, I don't think so. I think I understand perfectly. Don't worry, my dear, I will make any necessary excuses to your employer."* | **Erikur**: *"So you think you can toy with me, is that it? No, my dear. I have my heart set on you, and I always get what I want."*  **Brelas**: *"I'm sorry, sir. I didn't mean to give you the wrong impression earlier. I meant no disrespect."*  **Erikur**: *"Don't worry, I'll let you make it up to me. Now, where can we go for a little privacy, hmm?"* |

Either way, it will end disastrously, creating a distraction in the party:

:   **Brelas**: *"No, I'm sorry, but I can't go anywhere with you. I won't. Please, I must get back to my duties."*
:   **Erikur**: *"Don't you dare walk away from me, you slut! Do you know who I am?"*
:   **Brelas**: *"Please, sir, leave me alone!"*
:   **Erikur**: *"Now you're going to be sorry you crossed me. [Elenwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Elenwen "Skyrim:Elenwen")! This servant girl has been throwing herself at me in a most disgusting manner."*
:   **Elenwen**: *"Is that so, Erikur? And you with such delicate sensibilities. It must have been most upsetting."*
:   **Erikur**: *"I demand that you have this wench removed from my presence at once!"*
:   **Elenwen**: *"Well. Whatever the truth of it, I'm sure a few words with Master [Rulindil](/wiki/Skyrim:Rulindil "Skyrim:Rulindil") will have a salutary effect. Take her downstairs."*
:   **Brelas**: *"No!"*
:   **Guard**: *"Yes, Madame Ambassador."*
:   **Brelas**: *"Mistress Elenwen, it's not true! I did nothing! Sir, you must tell her! You don't know what they'll do to me! Please!"*
:   **Erikur**: *"Well, I'm glad that little unpleasantness is over."*

When spoken to in the jailcell:

:   *"You've got to help me! Please!"*

:   **Come on, you'd better get out of here. (Free her)**

    :   *"Oh... thank you. I don't understand what's happening. I can't stay here. What will I do now?"*

:   **I can't help you right now.**

    :   *"What? Why? But... you must have said something to Erikur! You lied to him and now here I am! You're a heartless monster!"* **(If you lied to Erikur)**

:   :   *"No... please, you have to help me! You don't understand what they do to people here!"*

## Notes

- During [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin"), she will not gain any new dialogue, nor will Malborn's dialogue change to reflect the fact she is there with him.

## Bugs

- If you freed Brelas from the Thalmor Embassy Dungeon during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), after arriving in Windhelm she runs over to the left of [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") and vanishes, rather than going to [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.

Brelyna Maryon

Brelyna without her hood

**Brelyna Maryon** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [mystic](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystic "Skyrim:Mystic") and a student at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). She is most likely to be met during [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir")'s [lecture](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons"). Afterwards, she is found in the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"), sleeping from 10pm to 6am and studying there for the rest of the day.

Unlike her fellow students, [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") and [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo"), Brelyna tends to cast summoning spells and wards in combat. Because of this, she may be very useful if you seek a follower who will provide defenses and distractions. She is most skilled in [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion"), [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), and [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") in that order. She does not know any Illusion spells, however, and often uses [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells as well as bows, despite having minimal [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") and Destruction skills.

Her default clothing is an [apprentice hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Apprentice_Hood "Skyrim:Apprentice Hood"), [apprentice robes of destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Apprentice_Robes_of_Destruction "Skyrim:Apprentice Robes of Destruction"), and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing"). She also carries a [staff of lightning bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") and a copy of the book *[Gods and Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Gods_and_Worship "Skyrim:Gods and Worship")*.

After joining the College and completing Under Saarthal, Brelyna will [request](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna%27s_Practice "Skyrim:Brelyna's Practice") to test spells on you. If you agree and complete this minor quest, she will be available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") and you can [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") her. She is also a potential [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") [candidate](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades"). If you steal from the College while she is a follower, she will tolerate it at first, but eventually attack you if you do so too many times.

## Spells

Brelyna Maryon knows the following spells:

| [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") | [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") | [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") | [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh") | [Conjure Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar") | [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames") | [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") |
| [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh") | [Conjure Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach") | [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt") | [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing") |
| [Ironflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironflesh "Skyrim:Ironflesh") | [Conjure Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Frost Atronach") | [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball") | [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward") |

## Related Quests

- **[First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons")**: Join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)").
- **[Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal")**: Uncover the mysteries beneath this ancient ruin.
- **[Brelyna's Practice](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna%27s_Practice "Skyrim:Brelyna's Practice")**: Help Brelyna Maryon by allowing her to practice her spells on you.
- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Dialogue

Attempting conversation with Brelyna during the lecture will fail, as she will tell you:

:   *"I'm trying to pay attention."*

When the class is over, you may now properly talk to her, though she will already explain everything to you:

:   *"Before you even ask, yes I have an ancestry steeped in magic, and no I don't want to talk about it. Yes, I know [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") used to be full of my kind, and no I don't care that they're all gone now. Does that cover everything?"*

    :   **We haven't really been introduced.**
    :   *"No, I suppose we haven't. Brelyna Maryon, of [House Telvanni](/wiki/Lore:House_Telvanni "Lore:House Telvanni"). First of my family to leave [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") in a long time. Now I'm here to study [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"). That's what's important."*

:   :   **I'm sorry, what?**
    :   *"I've just been asked enough questions. I'm here to learn, not to explain myself over and over."* and promptly apologize, *"Forgive me, I didn't mean to assume."*

Brelyna may greet you with:

:   *"You know, this is one of a very few places where you can receive a real education in the schools of magic."*
:   *"I think my parents reserved a spot for me here at the College on the day I was born."*
:   *"There's a lot of pressure for me to excel in my studies. I hope I can live up to expectations."*

After the [excavation](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") at [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal"), Brelyna may comment on the [dangers](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") of exploring Nordic ruins:

:   *"At least something good came out of that trip to Saarthal. I didn't find anything but dust."*

If you are Arch-Mage, Brelyna will surprisingly offer you a backhanded compliment:

:   *"I still can't believe it. You, the Arch-Mage? Never would have guessed it."*

As Brelyna is from House Telvanni, known for its skill and dedication in magic, the pressure to succeed from her family results in her lack of confidence in her skills. You may ask her if she likes it here at the College, in which case she will agree:

:   **Do you like it here at the College?**
:   *"So far, if only because no one is telling me how great I ought to be. I just want to learn, I don't want to think about what's expected of me."*

If asked, Brelyna will explain that Winterhold used to be full of Dark Elves, along with the reason they left:

:   **Winterhold used to be full of dark elves?**
:   *"Didn't you know? Before the Oblivion Crisis, many elves called Winterhold their home. More visited the College from Morrowind every year. After, growing distrust of magic made life difficult for many. Some left rather than endure the growing hatred from the local Nords. Others returned home after the [Red Year](/wiki/Lore:Red_Year "Lore:Red Year"), when [Vvardenfell](/wiki/Lore:Vvardenfell "Lore:Vvardenfell") erupted and caused much destruction. Winterhold itself died in the years between then and now. What's left out there is a husk. Only the College really remains."*

## Quest-Related Events

Should you ask her, Brelyna will tell you what she knows about [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano"), [Arch-Mage Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren")'s advisor:

:   *"I know I don't like the way he looks at me. I can't tell if he expects me to blow myself up, or to try and murder him. But he clearly doesn't trust any of us."*

After you [meet](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") with [Quaranir](/wiki/Skyrim:Quaranir "Skyrim:Quaranir"), a [Psijic](/wiki/Skyrim:Psijic_Order "Skyrim:Psijic Order") monk, Brelyna will remark on it:

:   *"Is it true? One of the Psijics was here in the College?"*

You may inquire about the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain"), which will be replied with:

:   *"Huh? That sounds ominous. Are you getting yourself into even more trouble? Did you ask [Mirabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine")? She runs things around here, after all."*

During [Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen"), you will discover the [location](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") of the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus"), but Brelyna will show skepticism:

:   *"So you're off to find some staff now? I don't see the point of that."*

As Ancano releases the power of the Eye of Magnus, she will exclaim:

:   *"By [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura"), what's happening?"*

You will then be tasked to [retrieve the Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus"), and Brelyna will still not be convinced of the Staff's importance, saying either :

:   *"You really think the Staff of Magnus is the key?"*
:   *"How long can we keep this up?"*

When you set out to [defeat](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") Ancano, Brelyna will understandably be shocked over current events:

:   *"I can't believe any of this is happening!"*

### First Lessons

*"We wouldn't be here if we couldn't control magic!"*

Upon first entering the Hall of the Elements, you will see Brelyna, [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo"), and [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") arguing with Tolfdir over safety:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Tolfdir**: | (to you) *"Welcome, welcome! We were just beginning. Please, stay and listen."* |
| **Tolfdir**: | *"So, as I was saying, the first thing to understand is that magic is, by its very nature, volatile and dangerous. Unless you can control it, it can and will destroy you."* |
| **Brelyna**: | *"Sir, I think we all understand that fairly well. We wouldn't be here if we couldn't control magic!"* |
| **Tolfdir**: | *"Of course, my dear. Of course. You all certainly possess some inherent natural ability. That much is not being questioned. What I'm talking about is true control, mastery of magic. It takes years, if not decades, of practice and study."* |
| **J'zargo**: | *"Then what are we waiting for? Let's get started!"* |
| **Tolfdir**: | *"Please, please! This is exactly what I'm talking about. Eagerness must be tempered with caution, or else disaster is inevitable."* |
| **Onmund**: | *"But we've only just arrived here -- you've no idea what any of us are capable of. Why not give us a chance to show you what we can do?"* |

Tolfdir will then approach you and ask:

:   *"You've been quiet so far. What do you think we should do?"*

    :   **I think we should learn something practical.**
    :   *"Is that so?"*

Brelyna will add:

:   *"See? He/she agrees with us too! Why don't you actually show us something?"*

No matter your option, Tolfdir will eventually give in and ask you to cast a ward while he casts a spell against it. Brelyna and the other students will stand behind Tolfdir to watch the demonstration.

### Under Saarthal

*"This is better than sitting around talking about magic, don't you think?"*

During Under Saarthal, Brelyna will be found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal"), enthusiastic about the excavation. She may converse with the other students about this:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **J'zargo**: | *"What do you think we'll find in there?"* | **Brelyna**: | *"Can you believe we're here? Saarthal, of all places."* |
| **Brelyna**: | *"It's thousands of years old. Who knows what we might find?"* | **Onmund**: | *"I'm surprised that the College is allowed to excavate here."* |
| **J'zargo**: | *"I'm betting bodies. Lots and lots of bodies. And maybe some valuables..."* | **Brelyna**: | *"I bet your family would be amazed, right?"* |
| **Brelyna**: | *"Don't get any ideas. We're here on official business, remember?"* | **Onmund**: | *"Amazed isn't the right word. They might find this... offensive."* |

When approached, Brelyna may say either:

:   *"This is exciting, isn't it?"*
:   *"This is better than sitting around talking about magic, don't you think?"*
:   *"To think, my ancestors destroyed the homes of Onmund's ancestors. So much bloodshed."*

:   **Are you nervous about being here?**
:   *"Why? Because it's old, and full of dead things? Clearly you've never spent any time in Morrowind."*

:   **Do you know anything about Saarthal?**
:   *"Not really. Just that it's very, very old. It was one of the first cities of men in [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"), I think."*

As the students delve deeper into the ruin, Tolfdir will assign Brelyna something:

:   *"Brelyna, my dear, why don't you search for warding magics. Anything designed to keep people out. Don't interact with them, just identify them."*

After this, she can be found saying:

:   *"I'm not seeing signs of any warding magics at all. Either they're not here, or they were removed long ago."*

Through her conversations, Brelyna will express her disappointment:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Brelyna**: *"I'm not sure what I was expecting, but this isn't it."* | **Brelyna**: | *"This is a little creepy."* |
| **J'zargo**: *"There's no gold, nothing shiny at all."* | **Onmund**: | *"That doesn't begin to describe it."* |
| **Brelyna**: *"Don't sound so disappointed. You wouldn't be allowed to take it even if there was."* | **Brelyna**: | *"You seem uncomfortable being here."* |
| **J'zargo**: *"Like anyone would even notice, in all this mess."* | **Onmund**: | *"I just don't know that it's right for us to be in here like this, picking through the ruins .*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*"* |

### Brelyna's Practice

*"We're all trying to become better mages, right?"*

Back in the College, Brelyna has been working on a spell and needs someone to test it on: you. She will ask for your help:

:   *"If you have a moment, could you help me with something?"* or if you have refused to help before, she will tell you,
:   *"I still need some help, if you can spare the time."*

:   **What do you need help with?**
:   *"We're all trying to become better mages, right? Well, I need someone I can practice a few spells on. Nothing dangerous, really. Would you be willing to assist me?"*

:   :   **I don't think so.**
    :   *"Oh. Well, if you change your mind, let me know."*

:   :   **What's in it for me?**
    :   *"Well, I... I simply thought you might wish to help out one of your fellow mages. If that's not enough, I suppose... I have this amulet you could take."*

:   :   **Can't you practice on yourself?**

*"No, not that kind of spell. Believe me when I say I wouldn't be asking if it weren't necessary."*

:   :   **Okay, I'll help.**
    :   *"Oh, good. I was afraid I'd have to go ask J'zargo. Now, you just stand there..."*

As she prepares to cast the spell, she will tell you:

:   *"Please hold still, and don't move."*

She will cast a flawed spell that causes your vision to become greenish, and exclaim:

:   *"There! Now, I..."*

She will then realize what she has done:

:   *"Oh dear. That wasn't supposed to happen."*

She will ask you worriedly,

:   *"Do you... do you feel all right? You look very, umm, green."*

Brelyna will then apologize,

:   *"I am so very sorry. I went over this again and again, and I was sure it would have better results."*

:   :   **Tell me this isn't permanent.**
    :   *"It's not! It shouldn't be. You'll be back to normal in no time. And when you are, we can try this again and I'll be sure to get it right."*

:   :   **What did you do?**
    :   *"I'm not really sure. I think it's just a minor miscalculation on my part. I'm sure it will wear off soon. When it does, you'll be perfectly fine, and then we can try again. In the meantime, I'll see about figuring out what went wrong."*

After her spell wears off, you can report back.

:   **Your spell finally wore off.**
:   *"Exactly as I said it would. Now, are you ready to try again? I am confident it will work this time."*

:   :   **Okay, you can try again.**
    :   *"This will be worth it."*

:   :   **One more chance. That's it.**
    :   *"Good, good. It'll be worth it, I assure you."*

:   :   **I've had enough for now.**
    :   *"Well I really would like to make sure I've corrected what happened last time. Please give me a chance to try again."*

Brelyna will then order you:

:   *"Okay, now don't move at all."*

As she readies her spell. You will be turned into a cow, which will have her exclaim:

:   *"Oh my. That isn't right! Just wait. Just... I can fix this."*

She will cast another spell and instead transform you into a horse:

:   *"Oh no, that's not it at all. Let me try again..."*

The next time you will turn into a dog:

:   *"This really isn't turning out the way I'd hoped."*

Brelyna will obviously be embarrassed over this as she tries to assure you,:
*"I'll get it right this time, I swear."*

She will then return you to normal.

:   *"There, all better."*

When she finishes experimenting on you, Brelyna will say:

:   **So...**
:   *"Well, it all worked out in the end, didn't it?"*

:   :   **Let's never speak of this again.**
    :   *"Agreed. And thank you for your help. You're a good friend."*

:   :   **It's been a pleasure.**
    :   *"Oh, no it hasn't. Let's be honest. I have a long way to go before I'm ready for the kind of advanced magic I've been attempting. But at least I know where to start now. Thank you, you've been a great help to me."*

## Conversations

Brelyna was supposed to talk with Onmund about their families, but doesn't due to a [bug](#Bugs).

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Brelyna**: | *"Still no word from your family?"* | **Onmund**: | *"Have you heard from your family recently?"* |
| **Onmund**: | *"No, and I'm not expecting any."* | **Brelyna**: | *"No, not really. Couriers don't seem to like delivering letters here."* |
| **Brelyna**: | *"Really? That must be so nice. I came all the way to Skyrim just to get away from my family's expectations."* | **Onmund**: | *"Ah, that's too bad."* |
| **Onmund**: | *"My family didn't really approve of me coming here at all."* | **Brelyna**: | *"Not at all. It means I'm not being hounded about my progress at the College."* |
| **Brelyna**: | *"Oh. Well, that's... awkward. Sorry to have brought it up."* |

She was also supposed to be approached by [Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") for his [research](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor"), which never happens due to the same bug.

| --- | --- |

| **Brelyna**: | *"If this is another dwarven trinket, I keep telling you I'm not familiar with them."* |
| **Arniel**: | *"Yes, I just thought perhaps you'd have, err, come across something like this before."* |
| **Brelyna**: | *"Why, because I'm a Dunmer? We didn't all grow up in dwarven ruins, you know."* |
| **Arniel**: | *"Well, err, yes. Sorry to have troubled you."* |

## Follower Dialogue

Brelyna in combat

| When asked to trade items | *"I'm a mage, not a pawnbroker, you know."* | |

| When told to follow | *"Of course. Let's go."* | |
| When dismissed | *"You'll be all right on your own? Then I'll see you back at the College."* | |

## Notes

- If you decide to marry Brelyna, her dialogue is the same as if she were at the College of Winterhold no matter where she is, until you finish The Eye of Magnus. She will still open a store and will give you 100 gold per day.
  - If she moves to your house, dismissing her when she is a follower will have her reply with, *"You'll be all right on your own? Then I'll see you back at the College."* after The Eye of Magnus.

## Bugs

- Brelyna will never initiate conversation with other College members, as all the scenes were set in the Hall of Countenance, where none of them will ever meet.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- As a [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") she may say she is going back to the College whenever she leaves your service as a follower, but actually goes back to the property of which she is steward.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Dismissing Brelyna as a follower after she's been married or recruited as a Blade still plays dialogue saying she's returning to the College when this is not where she'll be going.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- If turned into a vampire with [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed, her eyes do not glow but are the vanilla vampire eyes.

# Skyrim:Brelyna's Practice

## Overview

Brelyna casting a spell

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon").
2. Let her cast a spell on you.
3. Wait a few in-game hours to let the effects wear off.
4. Let Brelyna try again.
5. Wait for her to finish.

### Helping Out A Friend

[Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon") is a serious student at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). After completing [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal"), you can find her back at the College (likely in the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment")). When you speak to her, she'll request your help: *"We're all trying to become better mages, right? Well, I need someone I can practice a few spells on. Nothing dangerous, really. Would you be willing to assist me?"* If you agree to help her for a price, she will offer an amulet in return. Apparently, she has developed a type of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") spell that she needs to cast onto someone else, and she will be relieved that she won't have to ask [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo") for help.

### It's Not Easy Being Green

When you are ready, Brelyna will instruct you: *"Please hold still, and don't move."* As the spell is cast, a tiny flaw becomes apparent: your vision is now green. Alarmingly, Brelyna will exclaim, *"Oh dear. That wasn't supposed to happen."* Then she will ask, *"Do you... do you feel all right? You look very, umm, green."*
She will apologize profusely, assuring you that the green effect is temporary. It will fade after a few in-game hours.

### Altered States

After the effects of the first attempt fade, and if you are being a good sport about it all, return to Brelyna and she will ask you to help her again. She confidently asserts that she has everything worked out. You can also express your doubts about proceeding, but in the end, agree to her ministrations. She will cast several more spells which will turn you into a horse, a cow, and a dog.

The results of the second spell

The results of the third spell

Brelyna casting her fourth spell

The results of the fourth spell

With each mishap, Brelyna bolsters her resolve: *"Oh my. That isn't right! Just wait. Just... I can fix this."*, *"Oh no, that's not it at all. Let me try again..."*, *"This really isn't turning out the way I'd hoped."*, and then, *"I'll get it right this time, I swear."* On her final attempt, you are returned to normal, and she says, *"There, all better."*

### Your Compensation

When all is set to right, Brelyna will reward you with a random, level-dependent [Resist Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic") necklace, and you both can agree to never speak of this again. Brelyna will also become a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage"), and can be asked to join you as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

| Necklace | Level | Enchantment |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Necklace of Resist Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace_of_Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Necklace of Resist Magic") | 8 | *Increases Magic Resistance by 10%.* |
| [Necklace of Waning Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace_of_Waning_Magic "Skyrim:Necklace of Waning Magic") | 16 | *Increases Magic Resistance by 12%.* |
| [Necklace of Dwindling Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace_of_Dwindling_Magic "Skyrim:Necklace of Dwindling Magic") | 24 | *Increases Magic Resistance by 15%.* |
| [Necklace of Magic Suppression](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace_of_Magic_Suppression "Skyrim:Necklace of Magic Suppression") | 32 | *Increases Magic Resistance by 17%.* |
| [Necklace of Magic Abatement](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace_of_Magic_Abatement "Skyrim:Necklace of Magic Abatement") | 40 | *Increases Magic Resistance by 20%.* |
| [Necklace of Nullification](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace_of_Nullification "Skyrim:Necklace of Nullification") | 48 | *Increases Magic Resistance by 22%.* |

The level provided in the table is the minimum level that you must be to obtain that version of the necklace; however, even at higher levels it is still possible to receive the lowest-level necklace. Below level 8, you will not receive any necklace.

## Bugs

- If you are currently under any spell absorption effect, Brelyna's spells may not always work on you. If this happens, you will need to reload to prevent from getting permanently stuck with "Wait for Brelyna's Spell to wear off" stuck in your quest log and the quest never advancing.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  -  Using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `setstage MGRAppBrelyna01 30` will manually advance the quest to the next stage.
  -  If you have the [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_(perk) "Skyrim:Atronach (perk)") perk, you can temporarily remove it using the console command `Player.removeperk 000581F7`. Once the spell effect wears off, you can add it again using `Player.addperk 000581F7`.
- The quest reward may randomize the level of its resist magic magnitude when it wasn't supposed to.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- If you are in third person view, or if the view between Brelyna and you is obstructed (thereby preventing you from being hit by the spell), then the quest will remain stuck on the "wait for Brelyna's spell to wear off" part of the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
  -  This issue can be fixed by entering `setstage MGRAppBrelyna01 30` into the game console. This will force the quest to move to the next stage, when the spell has worn off.
  -  If the above step doesn't remove the green tint, enter `Player.addspell 000EA5EA` into console, cast her practice spell on any NPC, wait a few in-game hours, then enter `Player.removespell 000EA5EA`. The quest will update itself.
- This quest is incorrectly marked as a Miscellaneous quest when it should be marked as a College quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- You may remain invisible after the last phase of the quest (needed for the simulation of being transformed into an animal).
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Use the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout to fix it.
  -  This can be fixed by entering `player.setactoralpha 100` into the console command.
- When you complete the quest, there will be a leftover active effect called Brelyna's Practice Spell with a description of +1 Brelyna's Practice Spell 1 hour. It does not appear to have any effect, and it should wear off.

## Quest Stages

| Brelyna's Practice (MGRAppBrelyna01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

Her first attempt ended badly, but she has assured me that if I let her try one more time, it will work out. I should find her once her spell has worn off. *Objective 20:* Wait for Brelyna's spell to wear off |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Speak to Brelyna |
| 200 | ☑ | After two attempts at helping Brelyna with trying out new spells, she has agreed that perhaps she should work a bit more before trying anything else. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRAppBrelyna01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRAppBrelyna01`.

Brenuin

**Brenuin** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggars "Skyrim:Beggars") and drunkard living in the city of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). He wants someone to steal a rare [Argonian ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale") from [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare"), the local inn. He offers a healing potion in return.

Brenuin can't afford a place to sleep so he wanders around town all night long, from 1am to 9am, begging for coins and food. When the sun rises he heads to the Gildergreen and spends five hours listening to [Heimskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr "Skyrim:Heimskr")'s ramblings. At 2pm he walks down to the market in the Plains District and spends his afternoon trying to get some free food from either [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda"), [Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Anoriath "Skyrim:Anoriath") or [Carlotta Valentia](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia"). At 7pm he enters the [Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") where he strolls around the taproom until he hits the streets again at 1am. The only exception to this routine occurs when [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") is attacked by the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") at the end of the quest [Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor"). Brenuin will then be in the crowd gathered outside Jorrvaskr.

He wears a set of [ragged robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Robes "Skyrim:Ragged Robes") with [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Boots "Skyrim:Ragged Boots") and a [cap](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Cap "Skyrim:Ragged Cap"). He only carries a small selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Argonian Ale Extraction](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale_Extraction "Skyrim:Argonian Ale Extraction")**: Brenuin longs for the taste of [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale"). Can you steal some for him?
- **[A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming"): Develop your farm.
- **[Quest all Beggars Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Beggars_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Beggars Have")**: Take pity on a beggar. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

When passing by he will usually remark:

:   *"I ain't done nothin'."*
:   *"What? Why you lookin' at me?"*
:   *"That Heimskr's crazy. Him and his talk o' Talos. Wish he'd just shut up."*

### Argonian Ale Extraction

To initiate his quest, [Argonian Ale Extraction](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale_Extraction "Skyrim:Argonian Ale Extraction"), you must ask him:

:   **Are you always drunk?**
:   *"Only if I can help it. But damn if I ain't almost sober. Hey. In the Bannered Mare, there's this bottle of Argonian Ale. The good stuff. Get it for me. They won't even know it's gone. Come on..."*

:   :   **I'll bring you that ale, old man.**
    :   *"Argonian Ale! I can almost taste it!"*

:   :   **I'm not going to feed your bad habit.**
    :   *"Then we got nothin' more to talk about."*

If asked again before you have the ale:

:   **Are you always drunk?**
:   *"Well that all depends on you, now. Doesn't it?"*

When you retrieve the ale:

:   **Here's that special ale you wanted.**
:   *"Well, would you look at that! Argonian Ale! My thanks, friend. Here, take this here healing potion. I, er, "found" it in the temple."*

Afterwards you may ask him:

:   **Still thirsty?**
:   *"Not anymore. Thanks to you. Friend."*

## Conversations

When he spends time at the market stalls in the afternoon, he will occasionally talk with the merchants:

:   **Brenuin**: *"Spare a coin for a fellow Nord who's down on his luck?"*
:   **Ysolda**: *"So you can spend it on drinks at the Bannered Mare? If it's food you need, ask for that instead."*
:   **Brenuin**: *"Never you mind, then. I'll find a more charitable soul."*
:   **Ysolda**: *"That's what I thought."*

:   **Anoriath**: *"I don't suppose you're going to buy something this time?"*
:   **Brenuin**: *"Just browsin' today. If the gods be kind, someone will take mercy on me and spare a few septims."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"If they do, promise you'll actually purchase something for once."*
:   **Brenuin**: *"By Ysmir, I will. Gods know it's been too long since I tasted real meat."*

:   **Carlotta**: *"How goes the begging today, Brenuin?"*
:   **Brenuin**: *"That's right, mock the town beggar like everyone else. But I've got a right to browse, don't I? I ain't hurtin' anyone."*
:   **Carlotta**: *"Make it quick, then. I don't want your stink driving my customers away."*
:   **Brenuin**: *"The gods smile on them who show charity. Best you remember that."*

:   **Carlotta**: *"And what might you be looking at?"*
:   **Brenuin**: *"Oh, the fruit looks so good. So juicy."*
:   **Carlotta**: *"No handouts today, Brenuin. Now scat. You'll scare off my paying customers."*
:   **Brenuin**: *"Oh, just one apple, Carlotta? Just one tiny apple. I'll pay you tomorrow, I swear it."*
:   **Carlotta**: *"That's what you said last week, and the week before that. Now go, before I call a guard."*
:   **Brenuin**: *"No, no! Don't do that. No need to do that. I'm going. See? I'm leaving. No guards, please."*
:   **Carlotta**: *"Look, come back tomorrow, okay? If I have anything left that's not sold or spoiled, you can have it."*
:   **Brenuin**: *"You've got the heart of Mara herself, you know that? Thank you, Carlotta. Thank you."*

## Rumors

Asking [Lucia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucia "Skyrim:Lucia") why she is begging will reveal that Brenuin has a soft side for the orphan, and has been giving her some advice since she came to the city:

:   *"It's... it's what Brenuin said I should do. He's the only one that's been nice to me since... since mama..."*

## Notes

- Brenuin is the only beggar that wears the matching ragged cap with his robes.
- His dialogue during scenes seems to be written with a Nord character in mind. Brenuin can heard referring to himself as "a fellow Nord" in one scene, and in another he uses the expression "By Ysmir", which is almost exclusively used by Nords, usually even being conditioned to not be said by members of any other race.
  - [Reburrus Quintilius](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius"), a man living in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), exhibits very similar issues.
- Brenuin can be hired as a [farmhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmhand "Skyrim:Farmhand") for [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming") for 250 gold.

## Bugs

- Brenuin's burial urn was supposed to get enabled in Whiterun's [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") in the case of his death. However, the enable parent is mistakenly linked to a nearby fire shader, resulting in the urn never getting being enabled.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Brenuin never sleeps due to lack of a sleep package.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=13030))
- While begging for money from [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda"), Brenuin refers to himself as a "fellow Nord", despite being a Redguard.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
